No. 1论文详情NBER w34786

Well-being Increases in Age Among Workers: Evidence From 103 Countries

工作者幸福感随年龄增长而提升：来自103个国家的证据

David G. Blanchflower, Alex Bryson

Abstract

We examine how workers’ and non-workers’ wellbeing varies by age across 171 countries in eight international surveys. In 103 countries (60%) we find evidence that workers’ wellbeing rises with age and workers' illbeing falls with age. This relationship appears to have strengthened over time in some countries. Patterns are different among non-workers and are sensitive to survey mode. Where surveys are conducted using Computer-Assisted Web-based Interviews (CAWI) non-workers’ wellbeing is U-shaped, but this is less clear-cut when the data are collected with Computer-Assisted Telephone Interviews (CATI). The change in the age profile of workers’ wellbeing may reflect changes in selection into (out of) employment by age, changes in job quality, or changes in young workers’ orientation to similar jobs over time. But changes in smartphone usage – often the focus of debate regarding declining young peoples’ wellbeing – are unlikely to be the main culprit unless there are sizeable differences in smartphone usage across young workers and non-workers, which appears unlikely.

中文摘要

我们利用八项国际调查，研究了171个国家中工作者和非工作者的幸福感如何随年龄变化。在103个国家（60%）中，我们发现证据表明工作者的幸福感随年龄增长而上升，工作者的不幸福感随年龄增长而下降。这种关系在一些国家似乎随时间推移而增强。非工作者的模式则不同，并且对调查模式敏感。在采用计算机辅助网络访谈（CAWI）进行的调查中，非工作者的幸福感呈U型，但当数据通过计算机辅助电话访谈（CATI）收集时，这种模式就不那么明确了。工作者幸福感年龄曲线的变化可能反映了不同年龄人群就业（或退出就业）选择的变化、工作质量的变化，或者年轻工作者对类似工作态度随时间的变化。但智能手机使用的变化——这通常是关于年轻人幸福感下降争论的焦点——不太可能是主要原因，除非年轻工作者和非工作者在智能手机使用上存在显著差异，而这似乎不太可能。

No. 2论文详情NBER w34785

Trade and US Inequality in the Tokyo Round

东京回合贸易谈判与美国不平等问题

Andrew Greenland, James Lake, John Lopresti

Abstract

Against a backdrop of sharply rising inequality, the Tokyo Round of the GATT resulted in a 1.6 percentage point reduction in average US tariffs – larger than CUSFTA, NAFTA, and the liberalization accompanying the granting of PNTR to China. We construct a novel IV based on the so-called “Swiss formula” that governed the Tokyo Round tariff liberalization to provide evidence of its effects on imports and inequality. Instrumented tariff reductions explain approximately 20% of the rise in income inequality between non-production and production workers between 1979 and 1988. This effect is largest among women, workers in routine occupations, and workers in more technology-intensive industries, suggesting a complementarity between trade liberalization and skill-biased technological change.

中文摘要

在不平等急剧上升的背景下，关贸总协定东京回合谈判导致美国平均关税降低了1.6个百分点——这一降幅大于美加自由贸易协定、北美自由贸易协定以及给予中国永久正常贸易关系地位所带来的自由化。我们基于指导东京回合关税自由化的所谓“瑞士公式”构建了一个新颖的工具变量，以提供其进口和不平等影响的证据。工具变量估计的关税削减解释了1979年至1988年间非生产工人与生产工人之间收入不平等上升的大约20%。这种效应在女性、从事常规职业的工人以及技术更密集型行业的工人中最为显著，表明贸易自由化与技能偏向型技术变革之间存在互补性。

No. 3论文详情NBER w34784

Changing Culture and Norms in Developing Countries

发展中国家的文化与社会规范变迁

Eliana La Ferrara, David H. Yanagizawa-Drott

Abstract

We survey recent research on changing culture and social norms in developing countries and propose a simple framework to interpret these changes. We conceptualize individual utility from a given action as a function of three components: intrinsic valuations, material payoffs, and social interactions. Using this lens, we review evidence on interventions that target each component and their interactions.

中文摘要

我们调查了近期关于发展中国家文化与社会规范变迁的研究，并提出了一个解释这些变迁的简单框架。我们将个体从特定行为中获得的效用概念化为三个组成部分的函数：内在价值、物质回报和社会互动。运用这一视角，我们回顾了针对每个组成部分及其相互作用进行干预的证据。

No. 4论文详情NBER w34783

Banking on Inattention

基于注意力不足的银行业务

Xu Lu, Lingxuan Wu

Abstract

We show that depositor inattention gives banks deposit market power, explaining incomplete monetary pass-through and generating interest rate exposure that changes sign over the monetary cycle. We present a dynamic deposit-pricing model in which banks trade off current deposit spreads against future deposit base, with inattention dampening spread-sensitive outflows. Empirically, we measure inattention using differential responses to scheduled versus unscheduled income and show that inattentive depositors withdraw less following rate hikes. The data confirm that banks with more inattentive depositors have lower deposit rates, weaker pass-through, and less spread-sensitive outflows. Our calibration quantifies how inattention shapes pass-through and financial stability.

中文摘要

我们表明，存款人的注意力不足赋予了银行存款市场势力，这解释了不完全的货币传导，并产生了在整个货币周期中符号发生变化的利率风险敞口。我们提出了一个动态存款定价模型，在该模型中，银行在当前的存款利差与未来的存款基础之间进行权衡，而注意力不足则抑制了对利差敏感的存款外流。在实证方面，我们利用对计划内与计划外收入的不同反应来衡量注意力不足，并表明注意力不足的存款人在加息后提取的资金更少。数据证实，拥有更多注意力不足存款人的银行，其存款利率更低，传导效应更弱，且对利差敏感的存款外流也更少。我们的校准量化了注意力不足如何塑造传导效应和金融稳定性。

No. 5论文详情NBER w34782

Managers and the Cultural Transmission of Gender Norms

管理者与性别规范的文化传播

Virginia Minni, Kieu-Trang Nguyen, Heather Sarsons, Carla Srebot

Abstract

This paper studies how managers’ gender attitudes shape workplace culture and gender inequality. Using data from a multinational firm operating in over 100 countries, we leverage cross-country manager rotations to identify the effects of male managers' gender attitudes on gender pay gaps within a team. Managers from countries with one standard deviation more progressive gender attitudes reduce the pay gap by 5 percentage points (18%), largely through higher promotion rates for women. These effects persist after managers rotate out and are strongest in more conservative countries. Managers with progressive attitudes also influence the local office culture, as local managers who interact with but are not under the purview of the foreign manager begin to have smaller pay gaps in their teams. Our evidence points to individual managers as critical in shaping corporate culture.

中文摘要

本文研究管理者的性别态度如何塑造工作场所文化和性别不平等。利用一家在100多个国家运营的跨国公司的数据，我们利用跨国的管理者轮换来识别男性管理者的性别态度对团队内部性别薪酬差距的影响。来自性别态度更进步一个标准差国家的管理者，将薪酬差距缩小了5个百分点（18%），这主要通过提高女性的晋升率实现。这些效应在管理者轮换后仍然持续，并且在更保守的国家最为显著。具有进步态度的管理者也影响着当地办公室的文化，因为与外国管理者互动但不受其管辖的本地管理者，其团队中的薪酬差距也开始缩小。我们的证据表明，个体管理者在塑造企业文化方面至关重要。

No. 6论文详情NBER w34781

Enhancing Worker Productivity Without Automating Tasks: A Different Approach to AI and the Task-Based Model

在不自动化任务的前提下提升工人生产力：一种不同的AI方法与基于任务的模型

Ajay K. Agrawal, John McHale, Alexander Oettl

Abstract

The task-based approach has become the dominant framework for studying the labor-market effects of artificial intelligence (AI), typically emphasizing the replacement of human workers by machines. Motivated by growing empirical evidence that contemporary AI is more often used as a tool that augments workers, this paper develops two related task-based models in which AI enhances worker productivity without automating tasks. Abstracting from capital, we develop a pair of related task-based models that examine how technological progress in AI that provides new tools to augment workers affects aggregate productivity and wage inequality. Both models emphasize the role of human capital in intermediating the effects of AI-related technological shocks. In the first model, AI use requires specialized expertise, and technological progress expands the set of tasks for which such expertise is effective. We show that a larger supply of AI expertise amplifies the productivity gains from improvements in AI technology while attenuating its adverse effects on wage inequality. The second model focuses on non-AI skills, allowing AI tools to alter the set of tasks that workers can perform given their skills. In equilibrium, workers allocate across tasks in response to wages, generating an endogenous distribution of skills across the task space. A central result is that aggregate productivity and wage inequality depend on different global properties of this equilibrium distribution: productivity is particularly sensitive to thinly staffed tasks that create bottlenecks, while wage inequality is driven by the concentration of workers in a narrow set of tasks. As a result, improvements in AI tools can induce non-monotonic co-movement between productivity and inequality. By linking these mechanisms to multidimensional human capital---including AI expertise and higher-order non-AI skills---the paper highlights the role of education and training policies in shaping the economic consequences of AI-driven technological change.

中文摘要

基于任务的方法已成为研究人工智能（AI）对劳动力市场影响的主导框架，通常强调机器对人类工人的替代。受越来越多的实证证据表明当代AI更常被用作增强工人的工具的启发，本文开发了两个相关的基于任务的模型，在这些模型中，AI在不自动化任务的前提下提升了工人的生产力。撇开资本不谈，我们开发了一对相关的基于任务的模型，研究提供新工具以增强工人的AI技术进步如何影响总生产率和工资不平等。两个模型都强调了人力资本在调节AI相关技术冲击影响中的作用。在第一个模型中，AI的使用需要专业知识，技术进步扩展了这种专业知识有效的任务集。我们表明，更大的AI专业知识供给放大了AI技术改进带来的生产率提升，同时减轻了其对工资不平等的不利影响。第二个模型侧重于非AI技能，允许AI工具根据工人的技能改变他们能够执行的任务集。在均衡状态下，工人根据工资在任务间进行分配，从而在任务空间中产生内生的技能分布。一个核心结果是，总生产率和工资不平等取决于该均衡分布的不同全局属性：生产率对造成瓶颈的人员配备稀少的任务特别敏感，而工资不平等则由工人集中在狭窄的任务集所驱动。因此，AI工具的改进可以引发生产率和不平等之间的非单调联动。通过将这些机制与多维人力资本（包括AI专业知识和高阶非AI技能）联系起来，本文强调了教育和培训政策在塑造AI驱动技术变革的经济后果中的作用。

No. 7论文详情NBER w34780

Optimal Use of Preferences in Artificial Intelligence Algorithms

人工智能算法中偏好的最优使用

Joshua S. Gans

Abstract

Machine learning systems embed preferences either in training losses or through post-processing of calibrated predictions. Applying information design methods from Strack and Yang (2024), this paper provides decision-problem-agnostic conditions under which separation—training preference-free and applying preferences ex post is optimal. Unlike prior work that requires specifying downstream objectives, the welfare results here apply uniformly across decision problems. The key primitive is a diminishing-value-of-information condition: relative to a fixed (normalised) preference-free loss, preference embedding makes informativeness less valuable at the margin, inducing a mean-preserving contraction of learned posteriors. Because the value of information is convex in beliefs, preference-free training weakly dominates for any expected-utility decision problem. This provides theoretical foundations for modular AI pipelines that learn calibrated probabilities and implement asymmetric costs through downstream decision rules. However, separation requires users to implement optimal decision rules. When cognitive constraints bind—as documented in human-AI decision-making—preference embedding can dominate by automating threshold computation. These results provide design guidance: preserve optionality through postprocessing when objectives may shift; embed preferences when decision-stage frictions dominate.

中文摘要

机器学习系统要么在训练损失中嵌入偏好，要么通过对校准预测进行后处理来嵌入偏好。应用Strack和Yang（2024）的信息设计方法，本文提供了与决策问题无关的条件，在这些条件下，分离——即训练无偏好模型并在事后应用偏好——是最优的。与需要指定下游目标的先前工作不同，这里的福利结果统一适用于各种决策问题。关键前提是信息价值递减条件：相对于固定的（标准化）无偏好损失，偏好嵌入使得信息在边际上的价值降低，导致学习到的后验分布发生均值保持收缩。由于信息价值在信念上是凸函数，对于任何期望效用决策问题，无偏好训练都弱占优。这为模块化AI流水线提供了理论基础，该流水线学习校准概率并通过下游决策规则实现非对称成本。然而，分离要求用户实施最优决策规则。当认知约束起作用时——正如在人机决策中记录的那样——偏好嵌入可以通过自动化阈值计算而占优。这些结果提供了设计指导：当目标可能发生变化时，通过后处理保留可选择性；当决策阶段摩擦占主导时，嵌入偏好。

No. 8论文详情NBER w34779

A.I. and Our Economic Future

人工智能与我们的经济未来

Charles I. Jones

Abstract

Artificial intelligence (A.I.) will likely be the most important technology we have ever developed. Technologies such as electricity, semiconductors, and the internet have been transformative, reshaping economic activity and dramatically increasing living standards throughout the world. In some sense, artificial intelligence is simply the latest of these general purpose technologies and at a minimum should continue the economic transformation that has been ongoing for the past century. However, the case can certainly be made that this time is different. Automating intelligence itself arguably has broader effects than electricity or semiconductors. What if machines—A.I. for cognitive tasks and A.I. plus advanced robots for physical tasks—can perform every task a human can do but more cheaply? What does economics have to say about this possibility, and what might our economic future look like?

中文摘要

人工智能很可能将是我们开发过的最重要的技术。像电力、半导体和互联网这样的技术已经具有变革性，重塑了经济活动并显著提高了全世界的生活水平。从某种意义上说，人工智能只是这些通用技术中最新的一个，至少应该延续过去一个世纪以来一直在进行的经济转型。然而，确实有理由认为这次情况不同。自动化智能本身的影响可能比电力或半导体更广泛。如果机器——用于认知任务的人工智能以及用于物理任务的人工智能加上先进机器人——能够以更低的成本执行人类能做的每一项任务，那会怎样？经济学对这种可能性有何看法，我们的经济未来可能是什么样子？

No. 9论文详情NBER w34778

The Effect of Charter Schools on Identification, Service Provision, and Achievement of Students with Disabilities

特许学校对残疾学生识别、服务提供及学业成就的影响

Scott A. Imberman, Andrew S. Johnson

Abstract

Students with disabilities (SWDs) encompass a sizable share of charter students and have an array of individualized needs. Charter schools may operate differently than traditional public schools with respect to SWDs and special education (SPED), as funding incentives may induce charter schools to underserve SWDs. Nonetheless, there is little empirical evidence regarding how enrollment in charter schools affects SWDs’ educational environments and outcomes. We use data from Michigan to estimate charter impacts using a heterogeneous difference-in-differences model that compares students who enter charters to students who have not yet but will eventually enter charters. We find that charters are slightly more likely to identify students as SWDs after charter entry. While assignments to SPED programs increase comparably, there is a significant reduction and subsequent reversion in time spent in SPED-specific environments and services provided. Despite these changes, SWDs realize achievement and attendance gains after charter entry at similar levels to non-SWDs.

中文摘要

残疾学生（SWDs）在特许学校学生中占有相当大的比例，并且具有一系列个性化的需求。在对待残疾学生和特殊教育（SPED）方面，特许学校的运作方式可能与传统公立学校不同，因为资金激励可能促使特许学校对残疾学生服务不足。尽管如此，关于就读特许学校如何影响残疾学生的教育环境和结果，目前几乎没有实证证据。我们使用密歇根州的数据，采用异质性双重差分模型来估计特许学校的影响，该模型将进入特许学校的学生与尚未进入但最终将进入特许学校的学生进行比较。我们发现，在进入特许学校后，特许学校将学生识别为残疾学生的可能性略高。虽然特殊教育项目的分配相应增加，但在特殊教育特定环境中度过的时间以及所提供的服务出现了显著减少，随后又恢复。尽管存在这些变化，残疾学生在进入特许学校后，其学业成就和出勤率的提升与非残疾学生处于相似水平。

No. 10论文详情NBER w34777

AI and the Quantity and Quality of Creative Products: Have LLMs Boosted Creation of Valuable Books?

人工智能与创意产品的数量和质量：大型语言模型是否促进了有价值书籍的创作？

Imke Reimers, Joel Waldfogel

Abstract

The diffusion of LLMs from 2022 to 2025 tripled new book releases. While average book quality, measured by usage, declined, the surge in releases raised the number of modest-quality books. Direct evidence using AI detection shows that AI-containing books have lower quality, and their rising share – topping half of 2025 releases – drives the overall decline. A nested logit calibration shows that AI books raised consumer surplus by seven percent in 2025. Author selection accounts for most of the AI quality differential, and the AI-human differential shrinks over time. Finally, AI has not displaced authors active prior to LLMs.

中文摘要

从2022年到2025年，大型语言模型（LLMs）的普及使新书发行量增加了两倍。虽然以使用量衡量的平均书籍质量有所下降，但发行量的激增提高了中等质量书籍的数量。使用人工智能检测的直接证据表明，包含人工智能内容的书籍质量较低，并且其不断上升的份额——在2025年发行量中占比超过一半——推动了整体质量的下降。嵌套Logit校准显示，人工智能书籍在2025年使消费者剩余增加了7%。作者选择解释了人工智能质量差异的大部分原因，并且人工智能与人类之间的质量差异随时间推移而缩小。最后，人工智能并未取代在大型语言模型出现之前活跃的作者。

No. 11论文详情NBER w34776

Audit Centralization and Audit Quality: Evidence from Chinese Cities

审计集权与审计质量：来自中国城市的证据

Jian Chu, Raymond Fisman, Yongxiang Wang, Maoliang Ye

Abstract

Audit design invokes a tradeoff between a monitor’s local knowledge and their independence from influence. We study this tradeoff in the context of a pilot program in six Chinese provinces in 2016, in which provincial governments were given control over budgeting and personnel decisions for city audits. Using a difference-in-differences framework we show that, compared to non-pilot provinces, centralization increases detection of suspicious expenditures by over 50%. These improvements occur also in cities with auditors appointed pre-2016, suggesting that stronger incentives and greater resources rather than auditor selection explain the improvements. Consistent with this interpretation, we find that financial (but not human) resources devoted to city audits increase with centralization. Further results show that centralization’s benefits are strongest in provinces that centralized audit office financing as part of the reform – particularly in poorer cities – suggesting a role for resources in improved performance.

中文摘要

审计设计涉及监督者的地方知识与其免受影响的独立性之间的权衡。我们以2016年中国六个省份的试点项目为背景研究这一权衡，在该项目中，省级政府获得了对城市审计预算和人事决策的控制权。使用双重差分框架，我们表明，与非试点省份相比，集权化使可疑支出的检出率提高了50%以上。这些改进也发生在2016年之前任命审计师的城市，这表明是更强的激励和更多的资源而非审计师的选择解释了这些改进。与这一解释一致，我们发现，随着集权化，投入到城市审计的财务（而非人力）资源有所增加。进一步的结果表明，集权化的好处在作为改革一部分而集中了审计办公室融资的省份最为显著——尤其是在较贫困的城市——这表明资源在绩效改善中发挥了作用。

No. 12论文详情NBER w34775

Immigration Restrictions and Natives' Intergenerational Mobility: Evidence from the 1920s US Quota Acts

移民限制与本地人的代际流动性：来自20世纪20年代美国配额法案的证据

James J. Feigenbaum, Yi-Ju Hung, Marco Tabellini, Monia Tomasella

Abstract

We study the effects of immigration restrictions on the intergenerational mobility of US-born men in the United States. We link US-born sons observed in 1900, 1920, and 1940 full-count Censuses to their fathers, and construct a measure of county-level exposure to the 1920s immigration acts, which sharply curtailed immigration from Southern and Eastern Europe. Exploiting this policy-induced variation, we find that the quotas reduced intergenerational mobility among US-born white men, but had no adverse effect for Black men. Among whites, losses were smaller for sons of richer fathers, who were more likely to migrate away from highly exposed areas. Evidence from the 1940 Census indicates that exposed white men were less likely to be employed and earned lower wages in adulthood, consistent with both occupational downgrading and reduced productivity within occupations. We show that these effects operated through both reduced immigrant–native complementarities and incomplete substitution from unrestricted migration, while human capital investment can explain at most only a modest part of the total effect.

中文摘要

我们研究了移民限制对美国本土出生男性代际流动性的影响。我们将1900年、1920年和1940年全量人口普查中观察到的美国本土出生儿子与其父亲进行匹配，并构建了一个县级层面的暴露于20世纪20年代移民法案的度量指标，该法案急剧削减了来自南欧和东欧的移民。利用这种由政策引起的变异，我们发现，这些配额降低了美国本土出生白人男性的代际流动性，但对黑人男性没有不利影响。在白人中，父亲更富有的儿子损失较小，他们更有可能从高暴露地区迁移出去。来自1940年人口普查的证据表明，暴露于该政策的白人男性在成年后就业的可能性更低，工资也更低，这与职业降级和职业内生产力下降是一致的。我们表明，这些影响是通过减少移民与本地人的互补性以及来自不受限制移民的不完全替代共同作用的，而人力资本投资最多只能解释总效应的一小部分。

No. 13论文详情NBER w34774

Estimating Demand Systems with Bidding Data

利用投标数据估计需求系统

Jason Allen, Jakub Kastl, Milena Wittwer

Abstract

We introduce a framework for estimating demand across multiple assets with bidding data. Unlike existing methods, our approach does not rely on price instruments, which are often difficult to obtain. We describe the data requirements for implementation and illustrate its versatility using two applications: message-level data from Nasdaq and bidder-level data from Canadian Treasury bill auctions. We argue that understanding demand systems is a crucial factor in assessing the impact of market design on price stability and liquidity.

中文摘要

我们引入了一个利用投标数据估计跨多种资产需求的框架。与现有方法不同，我们的方法不依赖于通常难以获得的价格工具变量。我们描述了实施所需的数据条件，并通过两个应用说明了其多功能性：来自纳斯达克的逐笔数据以及来自加拿大国库券拍卖的投标人层面数据。我们认为，理解需求系统是评估市场设计对价格稳定性和流动性影响的关键因素。

No. 14论文详情NBER w34773

How do Foundations Help Charities (Beyond Giving them Money)?

基金会如何帮助慈善机构（除了给钱之外）？

Daniel M. Hungerman, Teresa Harrison, Sherry X. Li

Abstract

Foundations are a rapidly growing source of charitable support, yet their effects on nonprofits remain poorly understood. We study applicants to a $\$100$ million funding competition whose sponsoring foundation subsequently offered publicity, networking, and advice to a subset of unsuccessful entrants. This support substantially improved later fundraising for smaller charities. Our estimates indicate that the foundation’s support generated over $\$40$ million in income in the years following the competition. These findings offer novel evidence of how large donors can influence nonprofit success even without awarding funds, and show how funding competitions might be structured to help charities raise additional resources.

中文摘要

基金会是慈善支持的一个快速增长来源，但它们对非营利组织的影响仍然知之甚少。我们研究了一个1亿美元资助竞赛的申请者，该竞赛的赞助基金会随后向一部分未获胜的参赛者提供了宣传、社交网络和建议。这种支持显著改善了小型慈善机构后来的筹款情况。我们的估计表明，该基金会的支持在竞赛结束后的几年内产生了超过4000万美元的收入。这些发现提供了新的证据，表明大型捐赠者即使不提供资金也能影响非营利组织的成功，并展示了资助竞赛如何被设计来帮助慈善机构筹集额外资源。

No. 15论文详情NBER w34772

Stress Relief? Externalities from Specialty Hospital Entry

缓解压力？专科医院进入的外部性

Daniel R. Arnold, Michael R. Richards, Christopher M. Whaley

Abstract

Mental illness exacts a heavy toll on the US healthcare system and strains general hospitals and their emergency departments. We study how psychiatric inpatient facility entry impacts the local hospital industry. We find that referrals, including from the legal system, are redirected to the specialized facilities––leaving general hospitals with approximately 60% fewer psychiatric admissions. General hospitals also discharge 50% more patients to psychiatric facilities and substitute away from high-skill psychiatric labor––consistent with specialization and market segmentation. Emergency department volumes do not change but care does. However, community-based crime, overdose deaths, and suicides do not decline in the short-run.

中文摘要

精神疾病给美国医疗系统带来了沉重负担，并使综合医院及其急诊科承受压力。我们研究了精神科住院设施进入对当地医院行业的影响。我们发现，包括来自法律系统的转诊被重新导向这些专科设施——使得综合医院的精神科入院人数减少了约60%。综合医院也将多出50%的患者出院至精神科设施，并减少了对高技能精神科劳动力的使用——这与专业化和市场细分是一致的。急诊科的就诊量没有变化，但护理内容发生了变化。然而，社区犯罪、药物过量死亡和自杀在短期内并未减少。

No. 16论文详情NBER w34771

Dynamic Selection and the Puzzle of Slow Climate Change Adaptation in U.S. Agriculture

动态选择与美国农业气候变化适应缓慢之谜

Robert Huang, Matthew E. Kahn

Abstract

Long-run studies of agricultural productivity use balanced county-level panel data to document slow adaptation to climate change in U.S. agriculture. We revisit this treatment-effect puzzle using a selection model that incorporates the optimizing behavior of heterogeneous farmers. Using data from 1980 to 2020, we document three dynamic selection effects. First, counties that completely exit farming alter the composition of the balanced panel sample. Second, higher-skilled workers are more likely to leave rural areas as weather conditions worsen. Third, smaller farms consolidate into larger farms in counties affected by climate change. We document that the yield damage function’s slope depends on the county’s educational level and farm size. Causal estimates of weather impacts must account for selection effects along several adaptation margins of adjustment.

中文摘要

关于农业生产力长期的研究使用平衡的县级面板数据，记录了美国农业对气候变化适应缓慢的现象。我们使用一个包含异质性农民优化行为的选择模型重新审视这个处理效应之谜。利用1980年至2020年的数据，我们记录了三种动态选择效应。首先，完全退出农业的县改变了平衡面板样本的构成。其次，随着天气条件恶化，技能更高的工人更有可能离开农村地区。第三，在受气候变化影响的县，较小的农场合并为较大的农场。我们记录了产量损害函数的斜率取决于该县的教育水平和农场规模。对天气影响的因果估计必须考虑沿着多个适应调整边际的选择效应。

No. 17论文详情NBER w34770

The Life-cycle of Concentrated Industries

集中产业的生命周期

Martin Beraja, Francisco J. Buera

Abstract

Are competition policies designed for static industries suitable for innovative industries where dynamic competition for the market is key? If not, how should policies differ? We develop a model of the life-cycle of an oligopolistic industry: a version of Jovanovic and MacDonald (1994) with a finite number of firms. The equilibrium features a period of intense entry, followed by a shakeout and eventual industry concentration as some firms scale through innovation while most exit. We analyze the second-best problem of a government subsidizing small firms to promote competition. Innovation and dynamic competition do not necessarily justify intervention, as the equilibrium can still be second best. In general, the optimal policy depends on the nature of competition. Firms primarily compete for the market when innovation leads to large differences in scale. The government can wait to intervene in this case; committing to do whatever it takes to promote competition if and when the industry concentrates excessively. Subsidies early in the life-cycle are unnecessary. These results contrast with calls for aggressive ex-ante regulation in highly innovative industries, suggesting a wait-and-see approach may be preferable. We apply these insights to digital and AI industries in the U.S. using data on venture-backed firms.

中文摘要

为静态产业设计的竞争政策是否适用于以市场动态竞争为关键的创新产业？如果不适用，政策应如何不同？我们构建了一个寡头垄断产业生命周期的模型：这是Jovanovic和MacDonald（1994）的一个版本，其中包含有限数量的企业。均衡的特征是激烈的进入期，随后是洗牌期，并最终导致产业集中，因为一些企业通过创新实现规模化，而大多数企业退出。我们分析了政府补贴小企业以促进竞争的次优问题。创新和动态竞争并不必然证明干预是合理的，因为均衡仍然可能是次优的。一般来说，最优政策取决于竞争的性质。当创新导致规模差异巨大时，企业主要争夺市场。在这种情况下，政府可以等待干预；承诺在产业过度集中时不惜一切代价促进竞争。生命周期早期的补贴是不必要的。这些结果与在高度创新产业中呼吁积极事前监管的观点形成对比，表明观望方法可能更可取。我们利用风险投资支持企业的数据，将这些见解应用于美国的数字和人工智能产业。

No. 18论文详情NBER w34769

Why Does Height Pay? Evidence from the Kenya Life Panel Survey

身高为何带来收入溢价？来自肯尼亚生命面板调查的证据

Wilson King, Edward Miguel, Michael W. Walker

Abstract

Taller people earn more, especially in low- and middle-income countries. We present among the first evidence of this phenomenon in Africa, using longitudinal microdata on a cohort of middle-aged Kenyan adults. We document a substantial height/earnings premium: controlling for gender, age, and other socio-demographics, monthly earnings increase by 1.07% per centimeter (or 2.72% per inch). Nearly half this effect can be explained by differences in cognition, measured from an unusually rich battery containing 27 modules. Additional shares of the premium can be attributed to measures of physical strength and non-cognitive ability. In contrast to prior work, we find little role for occupational sorting: conditional on cognitive and non-cognitive ability, taller people do not appear more likely to work in higher paid sectors. Leveraging repeated measures of height and an instrumental variables specification, we find suggestive evidence that measurement error may be attenuating the estimated relationship.

中文摘要

身高较高的人收入更高，尤其是在低收入和中等收入国家。我们利用肯尼亚中年成年人队列的纵向微观数据，提供了非洲这一现象的首批证据之一。我们记录了一个显著的身高/收入溢价：在控制性别、年龄和其他社会人口学特征后，月收入每厘米增加1.07%（或每英寸增加2.72%）。近一半的这种效应可以通过认知差异来解释，认知能力由一个包含27个模块的异常丰富的测试组来衡量。溢价的额外部分可归因于身体力量和非认知能力的测量。与先前的研究相反，我们发现职业分类的作用很小：在控制认知和非认知能力后，身高较高的人似乎并不更有可能在收入更高的部门工作。利用身高的重复测量和工具变量设定，我们发现了暗示性证据，表明测量误差可能正在衰减估计的关系。

No. 19论文详情NBER w34768

Welfare Added? Optimal Teacher Assignment with Value-Added Measures

福利增加？利用增值指标的最优教师分配

Tanner S. Eastmond, Michael Ricks, Julian Betts, Nathan Mather

Abstract

We study how teacher "value added" should inform optimal teacher-assignment policy. Our welfare-theoretic framework illustrates (1) how theoretically optimal assignments leverage variation in teachers' impacts both across student types and across different outcomes, and (2) how empirically optimal assignments trade off improved targeting from estimating richer student heterogeneity against increasing misallocation risk. In practice, optimal assignments use limited student types (only lagged achievement) and multiple outcomes (not just math). Even after correcting for policy overfitting, assignments raise average present-value earnings by $\$2,800$ and increase lower-achieving students' earnings by 70-156% more than benchmark value-added policies that assume that teacher effects are homogeneous across students, that allow for heterogeneous effects across students but for a single subject, or teacher deselection.

中文摘要

我们研究教师“增值”应如何为最优教师分配政策提供信息。我们的福利理论框架说明了（1）理论上最优的分配如何利用教师对不同学生类型以及不同结果影响的差异，以及（2）经验上最优的分配如何在通过估计更丰富的学生异质性来改善目标定位与增加错误分配风险之间进行权衡。在实践中，最优分配使用有限的学生类型（仅滞后成绩）和多个结果（不仅仅是数学）。即使在纠正政策过拟合之后，与假设教师效应在学生间是同质的、允许对学生有异质性效应但仅限于单一学科、或教师淘汰的基准增值政策相比，这些分配使平均现值收入增加2,800美元，并使成绩较低学生的收入增加70-156%。

No. 20论文详情NBER w34767

Life-Cycle Effects of Women's Education on their Careers and Children

女性教育对其职业生涯和子女的生命周期效应

Na'ama Shenhav, Danielle H. Sandler

Abstract

We study the causal effect of women's education on their wages, non-wage job amenities, and spillovers to children. Using a regression discontinuity at the school entry birthdate cutoff, we find that women born just before the cutoff are more likely to complete some college, and experience multi-dimensional career gains that grow over the life cycle: greater employment and earnings, as well as more professional and higher-status jobs, more socially meaningful work, and better working conditions. Children’s early-life health and prenatal inputs improve in tandem with career improvements, consistent with professional advances spurring—not hindering—infant investments. Career gains are concentrated in jobs that require exactly some college, the same schooling margin shifted by the cutoff, which indicates that increased post-secondary education is the primary channel for these effects. Together, the results show that women's college attendance generates large career returns—from both wages and amenities—that strengthen over time and produce meaningful benefits for children.

中文摘要

我们研究女性教育对其工资、非工资工作福利以及对子女溢出效应的因果影响。利用学校入学出生日期截止点的断点回归，我们发现，出生在截止点之前的女性更有可能完成部分大学教育，并经历多维度的职业收益，这些收益在整个生命周期中增长：更高的就业率和收入，以及更专业和更高地位的工作、更具社会意义的工作和更好的工作条件。儿童的早期健康产前投入随着职业改善而同步改善，这与职业进步促进而非阻碍婴儿投资的结论一致。职业收益集中在恰好需要部分大学教育的工作中，这与截止点所改变的教育边际相同，表明高等教育程度的增加是这些效应的主要渠道。总之，结果表明，女性上大学带来了巨大的职业回报——包括工资和福利——这些回报随着时间的推移而增强，并为儿童带来有意义的益处。

No. 21论文详情NBER w34766

Competition, Procurement and Learning-By-Doing in the Space Launch Industry

太空发射行业的竞争、采购与干中学

Ruibing Su, Chenyu Yang, Andrew Sweeting

Abstract

We estimate a dynamic model of the U.S. space launch industry. The model allows past launches to improve rocket reliability and lower launch costs. It also allows the government to make forward-looking procurement choices. We use the model to analyze policy-relevant issues in the recent history of the industry: the 2006 United Launch Alliance “merger-to-monopoly” and the effects of efficiencies in the form of learning synergies; innovations, such as SpaceX's Falcon 9 and ULA's recent introduction of Vulcan Centaur; the costs and benefits of forward-looking procurements; and, the trade-offs between the advantages of centralized control and possible inefficiencies.

中文摘要

我们估计了一个美国太空发射行业的动态模型。该模型允许过去的发射提高火箭可靠性并降低发射成本。它还允许政府做出前瞻性的采购选择。我们利用该模型分析该行业近期历史中与政策相关的问题：2006年联合发射联盟的“垄断式合并”以及学习协同效应形式的效率影响；创新，例如SpaceX的猎鹰9号和ULA最近推出的火神半人马座；前瞻性采购的成本和收益；以及集中控制的优势与可能的低效率之间的权衡。

No. 22论文详情NBER w34765

The Future of Monetarism after Milton Friedman

米尔顿·弗里德曼之后货币主义的未来

Michael D. Bordo

Abstract

On the fiftieth anniversary of Milton Friedman receiving the Nobel Prize in economics, I reflect on the legacy of monetarism – his revolutionary idea. Friedman developed the modern quantity of money in 1956 as a challenge to the prevailing Keynesian view that “money did not matter.” Friedman’s empirical and historical research made a strong case that changes in the money supply, largely instituted by the monetary authorities, account for much of the macro instability in the twentieth century including the Great Recession 1929-1933 and the Great Inflation 1965 -1982. Friedman’s ideas were at the base of the creation of modern macroeconomics, and of the adoption by many central banks of rules based monetary policy as a guidepost to maintain credibility for low inflation. His emphasis on monetary aggregates as the key monetary policy tool has been superseded by the use of policy interest rates, but the monetary aggregates are still useful as a crosscheck against incipient high inflation.

中文摘要

在米尔顿·弗里德曼获得诺贝尔经济学奖五十周年之际，我反思了货币主义——他的革命性思想——的遗产。弗里德曼在1956年发展了现代货币数量论，作为对当时盛行的凯恩斯主义“货币无关紧要”观点的挑战。弗里德曼的实证和历史研究有力地证明了，主要由货币当局实施的货币供应量变化，是20世纪大部分宏观不稳定的原因，包括1929-1933年的大萧条和1965-1982年的大通胀。弗里德曼的思想是现代宏观经济学创建的基础，也是许多中央银行采用基于规则的货币政策作为维持低通胀可信度指南的基础。他强调货币总量作为关键货币政策工具的观点已被政策利率的使用所取代，但货币总量作为对初期高通胀的交叉检查仍然有用。

No. 23论文详情NBER w34764

How Does Tort Reform Affect Health Care Delivery?

侵权法改革如何影响医疗保健服务？

Charles J. Courtemanche, Joseph Garuccio

Abstract

Health care costs in the U.S. have grown dramatically over the past several decades, with one possible cause being physicians providing unnecessary services out of fear of being sued for malpractice – a phenomenon known as “defensive medicine”. States responded by enacting different types of tort reforms. This paper reviews the literature on the effects of these tort reforms on outcomes related to malpractice risk, quantity and quality of health care services, overall utilization and expenditures, physician supply, and patient affordability. We use Google Scholar to identify papers that fall into this scope and use either associational or quasi-experimental quantitative methods. The preponderance of evidence points towards non-economic damage caps reducing malpractice risk, quantity of services (aside from diagnostics and obstetrics), and overall health care utilization and expenditures while increasing physician supply and not having detrimental effects on patient outcomes. In general, the effects of other types of tort reforms are less clear. The literature would benefit from further research utilizing recent methodological advances related to combining machine learning with causal inference and eliminating bias from heterogeneous treatment effects in staggered-treatment-time models.

中文摘要

美国医疗保健成本在过去几十年中急剧增长，一个可能的原因是医生出于担心被起诉医疗事故而提供不必要的服务——这种现象被称为“防御性医疗”。各州通过颁布不同类型的侵权法改革来应对。本文回顾了关于这些侵权法改革对医疗事故风险、医疗保健服务的数量和质量、总体利用率和支出、医生供应以及患者可负担性等相关结果影响的文献。我们使用谷歌学术来识别属于此范围并使用关联性或准实验定量方法的论文。大量证据表明，非经济损害赔偿上限降低了医疗事故风险、服务数量（除诊断和产科外）以及总体医疗保健利用率和支出，同时增加了医生供应，并且对患者结果没有产生不利影响。总的来说，其他类型侵权法改革的效果不太明确。该领域将受益于进一步的研究，利用最近的方法论进展，这些进展涉及将机器学习与因果推断相结合，以及在交错处理时间模型中消除异质性处理效应的偏差。

No. 24论文详情NBER w34763

Driving Innovation: The Policy Tools Powering Electric Vehicle Technological Inventions

驱动创新：推动电动汽车技术发明的政策工具

Jingni Zhang, David Popp

Abstract

Electric vehicles (EVs) are crucial for cutting transportation emissions, yet the policy drivers of EV innovation remain underexplored. This study analyzes firm-level panel data on EV and battery patents, covering more than 4,000 firms across 19 countries from 2010 to 2021, to assess how these policy tools and their interactions in different time horizons influence innovative activity. We test the effects of individual policy instruments that either raise demand for EVs or support the development of EV technologies. Stringent fuel-economy standards, financial incentives, adoption targets, and public R&D investments each significantly increase patenting in EV and battery technologies. Moreover, long-term EV targets amplify the innovative impact of public R&D and standards while diminishing the marginal effect of short-term price signals. The results suggest that governments can accelerate clean automotive innovation by combining long-term adoption commitments with sustained R&D investment or strong performance standards, and by managing these instruments as a coordinated policy portfolio rather than as separate tools. The study contributes cross-country, firm-level evidence that links policy design to the direction of clean technology innovation.

中文摘要

电动汽车对于减少交通排放至关重要，然而电动汽车创新的政策驱动因素仍未得到充分探索。本研究分析了涵盖2010年至2021年19个国家4000多家企业的电动汽车和电池专利的企业层面面板数据，以评估这些政策工具及其在不同时间范围内的相互作用如何影响创新活动。我们测试了提高电动汽车需求或支持电动汽车技术发展的个别政策工具的效果。严格的燃油经济性标准、财政激励、采用目标和公共研发投资各自显著增加了电动汽车和电池技术的专利申请。此外，长期电动汽车目标放大了公共研发和标准的创新影响，同时削弱了短期价格信号的边际效应。结果表明，政府可以通过将长期采用承诺与持续的研发投资或强有力的绩效标准相结合，并将这些工具作为协调的政策组合而非单独的工具来管理，从而加速清洁汽车创新。该研究提供了跨国、企业层面的证据，将政策设计与清洁技术创新的方向联系起来。

No. 25论文详情NBER w34762

The Macroeconomic Effects of Climate Policy Uncertainty

气候政策不确定性的宏观经济效应

Konstantinos Gavriilidis, Diego R. Känzig, Ramya Raghavan, James H. Stock

Abstract

We develop a measure of climate policy uncertainty based on newspaper coverage. Our index spikes during key U.S. climate policy events—including presidential announcements on international agreements, congressional debates, and regulatory disputes—and shows a recent upward trend. Using a novel instrument for plausibly exogenous uncertainty shifts, we find that higher climate policy uncertainty decreases output and emissions while raising commodity and consumer prices, acting as supply rather than demand shocks. Faced with this trade-off, monetary policy does not accommodate climate policy uncertainty shocks, shaping their transmission. Firm-level analyses show stronger declines in investment and R&D when firms have higher climate change exposure.

中文摘要

我们基于报纸报道构建了一个气候政策不确定性指标。该指标在美国关键气候政策事件期间（包括总统关于国际协议的声明、国会辩论和监管争议）出现峰值，并显示出近期的上升趋势。利用一个用于识别合理外生不确定性冲击的新工具变量，我们发现气候政策不确定性上升会降低产出和排放，同时推高大宗商品和消费价格，其作用类似于供给冲击而非需求冲击。面对这种权衡，货币政策并未对气候政策不确定性冲击做出适应性调整，从而塑造了其传导机制。企业层面的分析表明，当企业对气候变化的暴露程度更高时，其投资和研发的下降幅度更大。

No. 26论文详情NBER w34761

Clientelism: How It Works, Why It Persists and How to Break It

庇护主义：运作机制、持续原因与破解之道

Jimmy Graham, Horacio Larreguy, Pablo Querubín

Abstract

This chapter surveys the economics and political science literature on clientelism. We define clientelism as the exchange of votes or electoral participation for targeted material benefits and argue that it undermines electoral accountability, fostering rent-seeking and the underprovision of public goods. We document the prevalence of clientelism across countries and over time and examine how economic underdevelopment both facilitates clientelistic practices and may be perpetuated by them. We then analyze the agency problems that characterize clientelistic exchanges, focusing on broker–voter and politician–broker relationships, and review evidence on the roles of monitoring, selection, and social networks in sustaining these relationships. Finally, we discuss how clientelistic machines are financed, assess interventions aimed at weakening clientelism and promoting programmatic competition, and outline directions for future research.

中文摘要

本章综述了关于庇护主义的经济学和政治学文献。我们将庇护主义定义为用选票或选举参与换取有针对性的物质利益，并认为它削弱了选举问责制，助长了寻租行为和公共产品供给不足。我们记录了庇护主义在不同国家和时期的普遍性，并考察了经济欠发达如何既便利了庇护主义实践，又可能被其固化。接着，我们分析了庇护主义交换中特有的代理问题，重点关注中间人-选民和政客-中间人关系，并回顾了关于监督、筛选和社会网络在维持这些关系中作用的证据。最后，我们讨论了庇护主义机器如何获得资金，评估了旨在削弱庇护主义并促进纲领性竞争的干预措施，并概述了未来研究的方向。

Mapping Technological Trajectories: Evidence from Two Centuries of Patent Data

绘制技术轨迹：来自两个世纪专利数据的证据

Antonin Bergeaud, Ruveyda Nur Gozen, John Van Reenen

Abstract

We introduce a methodology to measure cross-country trends in innovation capability - “technological trajectories” and implement this on a new rich dataset covering patents between 1836 and 2016 across multiple countries. Intuitively, trajectories are revealed by a country’s sustained increases in patenting across multiple patent offices. We first describe the data patterns, showing the relative decline of the UK, and the rise first of the US and Germany, and then later of Japan and China. We then econometrically estimate trajectories on (i) the post-1902 period for France, Germany, Japan, the UK and US, and (ii) the post-1960 period for a wider sample of 40 countries. Our trajectories are strongly positively correlated with Total Factor Productivity growth, and also (but less strongly) associated with the growth of labour productivity and capital intensity. We show that future trajectories are predicted by a country’s initial levels of R&D, education and defence spending, classic drivers of innovation in modern growth theory.

中文摘要

我们引入了一种衡量各国创新能力趋势（即“技术轨迹”）的方法，并将其应用于一个涵盖1836年至2016年间多个国家的新专利数据集。直观上，技术轨迹通过一个国家在多个专利局持续增加的专利申请量来揭示。我们首先描述了数据模式，显示了英国的相对衰落，以及美国、德国首先崛起，随后日本和中国崛起的趋势。接着，我们通过计量经济学方法估算了以下时期的技术轨迹：(i) 1902年后法国、德国、日本、英国和美国的时期，以及 (ii) 1960年后一个包含40个国家的更广泛样本的时期。我们的技术轨迹与全要素生产率增长呈强正相关，也与劳动生产率增长和资本密集度增长相关（但相关性较弱）。我们表明，未来的技术轨迹可由一个国家初始的研发、教育和国防支出水平来预测，这些是现代增长理论中经典的创新驱动因素。

No. 28论文详情NBER w34759

Poverty and Dependency in the United States, 1939–2023

美国的贫困与依赖，1939–2023

Richard V. Burkhauser, Kevin Corinth

Abstract

We compare trends in absolute poverty before (1939–1963) and after (1963–2023) the War on Poverty was declared. Our primary methodological contribution is to create a post-tax post-transfer income measure using the 1940, 1950 and 1960 Decennial Censuses through imputations of taxes and transfers as well as certain forms of market income including perquisites (Collins and Wanamaker 2022), consistent with the full income measures developed by Burkhauser et al. (2024) for subsequent years. From 1939–1963, poverty fell by 29 percentage points, with even larger declines for Black people and all children. While absolute poverty continued to fall following the War on Poverty’s declaration, the pace was no faster, even when evaluating the trends relative to a consistent initial poverty rate. Furthermore, the pre-1964 decline in poverty among working age adults and children was achieved almost completely through increases in market income, during which time only 2–3 percent of working age adults were dependent on the government for at least half of their income, compared to dependency rates of 7–15 percent from 1972–2023. In contrast to progress on absolute poverty, reductions in relative poverty were more modest from 1939–1963 and even less so since then.

中文摘要

我们比较了“向贫困宣战”宣布之前（1939–1963年）和之后（1963–2023年）绝对贫困的趋势。我们的主要方法论贡献是，利用1940年、1950年和1960年十年一次的人口普查数据，通过对税收和转移支付以及某些形式的市场收入（包括津贴，参见Collins and Wanamaker 2022）进行插补，创建了一个税后转移后收入衡量指标，这与Burkhauser等人（2024）为后续年份开发的全面收入指标保持一致。从1939年到1963年，贫困率下降了29个百分点，黑人群体和所有儿童的贫困率下降幅度更大。尽管在“向贫困宣战”宣布后绝对贫困率继续下降，但其下降速度并未加快，即使相对于一致的初始贫困率来评估趋势也是如此。此外，1964年之前劳动年龄成人和儿童贫困率的下降几乎完全是通过市场收入的增加实现的，在此期间，只有2-3%的劳动年龄成人至少一半的收入依赖政府，而1972年至2023年期间的依赖率为7-15%。与绝对贫困方面的进展相比，相对贫困的减少在1939-1963年间更为温和，而自那以后则更加有限。

The Redistributive Effects of Federal Medicaid Outlays Across Counties: Evidence from the ACA

联邦医疗补助支出在县级层面的再分配效应：来自《平价医疗法案》的证据

Laura Montenovo, Kosali I. Simon, Coady Wing

Abstract

We examine how Medicaid expansion under the Affordable Care Act reshaped federal transfer inflows to counties using state Medicaid expansions between 2014 and 2017. We show that the ACA expansion increased federal Medicaid transfers by $\$361$ per capita in expansion counties. Using our estimates, we forecast that non-expansion counties would gain $\$554$ per capita if they expanded Medicaid. These transfers flow to counties with lower tax capacity and lower gross income. Our findings suggest that Medicaid expansion was a health policy intervention that also functioned as a budgetary mechanism reshaping federal to local transfers and fiscal smoothing across U.S. counties.

中文摘要

我们利用2014年至2017年间的州级医疗补助扩展，考察了《平价医疗法案》下的医疗补助扩展如何重塑了流向各县的联邦转移支付。我们表明，《平价医疗法案》扩展使扩展县的联邦医疗补助转移支付人均增加了361美元。利用我们的估计，我们预测如果非扩展县扩展医疗补助，它们将人均获得554美元。这些转移支付流向了税收能力较低和总收入较低的县。我们的研究结果表明，医疗补助扩展是一项健康政策干预，同时也作为一种预算机制，重塑了联邦到地方的转移支付以及美国各县之间的财政平滑。

No. 30论文详情NBER w34757

What Happens When Dating Goes Online? Evidence from U.S. Marriage Markets and Health Outcomes

当约会转向线上会发生什么？来自美国婚姻市场和健康结果的证据

Daniel Ershov, Jessica Fong, Pinar Yildirim

Abstract

This paper studies how online dating platforms have impacted marital outcomes, assortative matching, and sexually transmitted disease (STD) rates in the United States. We construct county-level measures of online dating usage using data from website-based platforms (2002–2013) and mobile app-based platforms (2017–2023). Leveraging county-level variation and an instrumental variable strategy, we show in the desktop era, a 1% increase in online dating sessions raises divorce rates by 0.50%, while in the mobile era, a 1% increase in online dating activity lowers marriage and divorce rates by 0.40% and 0.33%, respectively. We also document shifts in assortative matching. Desktop sites reduce sorting along education and employment dimensions, whereas mobile sites reduce sorting by employment, but increase sorting by race. Across both eras, we find no evidence that greater online dating usage increases average STD rates. Average effects are negative or statistically insignificant, but are positive for some subpopulations. We develop a search and matching model where technological changes that impact search costs, market size, and market noise can explain our empirical findings.

中文摘要

本文研究了在线约会平台如何影响美国的婚姻结果、分类匹配和性传播疾病发病率。我们利用基于网站的平台（2002-2013年）和基于移动应用平台（2017-2023年）的数据构建了县级在线约会使用量指标。利用县级差异和工具变量策略，我们表明，在桌面时代，在线约会会话量每增加1%，离婚率上升0.50%；而在移动时代，在线约会活动量每增加1%，结婚率和离婚率分别下降0.40%和0.33%。我们还记录了分类匹配的变化。桌面网站减少了按教育和就业维度的分类，而移动网站减少了按就业维度的分类，但增加了按种族的分类。在两个时代，我们都没有发现证据表明在线约会使用量增加会提高平均性传播疾病发病率。平均效应为负或统计上不显著，但对某些亚群而言为正效应。我们开发了一个搜索匹配模型，其中影响搜索成本、市场规模和市场噪音的技术变化可以解释我们的实证发现。

No. 31论文详情NBER w34756

Wedges: A Microeconomic Perspective on Misallocation

楔子：资源错配的微观经济学视角

Lauren F. Bergquist, Danial Lashkari, Eric Verhoogen

Abstract

This chapter takes stock of what has been learned from the recent micro-development literature about wedges—mechanisms generating dispersion in marginal revenue products of factors across firms, which are commonly interpreted as indicators of misallocation. We present a general theoretical framework that allows us to consider several different types of wedges simultaneously. We argue that it is important to distinguish between between technological wedges, which are present even in the efficient allocation that would be chosen by the social planner, and distortionary wedges, which are present in market equilibrium but not the social planner's allocation. Not all wedges, as we have defined them, are distortionary. We also argue that interactions among wedges are pervasive. We review empirical findings about different types of wedges—taxes, regulations, political connections, corruption, market power, contracting frictions, upgrading investments, and search—focusing on studies that present direct evidence on particular wedges and how they generate dispersion in marginal returns to factors. Throughout, we pay special attention to how wedges vary with firm size and whether the evidence supports the “large firms are constrained” view of development. We conclude with thoughts about promising directions for the misallocation literature.

中文摘要

本章总结了近期微观发展文献关于楔子（即导致企业间要素边际收益产品离散的机制，通常被解释为资源错配的指标）的研究成果。我们提出了一个通用的理论框架，允许我们同时考虑几种不同类型的楔子。我们认为，区分技术性楔子（即使在中央计划者会选择的有效配置中也存在）和扭曲性楔子（在市场均衡中存在但中央计划者的配置中不存在）非常重要。并非所有我们定义的楔子都是扭曲性的。我们还认为，楔子之间的相互作用是普遍存在的。我们回顾了关于不同类型楔子（税收、监管、政治关联、腐败、市场势力、契约摩擦、升级投资和搜寻）的实证发现，重点关注那些提供关于特定楔子及其如何导致要素边际回报离散的直接证据的研究。在整个过程中，我们特别关注楔子如何随企业规模变化，以及证据是否支持“大企业受到约束”的发展观。最后，我们提出了关于资源错配文献未来有前景方向的思考。

No. 32论文详情NBER w34755

Learning to Quit? A Multi-Year, Multi-Site Field Experiment with Innovation-Driven Entrepreneurs

学会退出？一项针对创新驱动型创业者的多年、多地点现场实验

Esther Bailey, Daniel Fehder, Eric Floyd, Yael Hochberg, Daniel J. Lee

Abstract

We use a randomized experiment with 553 science- and technology-based startups in 12 co-working spaces across the US to evaluate the effects of intensive, short-term entrepreneurial training programs on survival and performance for innovation-driven startups. Treated startups are more likely to shut down their businesses and do so sooner than control startups. Conditional on survival, however, treated startups are more likely to raise external funding for their ventures, raise funding faster, and raise more funding than the control group; they also exhibit higher employment and revenue. Treated founders are less likely to found a new startup after shutdown. Our findings are consistent with practitioner arguments that early entrepreneurship training interventions can help entrepreneurs with less viable ventures “rationally quit” (“fail fast”). We use machine learning techniques (causal random forest) to provide exploratory insights on the most impacted subgroups.

中文摘要

我们利用一项随机实验，对分布在美国12个联合办公空间的553家科技型初创企业进行了研究，以评估密集的短期创业培训项目对创新驱动型初创企业生存和绩效的影响。与对照组相比，接受培训的初创企业更有可能关闭其业务，并且关闭得更快。然而，在存活下来的条件下，接受培训的初创企业比对照组更有可能为其企业获得外部融资，融资速度更快，融资金额也更多；它们还表现出更高的就业和收入。接受培训的创始人在企业关闭后创立新初创企业的可能性更低。我们的发现与从业者的论点一致，即早期的创业培训干预可以帮助那些可行性较低的企业的创业者“理性退出”（“快速失败”）。我们使用机器学习技术（因果随机森林）来提供关于受影响最大子群体的探索性见解。

No. 33论文详情NBER w34754

The Macroeconomic Effects of Neighborhood Policies: a Dynamic Analysis

邻里政策的宏观经济效应：一项动态分析

Alessandra Fogli, Veronica Guerrieri, Mark Ponder, Marta Prato

Abstract

We study the macroeconomic effects of neighborhood-specific policies in a general equilibrium model of a city with endogenous residential sorting and educational investment. A key feature of the model is the presence of endogenous local spillovers that depend on the distribution of families across neighborhoods. We analyze three policies: a housing-voucher policy inspired by the MTO program, which enables poor families to relocate to low-poverty neighborhoods; a place-based transfer (PBT) policy that provides monetary transfers to families in poor neighborhoods; and a place-based investment (PBI) policy that invests resources in local institutions, such as public schools, to directly enhance local spillovers. We find that the MTO policy generates substantial income gains for children of recipient families, but scaling up the program dampens these gains and induces large welfare losses for non-recipients. By contrast, the PBT policy delivers larger average welfare gains but is less effective in reducing inequality and segregation. Finally, the PBI policy produces smaller short-run effects but, over time, resolves the trade-off by raising average welfare while simultaneously reducing inequality, lowering segregation, and improving intergenerational mobility.

中文摘要

我们在一个具有内生居住分选和教育投资的城市一般均衡模型中，研究了针对特定邻里政策的宏观经济效应。该模型的一个关键特征是存在内生的地方性溢出效应，这种效应取决于家庭在邻里间的分布。我们分析了三种政策：一项受“搬向机遇”项目启发的住房券政策，该政策使贫困家庭能够搬迁到低贫困率的邻里；一项基于地点的转移支付政策，为贫困邻里的家庭提供货币转移；以及一项基于地点的投资政策，将资源投资于当地机构（如公立学校），以直接增强地方性溢出效应。我们发现，“搬向机遇”政策为受益家庭的子女带来了可观的收入增长，但扩大该项目的规模会削弱这些收益，并给非受益者带来巨大的福利损失。相比之下，基于地点的转移支付政策带来了更大的平均福利收益，但在减少不平等和隔离方面效果较差。最后，基于地点的投资政策在短期内产生的效果较小，但随着时间的推移，它通过提高平均福利，同时减少不平等、降低隔离并改善代际流动性，解决了这一权衡问题。

No. 34论文详情NBER w34753

Psychology and Development: Applications from Cognitive and Social Psychology

心理学与发展：来自认知心理学和社会心理学的应用

Emily Breza, Supreet Kaur

Abstract

We outline a research agenda for behavioral development economics that seeks to understand the role of psychological channels in: (i) impeding individuals' ability to climb out of poverty, and (ii) shaping the organization of production, functioning of markets, and role of informal institutions in developing countries. We apply a missing markets lens to rationalize why tools, products and services that help individuals overcome their biases will be under-supplied by the market and why behavioral biases can have large impacts in steady state, even among highly experienced agents. We argue that these biases are especially likely to matter for the field of development because core features of poverty---proximity to subsistence, high volatility, market failures, weak formal institutions, and reliance on social ties---amplify the impact of psychological constraints. We organize our review around a core set of psychological constructs: self-control, cognitive constraints, self-beliefs, mental health, and social norms. For each construct, we highlight places where there is only a proof of concept versus evidence of meaningful impacts, and the resultant implications for future research. We also highlight where social capital can be deployed to mitigate the impacts of missing markets. The field research to date has only begun to scratch the surface in document how psychological mechanisms affect behavior and decision-making, and substantial scope remains for future work to determine whether these constraints play a first-order role in shaping poverty.

中文摘要

我们概述了行为发展经济学的研究议程，旨在理解心理渠道在以下方面的作用：(i) 阻碍个人摆脱贫困的能力，以及 (ii) 塑造发展中国家的生产组织、市场运作和非正式制度的作用。我们运用“缺失市场”的视角来解释，为什么帮助个人克服其偏见的工具、产品和服务会由市场供给不足，以及为什么行为偏见即使在经验丰富的代理人中也能在稳态下产生巨大影响。我们认为，这些偏见尤其可能对发展领域产生影响，因为贫困的核心特征——接近生存线、高波动性、市场失灵、正式制度薄弱以及对社会关系的依赖——放大了心理约束的影响。我们围绕一组核心的心理构念来组织我们的综述：自我控制、认知约束、自我信念、心理健康和社会规范。对于每个构念，我们着重指出哪些地方仅有概念验证，哪些地方有证据表明产生了有意义的影响，以及由此对未来研究产生的启示。我们还强调了社会资本在哪些方面可以用来减轻缺失市场的影响。迄今为止的实地研究在记录心理机制如何影响行为和决策方面仅触及了表面，未来的工作仍有很大空间来确定这些约束是否在塑造贫困方面发挥着首要作用。
