The Response of Debtors to Rate Changes

债务人对利率变化的反应

Andreas Fuster, Virginia Gianinazzi, Andreas Hackethal, Philip Schnorpfeil, Michael Weber

Abstract

How borrowers respond to future changes in the interest rate on their debt matters for the transmission of monetary policy and for household financial stability. Combining bank data, a letter RCT, and a survey, we study this question in the context of the German mortgage market, where since 2022 borrowers have faced high interest rates when their rate fixation period ends. We find that borrower actions substantially reduce the impact of higher rates on monthly payments. Survey responses corroborate high informedness and a strong propensity to prepare for rate changes. The letter intervention does not affect rate beliefs but increases awareness of available options and refinancing among borrowers close to expiration of their rate fixation.

中文摘要

借款人如何应对其债务未来利率的变化，对于货币政策的传导和家庭财务稳定性至关重要。结合银行数据、一项信件随机对照试验和一项调查，我们在德国抵押贷款市场的背景下研究了这一问题。自2022年以来，德国借款人在其利率固定期结束时面临着高利率。我们发现，借款人的行为显著降低了较高利率对月供的影响。调查回复证实了借款人知情程度高，并且有为利率变化做准备的强烈倾向。信件干预并未影响利率信念，但提高了临近利率固定期结束的借款人对可用选项和再融资的认识。

No. 36论文详情NBER w34751

Industrial Activity, State Capacity, and Deforestation: Evidence from Brazil

工业活动、国家能力与森林砍伐：来自巴西的证据

Daniel Da Mata, Mario Dotta, Edson R. Severnini

Abstract

Does industrial activity drive deforestation and land degradation, and can limited state capacity be overcome to decouple economic growth from environmental harm? We examine these questions in the context of slaughterhouse plant openings in Brazil from 1994 to 2019. Guided by a simple conceptual framework and using a staggered difference-in-differences approach, we show that plant openings increase livestock production while reducing forest cover and degrading pastureland. However, following the introduction of legally enforceable, incentive-compatible agreements between slaughterhouses and federal prosecutors—which penalize purchases of livestock from illegally deforested areas but act as a green certification mechanism—plant openings increase productivity without driving deforestation. Our findings suggest that tying firm performance to environmental goals through market-aligned legal mechanisms can generate economic and environmental gains at low cost to the government.

中文摘要

工业活动是否会导致森林砍伐和土地退化，能否克服有限的国家能力以实现经济增长与环境损害脱钩？我们在1994年至2019年巴西屠宰场开工的背景下考察了这些问题。在一个简单概念框架的指导下，并采用交错双重差分法，我们表明屠宰场开工增加了畜牧业产量，同时减少了森林覆盖并使牧场退化。然而，在屠宰场与联邦检察官之间引入具有法律约束力且激励相容的协议后——该协议惩罚从非法砍伐区域购买牲畜的行为，但作为一种绿色认证机制——屠宰场开工在未导致森林砍伐的情况下提高了生产率。我们的研究结果表明，通过市场导向的法律机制将企业绩效与环境目标挂钩，能够以较低的政府成本实现经济和环境收益。

No. 37论文详情NBER w34750

Effective and Scalable Programs to Facilitate Labor Market Transitions for Women in Technology

促进女性向技术行业劳动力市场转型的有效且可扩展的项目

Susan Athey, Emil Palikot

Abstract

We evaluate two interventions facilitating technology-sector transitions for women in Poland: Mentoring, focused on expanding professional networks, and Challenges, focused on building credible skill signals. Randomizing oversubscribed admissions, we find both programs substantially increase technology employment at twelve months-by 15 percentage points for Mentoring and 11 p.p. for Challenges. The distinct mechanisms through which the programs operate translate to heterogeneous treatment effects across geography, career stage, and baseline credentials. These differential effects create scope for improved allocation: algorithmic targeting across programs outperforms random assignment by 86% and outperforms experts' selection into Mentoring by 11%.

中文摘要

我们评估了在波兰促进女性向技术行业转型的两项干预措施：侧重于扩展职业网络的“导师制”，以及侧重于建立可信技能信号的“挑战赛”。通过对超额申请的录取进行随机化，我们发现这两个项目在十二个月后都显著增加了技术行业的就业——导师制提高了15个百分点，挑战赛提高了11个百分点。这些项目运作的不同机制转化为在地理位置、职业阶段和初始资质方面的异质性处理效应。这些差异效应为改进分配创造了空间：跨项目的算法目标分配比随机分配的效果高出86%，并且比专家选择进入导师制的效果高出11%。

No. 38论文详情NBER w34749

Understanding Latin America’s Fertility Decline: Age, Education, and Cohort Dynamics

理解拉丁美洲的生育率下降：年龄、教育与队列动态

Milagros Onofri, Inés Berniell, Raquel Fernández, Azul Menduiña

Abstract

This paper examines the sharp decline in fertility across Latin America using both period and cohort measures. Combining Vital Statistics, Census microdata, and UN population data, we decompose changes in fertility by age, education, and joint age–education groups. We show that the decline in period fertility between 2000 and 2022 is driven primarily by reductions in within-group birth rates rather than by changes in population composition, with the largest contributions coming from younger and less-educated women. Comparing the cohort born in the mid 1950s and the one born in the mid 1970s, we find that the decline in completed fertility reflects not only delayed childbearing but also substantial reductions in the average number of children per woman. This is driven primarily by lower fertility among mothers rather than by rising childlessness. Our findings provide new evidence on the nature of Latin America’s transition to below-replacement fertility and highlight several open questions for future research.

中文摘要

本文使用时期和队列两种度量指标，考察了拉丁美洲生育率的急剧下降。结合生命统计数据、人口普查微观数据和联合国人口数据，我们按年龄、教育程度以及年龄-教育联合组别分解了生育率的变化。我们表明，2000年至2022年间时期生育率的下降主要是由组内生育率的降低驱动的，而非人口构成的变化，其中年轻和受教育程度较低的女性贡献最大。比较20世纪50年代中期出生的队列和20世纪70年代中期出生的队列，我们发现，完成生育率的下降不仅反映了生育延迟，还反映了每位妇女平均子女数量的实质性减少。这主要是由母亲生育率降低而非无子女率上升驱动的。我们的发现为拉丁美洲向低于更替水平生育率转变的性质提供了新证据，并强调了未来研究的若干开放性问题。

No. 39论文详情NBER w34748

A Macroeconomic Perspective on Stock Market Valuation Ratios

股票市场估值比率的宏观经济学视角

Andrew Atkeson, Jonathan Heathcote, Fabrizio Perri

Abstract

Traditional valuation metrics for the U.S. stock market based on a comparison of the aggregate market value of U.S. corporations to measures of dividends, earnings, output, and the replacement cost of measured capital have been above historical norms for the past 25–30 years. Will they return to their historical means? We use macroeconomic data to argue that the observed decline in labor’s share of corporate output in conjunction with relatively weak corporate investment mechanically generates a persistent rise in the ratio of corporate valuation relative to corporate earnings, even absent any changes in expected returns or growth rates.

中文摘要

基于美国公司总市值与股息、盈利、产出以及已测资本重置成本等指标的比较，美国股市的传统估值指标在过去25至30年间一直高于历史常态。这些指标会回归历史均值吗？我们利用宏观经济数据论证，观察到的企业产出中劳动份额的下降，加上相对疲弱的企业投资，即使在预期回报率或增长率没有任何变化的情况下，也会机械地导致企业估值相对于企业盈利的比率持续上升。

No. 40论文详情NBER w34747

A Few Bad Apples? Academic Dishonesty, Political Selection, and Institutional Performance in China

几颗老鼠屎坏了一锅汤？学术不端、政治选拔与中国制度绩效

Zhuang Liu, Wenwei Peng, Shaoda Wang

Abstract

Honesty is perceived as fundamental to societal functioning, motivating education systems worldwide to enforce strict oversight and heavy penalties for dishonest behavior. Yet much academic misconduct remains unexposed, and its broader consequences are further obscured by the sorting of individuals into careers based on probity. Applying advanced plagiarism-detection algorithms to half a million publicly available graduate dissertations in China, we uncover hidden misconduct and validate it against incentivized measures of honesty. Linking plagiarism records to rich administrative data, we document four main findings. First, plagiarism is pervasive and predicts adverse political selection: plagiarists are more likely to enter and advance in the public sector. Second, plagiarists perform worse when holding power: focusing on the judiciary and exploiting quasi-random case assignments, we find that judges with plagiarism histories issue more preferential rulings and attract a greater number of appeals — effects partly mitigated by trial livestreaming. Third, plagiarizing judges generate spillovers onto other judges and lawyers. Fourth, exploiting the staggered adoption of detection tools, we demonstrate that enforcing academic integrity leads to modest improvements in future professional conduct.

中文摘要

诚实被视为社会运作的基础，这促使世界各地的教育系统对不诚实行为实施严格的监督和严厉的惩罚。然而，许多学术不端行为仍未曝光，其更广泛的后果又因个人根据诚信度选择职业而进一步被掩盖。我们将先进的剽窃检测算法应用于中国公开的五十万份研究生毕业论文，发现了隐藏的不端行为，并基于激励相容的诚实度量指标对其进行了验证。通过将剽窃记录与丰富的行政数据相关联，我们记录了四个主要发现。首先，剽窃行为普遍存在，并预示着不利的政治选拔：剽窃者更有可能进入公共部门并在其中晋升。其次，剽窃者在掌权时表现更差：聚焦司法部门并利用准随机案件分配，我们发现，有剽窃历史的法官会发布更多偏袒性裁决，并吸引更多的上诉——这些影响部分被庭审直播所缓解。第三，剽窃法官会对其他法官和律师产生溢出效应。第四，利用检测工具的分阶段采用，我们证明，执行学术诚信会带来未来职业行为的适度改善。

No. 41论文详情NBER w34746

Scaling Sustainable Investing in Emerging and Developing Economies: Frictions and Opportunities

在新兴和发展中经济体扩大可持续投资：摩擦与机遇

Caroline Flammer, Thomas Giroux, Geoffrey Heal

Abstract

Mobilizing private capital at scale is critical for financing sustainable development, particularly in emerging and developing economies (EMDEs), where capital is most needed. We conduct a global survey of senior investment decision-makers across a broad spectrum of capital providers, including asset managers, pension and sovereign wealth funds, development finance institutions, philanthropic investors, and others. The survey provides novel evidence on investors’ risk-return expectations, risk perceptions, and investment practices in EMDEs and in blended finance structures. We document four main findings. First, conditional on investor type, return expectations in EMDEs are comparable to those in developed markets, suggesting that categorical exclusions of EMDE assets might be inefficient. Second, investors’ dominant risk perceptions—particularly currency and political risks—are poorly aligned with the de-risking tools commonly employed in blended finance. Third, prevailing approaches to evaluating blended finance rely on both input- and outcome-based metrics, yet with limited measurement of financial and impact additionality. Fourth, our results highlight organizational and informational frictions, rather than unattractive financial fundamentals, as key barriers to scaling sustainable investing in EMDEs.

中文摘要

大规模调动私人资本对于为可持续发展融资至关重要，尤其是在最需要资本的新兴和发展中经济体。我们对广泛的资本提供者（包括资产管理公司、养老基金和主权财富基金、开发金融机构、慈善投资者等）中的高级投资决策者进行了一项全球调查。该调查提供了关于投资者在新兴和发展中经济体以及混合融资结构中的风险收益预期、风险认知和投资实践的新证据。我们记录了四个主要发现。首先，在给定投资者类型的情况下，新兴和发展中经济体的收益预期与发达市场相当，这表明对新兴和发展中经济体资产的类别性排除可能是低效的。其次，投资者主要的风险认知——尤其是货币风险和政治风险——与混合融资中常用的去风险工具匹配度较差。第三，评估混合融资的现行方法依赖于基于投入和基于结果的指标，但对财务和影响力附加性的衡量有限。第四，我们的结果强调，组织和信息方面的摩擦，而非不具吸引力的财务基本面，是在新兴和发展中经济体扩大可持续投资的关键障碍。

No. 42论文详情NBER w34745

Behavioral Economics of AI: LLM Biases and Corrections

人工智能的行为经济学：大语言模型的偏差与纠正

Pietro Bini, Lin William Cong, Xing Huang, Lawrence J. Jin

Abstract

Do generative AI models, particularly large language models (LLMs), exhibit systematic behavioral biases in economic and financial decisions? If so, how can these biases be mitigated? Drawing on the cognitive psychology and experimental economics literatures, we conduct the most comprehensive set of experiments to date—originally designed to document human biases—on prominent LLM families across model versions and scales. We document systematic patterns in LLM behavior. In preference-based tasks, responses become more human-like as models become more advanced or larger, while in belief-based tasks, advanced large-scale models frequently generate rational responses. Prompting LLMs to make rational decisions reduces biases.

中文摘要

生成式人工智能模型，特别是大语言模型，在经济和金融决策中是否会表现出系统性的行为偏差？如果是，这些偏差如何能被减轻？借鉴认知心理学和实验经济学的文献，我们对不同模型版本和规模的主要大语言模型家族进行了迄今为止最全面的实验——这些实验最初是为记录人类偏差而设计的。我们记录了大语言模型行为中的系统性模式。在基于偏好的任务中，随着模型变得更先进或更大，其反应变得更像人类；而在基于信念的任务中，先进的大规模模型经常产生理性的反应。提示大语言模型做出理性决策可以减少偏差。

No. 43论文详情NBER w34744

The United States as an Active Industrial Policy Nation

作为积极产业政策国家的美国

Jiandong Ju, Yuankun Li, Shang-Jin Wei

Abstract

We document and characterize a new history of U.S. federal-level industrial policies by scanning all 12,167 Congressional Acts and 6,030 Presidential Orders from 1973 through 2022. We find several interesting patterns. First, contrary to a common perception, the United States has always been an active industrial policy nation throughout the period, regardless of which party is in power, with 5.4 laws and 3.4 Presidential Orders per year on average containing new industrial policies. Second, we identify roughly 300% more instances of industrial policies than those in the Global Trade Alert (GTA) database during 2008-2022, despite using essentially the same definition. Third, industrial policies in practice are as likely to be justified by national security as by economic competitiveness. Fourth, many U.S. industrial policies incorporate design features that help mitigate potential drawbacks, such as explicit expiration dates and pilot programs for emerging technologies. Finally, based on stock market reactions and firm performance, the identified policies are recognized as economically significant in shifting resource allocations.

中文摘要

我们通过扫描1973年至2022年间所有12,167项国会法案和6,030项总统行政命令，记录并描述了美国联邦层面产业政策的新历史。我们发现了一些有趣的模式。首先，与普遍看法相反，在整个时期内，无论哪个政党执政，美国一直是一个积极的产业政策国家，平均每年有5.4项法律和3.4项总统行政命令包含新的产业政策。其次，尽管使用了基本相同的定义，我们在2008-2022年间识别出的产业政策实例比全球贸易预警数据库中的多出约300%。第三，实践中，产业政策以国家安全为由进行正当化的可能性与以经济竞争力为由进行正当化的可能性相当。第四，许多美国产业政策包含了有助于减轻潜在缺陷的设计特征，例如明确的到期日期和针对新兴技术的试点项目。最后，基于股市反应和企业绩效，所识别的政策被认为在改变资源配置方面具有经济上的显著性。

No. 44论文详情NBER w34743

Consumer Demand and Market Competition with Time-Intensive Goods

时间密集型商品的消费者需求与市场竞争

Joseph Goodman, Lancelot Henry de Frahan, Justin E. Holz, John A. List, Niall MacMenamin, Evan C. McKay, Magne Mogstad, Sally Sadoff, Hal Sider

Abstract

We leverage Becker’s time allocation theory to examine consumer demand and market competition for time-intensive goods. The Beckerian model predicts higher diversion ratios for goods with substantial time shares and those with high time costs relative to monetary prices. Applying this model to data from two field experiments, we analyze demand for Facebook and Instagram, focusing on substitution patterns across online activities and offline time use. Our findings indicate that users exhibit low elasticity to ad load, the primary user cost, and that time shares and time costs significantly influence diversion ratios. We explore the implications for user costs and benefits on these platforms and assess the potential impact of a Federal Trade Commission-proposed de-merger of Facebook and Instagram.

中文摘要

我们利用贝克尔的时间分配理论来研究时间密集型商品的消费者需求和市场竞争。贝克尔模型预测，对于具有显著时间份额的商品以及时间成本相对于货币价格较高的商品，其转移率更高。将该模型应用于来自两个现场实验的数据，我们分析了Facebook和Instagram的需求，重点关注在线活动之间以及线下时间使用的替代模式。我们的发现表明，用户对广告负载（主要的用户成本）的弹性较低，并且时间份额和时间成本显著影响转移率。我们探讨了这些平台上用户成本和收益的含义，并评估了联邦贸易委员会提议的Facebook和Instagram分拆的潜在影响。

No. 45论文详情NBER w34742

The Dynamics of Retail Deposit Balances

零售存款余额的动态变化

Bronson Argyle, Benjamin Iverson, Jason D. Kotter, Taylor D. Nadauld, Christopher Palmer

Abstract

We investigate the dynamics of household deposits using account-level data from 12 million accounts across 154 U.S. credit unions. Significant skewness in the retail deposit distribution–with 10% of depositors controlling 70% of total deposits–means large-balance accounts drive aggregate retail deposit flows. On average, high-balance accounts become large after significant one-time inflows and are more likely to experience large, idiosyncratic drawdowns. Unlike low-balance households, high-balance retail depositors are not sensitive to interest rate shocks. Additional evidence suggests that overall retail deposit stickiness is driven by high-balance accounts that are used as medium-run liquidity stores rather than for interest income.

中文摘要

我们利用来自美国154家信用合作社的1200万个账户的账户级数据，研究了家庭存款的动态变化。零售存款分布存在显著偏态——10%的储户控制了70%的总存款——这意味着大额账户驱动了总体零售存款流动。平均而言，高余额账户在经历显著的一次性资金流入后变得庞大，并且更有可能经历大规模、特异性的资金减少。与低余额家庭不同，高余额零售储户对利率冲击不敏感。额外证据表明，总体零售存款的粘性是由那些被用作中期流动性储存而非获取利息收入的高余额账户驱动的。

No. 46论文详情NBER w34741

The Demand for Grandchildren: Children as Family Public Goods and Implications for Cooperative Bargaining

对孙辈的需求：作为家庭公共品的子女及其对合作博弈的启示

Janice Compton, Robert A. Pollak

Abstract

The title says it all. Well, almost all. To economists, the situation suggests bargaining between parents and grandparents, where the grandparents can "bribe" the parents to have more children or to have children sooner than they otherwise would. Because cash transfers seem inappropriate, bribes are likely to take the form of promises of child care or down payments on houses. Coasian bargaining or, more generally, cooperative bargaining models with their explicit assumption of Pareto efficiency offer accessible off-the shelf models. Larger family size (e.g., the participation of both pairs of grandparents) and family complexity (e.g., resulting from divorce and repartnering in the parents' generation or the grandparents' generation) threaten the assumption of zero or low transaction costs. Low transaction costs, explicit in the Coasian analysis and implicit in cooperative game theory's assumption of Pareto efficiency, play a crucial role. The generalization of family economics from the analysis of bargaining between spouses to include family members beyond the household will at some point require replacing Coasian and cooperative bargaining with models of noncooperative bargaining.

中文摘要

标题说明了一切。嗯，几乎是一切。对经济学家而言，这种情况暗示了父母和祖父母之间的博弈，祖父母可以“贿赂”父母，让他们生育更多孩子或比原本更早生育孩子。由于现金转移似乎不合适，贿赂很可能采取承诺提供育儿服务或支付房屋首付的形式。科斯式谈判，或者更一般地，带有明确帕累托效率假设的合作博弈模型，提供了现成的现成模型。更大的家庭规模（例如，双方祖父母的参与）和家庭复杂性（例如，由于父母一代或祖父母一代的离婚和再婚导致）威胁到零或低交易成本的假设。低交易成本在科斯分析中是明确的，在合作博弈论的帕累托效率假设中是隐含的，它起着关键作用。将家庭经济学从分析配偶间的博弈推广到包括家庭以外的成员，在某个阶段将需要用非合作博弈模型取代科斯式谈判和合作博弈。

No. 47论文详情NBER w34740

Current Account Deficits and the Welfare of Future Generations

经常账户赤字与未来世代的福利

Christopher Phelan

Abstract

This paper explores the effects of one nation's taxation of consumption on the welfare of future generations of other countries. To do this, it presents an otherwise standard one-good, two-country optimal growth model with free capital markets, but where each date represents the lifetime of a generation which cares not only about its own consumption and leisure, but also that of its descendants.\nRelative to a no tax benchmark, a policy of one country taxing consumption of its initial generations has ambiguous welfare effects for future generations of the other country, as long as those future generations are not too far in the future. Higher initial savings in the first country raises capital levels, and thus wages, in both countries, raising welfare of future generations in the second country, but also induces lower bequests in the second country, lowering the welfare of its future generations. In the long run, or for generations born near the steady state, the welfare effects of the first country inducing lower consumption of its initial generations are unambiguous: future generations of the second country are made worse off. Households born in the second country will regret that their ancestors allowed such policy-induced intertemporal trade.

中文摘要

本文探讨了一国对消费征税对其他国家未来世代福利的影响。为此，它提出了一个在其他方面标准的单商品、两国最优增长模型，该模型具有自由资本市场，但每个日期代表一代人的生命周期，这代人不仅关心自己的消费和闲暇，也关心其后代的消费和闲暇。

No. 48论文详情NBER w34739

Is the Environmental Exposure Gap Shrinking? Evidence from an Extreme Multi-exposure Index

环境暴露差距在缩小吗？来自极端多重暴露指数的证据

Glenn Sheriff, Danae Hernandez-Cortes, TC Chakraborty, Theresa DeConcini

Abstract

Demographic disparities in exposure to various sources of environmental stress are well documented. While specific stressors are linked to adverse health outcomes, there is uncertainty about how they interact. A first step towards evaluating these joint impacts is to understand the degree to which the same individuals are exposed to extreme simultaneous exposure to each stressor. Here, we adapt the Alkire-Foster multi-dimensional poverty measure to rank exposures to multi-dimensional environmental harm in a way that accounts for the frequency, breadth, and severity of exposure among the extremely exposed. This measure can be used to normatively compare distributions of extreme simultaneous exposure for a given group both across time and in comparison with other groups. We use publicly-available data on air toxics, PM2.5, and land surface temperature to identify trends in the multi-exposure index for socio-demographic groups based on race/ethnicity and poverty status for 168 U.S. cities. Controlling for city-characteristics, we find persistent, yet narrowing, multi-exposure gaps on the basis of race/ethnicity between people of color (POC) and non-Hispanic White. Within each group, individuals in households above the poverty line fare better than those below, but above-poverty POC have similar multi-exposure to below-poverty non-Hispanic White.

中文摘要

不同人口群体在暴露于各种环境压力源方面的差异已有充分记录。虽然特定的压力源与不良健康结果相关，但关于它们如何相互作用仍存在不确定性。评估这些联合影响的第一步是了解同一个人是否同时极端暴露于每种压力源。在此，我们调整了Alkire-Foster多维贫困衡量方法，以对多维环境危害的暴露进行排序，这种方式考虑了极端暴露者中暴露的频率、广度和严重程度。该衡量方法可用于在规范意义上比较特定群体在时间上以及与其他群体相比的极端同时暴露分布。我们使用关于空气毒物、PM2.5和地表温度的公开数据，识别了美国168个城市中基于种族/民族和贫困状况的社会人口群体的多重暴露指数趋势。在控制城市特征的情况下，我们发现有色人种与非西班牙裔白人之间基于种族/民族的多重暴露差距持续存在，但正在缩小。在每个群体内部，生活在贫困线以上家庭的个人比贫困线以下的个人状况更好，但处于贫困线以上的有色人种的多重暴露水平与处于贫困线以下的非西班牙裔白人相似。

No. 49论文详情NBER w34738

The Informational Role of Emission Markets: Prices vs Quantities with Dispersed Information About Externalities

排放市场的信息角色：外部性信息分散下的价格与数量

Derek Lemoine

Abstract

I study asymmetric information about the social cost of an externality, as opposed to asymmetric information about private costs of abatement. I show that quantity regulation with bankable permits has an informational advantage because the permit market aggregates dispersed information about social costs. It has the disadvantage of making private costs more uncertain ex ante. I analytically derive the expression for the (dis)advantage of prices over quantities in this setting. I show that a quantity policy can dominate a price policy for any slope of marginal private costs and always dominates when marginal private costs are sufficiently flat.

中文摘要

我研究了关于外部性社会成本的不对称信息，这与关于私人减排成本的不对称信息形成对比。我证明，具有可储存配额的数量监管具有信息优势，因为配额市场汇集了关于社会成本的分散信息。其劣势在于，它使私人成本在事前更加不确定。我解析推导了在此设定下价格相对于数量的（劣势）优势表达式。我证明，对于任何斜率的边际私人成本，数量政策都可能优于价格政策，并且当边际私人成本足够平坦时，数量政策始终占优。

No. 50论文详情NBER w34737

Measuring the Growth of Skills

衡量技能的增长

James J. Heckman, Haihan Tian, Zijian Zhang, Jin Zhou

Abstract

This paper discusses a fundamental problem in measuring the growth of knowledge and comparing the skills of people. New skills emerge that are not just more of the previously acquired skills. Psychometric convention forces these skills into arbitrarily constructed scales, which can severely distort measurement. To formally address this problem, we measure skills using a novel measurement scheme, estimate a stochastic learning process and reject the common scale assumption across levels for language and cognitive skills. Furthermore, we estimate dynamic complementarity without imposing arbitrary scales for skills.

中文摘要

本文讨论了衡量知识增长和比较人们技能时的一个基本问题。新的技能会出现，它们不仅仅是先前获得技能的更多积累。心理测量学的惯例将这些技能强行纳入任意构建的量表，这可能会严重扭曲测量结果。为了正式解决这个问题，我们使用一种新颖的测量方案来衡量技能，估计一个随机学习过程，并拒绝了语言和认知技能在不同水平上存在共同量表的假设。此外，我们在没有对技能施加任意量表的情况下估计了动态互补性。

No. 51论文详情NBER w34736

College Major Choice, Payoffs, and Gender Gaps

大学专业选择、回报与性别差距

Christopher Campos, Pablo Muñoz, Alonso Bucarey, Dante Contreras

Abstract

This paper studies how college major choices shape earnings and fertility outcomes. Using administrative data that link students' preferences, random assignment to majors, and post-college outcomes, we estimate the causal pecuniary and non-pecuniary returns to different fields of study. We document substantial heterogeneity in these returns across majors and show that such variation helps explain gender gaps in labor market outcomes: women place greater weight on balancing career and family in their major choices, and these preference differences account for about 30% of the gender earnings gap among college graduates. Last, we use our causal estimates to evaluate the effects of counterfactual assignment rules that target representation gaps in settings with centralized assignment systems. We find that gender quotas in high-return fields can significantly reduce representation and earnings gaps with minimal impacts on efficiency and aggregate fertility.

中文摘要

本文研究了大学专业选择如何塑造收入和生育结果。利用将学生的偏好、专业随机分配以及毕业后的结果联系起来的行政数据，我们估算了不同研究领域的因果性金钱和非金钱回报。我们记录了这些回报在不同专业之间存在显著的异质性，并表明这种差异有助于解释劳动力市场结果中的性别差距：女性在选择专业时更重视平衡职业与家庭，这些偏好差异解释了大学毕业生中约30%的性别收入差距。最后，我们利用因果估计来评估反事实分配规则的效果，这些规则旨在针对具有集中分配系统的环境中的代表性差距。我们发现，在高回报领域实施性别配额可以在对效率和总体生育率影响最小的情况下，显著减少代表性和收入差距。

No. 52论文详情NBER w34735

Economic Development and the Environment

经济发展与环境

B. Kelsey Jack, Nicholas Ryan

Abstract

Economic development relies on and transforms the environment. The transformation is evident in the poor environmental quality in many developing countries. For example, air quality in Southeast Asia is three times worse than in the United States, in sub-Saharan Africa four times worse and in South Asia more than six times worse. We model how environmental quality affects health, productivity and well-being and how individuals privately adapt to environmental hazards. We also model how collective action and formal regulation contribute to environmental quality. We draw three main findings from a review of empirical research on these mechanisms. First, individual adaptation to environmental hazards is both inadequate as a remedy and inefficiently low. Second, collective action, without the state, to manage resources or address externalities has been outstripped by the scale of environmental problems. Third, state action through formal regulation works better than it looks. Many formal regulations are coarse, poorly targeted and inefficient, but nonetheless yield benefits in excess of their costs.

中文摘要

经济发展依赖并改变着环境。这种转变在许多发展中国家糟糕的环境质量中显而易见。例如，东南亚的空气质量比美国差三倍，撒哈拉以南非洲差四倍，南亚则差六倍以上。我们模拟了环境质量如何影响健康、生产力和福祉，以及个人如何私下适应环境危害。我们还模拟了集体行动和正式监管如何促进环境质量。我们从对这些机制的实证研究回顾中得出三个主要发现。首先，个人对环境危害的适应既不足以作为补救措施，其效率也低得令人担忧。其次，在没有国家参与的情况下，为管理资源或解决外部性而采取的集体行动已被环境问题的规模所超越。第三，通过正式监管的国家行动效果比表面看起来要好。许多正式监管是粗略的、针对性差且效率低下的，但尽管如此，其产生的收益仍超过了成本。

No. 53论文详情NBER w34734

War and Democratic Backsliding

战争与民主倒退

Efraim Benmelech, Joao Monteiro

Abstract

We provide the first global, long-run evidence on how war reshapes democratic institutions. Using data on all conflicts since 1948, we show that the onset of conflict causes a large and persistent decline in democracy: institutions weaken immediately, continue to erode for nearly a decade, and do not recover. Yet this deterioration is highly selective. It appears only in first-time conflicts, intrastate wars, highly fractionalized societies, and conflicts that governments win. The decline operates through political channels – media censorship, judicial purges, curtailed civil liberties, irregular leadership turnover, and constitutional suspensions - rather than through any functional requirement of war-making. Autocratization does not increase the probability of victory, and institutional instability reduces it. Taken together, the findings show that war does not require autocracy; it enables executives to expand their authority and implement institutional changes that would be difficult to enact in peacetime.

中文摘要

我们提供了首个关于战争如何重塑民主制度的全球性长期证据。利用自1948年以来所有冲突的数据，我们表明冲突的爆发会导致民主程度大幅且持续地下降：制度立即削弱，持续恶化近十年，并且无法恢复。然而，这种恶化具有高度选择性。它仅出现在首次冲突、国家内部战争、高度分裂的社会以及政府获胜的冲突中。这种衰退通过政治渠道运作——媒体审查、司法清洗、公民自由受限、非常规领导层更迭和宪法暂停——而不是通过任何战争所需的职能要求。威权化并未增加获胜的概率，而制度不稳定则降低了获胜概率。综合来看，这些发现表明，战争并不需要独裁；它使行政长官能够扩大其权力，并实施在和平时期难以推行的制度变革。

No. 54论文详情NBER w34733

Does Generative AI Crowd Out Human Creators? Evidence from Pixiv

生成式人工智能会排挤人类创作者吗？来自Pixiv的证据

Sueyoul Kim, Ginger Zhe Jin, Eungik Lee

Abstract

Using a comprehensive dataset of posts from a major platform for anime- and manga-style artwork, we study the impact of the launch of a prominent text-to-image generative AI. Focusing on the majority of incumbent creators who do not adopt AI as a primary tool, we show that the AI launch led to a significant decline in post uploads by illustrators, whereas comic artists were less affected, reflecting the need for tight stylistic alignment across sequential images in comics. We present empirical evidence for two underlying mechanisms. First, illustration posts experience a loss of viewer attention, measured by bookmarks, following the AI launch, which can significantly harm creators’ business models. Second, direct competition from AI-generated content plays an important role: illustrators working on intellectual properties (IPs, such as Pokémon) that are more heavily invaded by AI reduce their uploads disproportionately more. We further examine creators’ responses and show that illustrators with greater exposure to AI avoid using tags favored by AI-generated content after the AI launch and broaden the range of IPs they work on, consistent with a risk-hedging response to AI invasion.

中文摘要

利用来自一个主要的动漫和漫画风格艺术作品平台的综合帖子数据集，我们研究了著名的文生图生成式人工智能发布的影响。聚焦于大多数未将人工智能作为主要工具的现有创作者，我们表明，人工智能的发布导致插画师的帖子上传量显著下降，而漫画艺术家受到的影响较小，这反映了漫画中跨连续图像需要紧密的风格一致性。我们为两个潜在机制提供了实证证据。首先，插画帖子在人工智能发布后经历了观众注意力（以书签衡量）的流失，这会严重损害创作者的商业模式。其次，来自人工智能生成内容的直接竞争起着重要作用：在那些被人工智能入侵更严重的知识产权（IP，例如宝可梦）上工作的插画师，其上传量减少得不成比例地多。我们进一步考察了创作者的回应，并表明，接触人工智能更多的插画师在人工智能发布后会避免使用人工智能生成内容偏好的标签，并拓宽他们工作的知识产权范围，这与应对人工智能入侵的风险对冲反应一致。

No. 55论文详情NBER w34732

The Twenty-four Hour Economy or Rolled-up Sidewalks: Trends in Work Timing and Their Causes

24小时经济还是收摊的人行道：工作时间安排的趋势及其原因

Jeff Biddle, Daniel S. Hamermesh

Abstract

We demonstrate nearly steady trends from 1973-2023 in the U.S. in the timing of when people work for pay, away from evening and night hours toward “usual” daytime hours. Much of the trend is related to increased real incomes, with rising educational attainment, the changing composition of the (declining) manufacturing industry, and the increased wage premium for undesirable work times—evenings and nights—that we document accounting for the rest. The trend exists in all major industries except retail, in which changes in technology biased work away from daytime hours. It was accelerated by the sharp increase in telework that occurred after the Covid pandemic, an increase that was especially concentrated during daytime hours. While we observe the same phenomenon in France from 1966 to 2010, we do not in the U.K. from 1974-2015, arguably because of the very sharp decline in unionization in the U.K. and the changes in retailing.

中文摘要

我们展示了1973年至2023年间美国人们从事有偿工作的时间安排几乎稳定的趋势，即从晚间和夜间时段转向“通常的”白天时段。这一趋势很大程度上与实际收入增加有关，而教育程度的提高、（衰退的）制造业的构成变化以及我们所记录的不受欢迎工作时间（晚间和夜间）工资溢价的上升则解释了其余部分。这一趋势存在于除零售业外的所有主要行业中，在零售业中，技术变革使工作时间偏离了白天时段。新冠疫情后远程工作的急剧增加加速了这一趋势，这种增加尤其集中在白天时段。虽然我们在1966年至2010年的法国观察到了同样的现象，但在1974年至2015年的英国却没有，这可以说是因为英国工会化程度的急剧下降以及零售业的变化。

No. 56论文详情NBER w34731

Salience and the Elasticity of Taxable Income: Evidence from Top-bracket Tax Reforms

显著性与应税收入弹性：来自最高税率改革的证据

Xavier Dufour, Pierre-Carl Michaud, Michael G. Smart

Abstract

We estimate heterogeneous responses to top-bracket tax reforms using a triple-difference design that exploits variation in tax rate changes and the thresholds at which they apply. This strategy identifies behavioral responses even in the presence of unobservable shocks to the income distribution. Higher-income taxpayers respond more to top-rate changes, but our results indicate that this reflects the salience of the reforms—the larger mechanical change in average tax rates at higher incomes—rather than heterogeneity in substitution elasticities. We discuss implications for the revenue and distributional effects of top-bracket tax reforms.

中文摘要

我们利用一种三重差分设计来估计对最高税率改革的异质性反应，该设计利用了税率变化及其适用门槛的差异。这种策略即使在收入分配存在不可观测冲击的情况下也能识别出行为反应。较高收入的纳税人对最高税率变化的反应更大，但我们的结果表明，这反映了改革的显著性——在较高收入水平上平均税率有更大的机械性变化——而不是替代弹性的异质性。我们讨论了这对最高税率改革的收入和分配效应的影响。

No. 57论文详情NBER w34730

Technology and Economic Development

技术与经济发展

Daron Acemoglu, Ufuk Akcigit, Simon Johnson

Abstract

This chapter presents a tractable framework for the study of technology adoption and diffusion in the context of economic development. Firms in countries behind the world technology frontier can rapidly adopt new techniques from the world frontier. Lower absorptive capacity (because of weak education systems, poor management practices, or barriers to technology adoption), institutional distortions, mismatch between frontier technologies and the needs of firms in the country (i.e., “inappropriate technology”), and credit market frictions slow down technology adoption and cause the economy in question to have a greater distance to the frontier and thus lower income per capita—although the long-run growth rate of the country still remains equal to that of the frontier. This framework is extended to study the choice between innovation and imitation, as well as the role of selection for higher-productivity and higher-absorptive capacity firms during the process of economic development. We illustrate the main comparative statics of our framework with a number of correlations based on cross-country and firm-level data. The tractability of the framework makes it amenable to a range of additional extensions.

中文摘要

本章提出了一个易于处理的框架，用于研究经济发展背景下的技术采用与扩散。处于世界技术前沿之后国家的企业可以迅速从世界前沿采用新技术。较低的吸收能力（由于教育体系薄弱、管理实践不佳或技术采用障碍）、制度扭曲、前沿技术与国内企业需求之间的不匹配（即“不适当技术”），以及信贷市场摩擦，会减缓技术采用，并导致该经济体与前沿的距离更大，从而人均收入更低——尽管该国的长期增长率仍等于前沿国家的增长率。该框架被扩展用于研究创新与模仿之间的选择，以及经济发展过程中对高生产率和强吸收能力企业的筛选作用。我们利用基于跨国和企业层面数据的一系列相关性，说明了我们框架的主要比较静态分析结果。该框架的易处理性使其适用于一系列额外的扩展。

No Taxation Without Administration: Bringing The State Back Into The Public Finance Of Developing Countries

无行政，不征税：将国家带回发展中国家的公共财政研究

Anders Jensen, Jonathan L. Weigel

Abstract

The empirical economics literature on taxation in developing countries has centered on the importance of third-party information for enforcement. Yet, while surely a long-run objective, leveraging such information remains out of reach in many developing countries due to largely informal economies and low state capacity. This article examines an emerging complementary literature focused on strengthening the 'sinews' of state capacity: tax administration. We argue that reforms to the organizational structure, personnel management, and task management of tax authorities have potential to raise tax capacity in developing countries. We also argue that efforts to improve the state's legitimacy – popular acceptance of its right to tax – can increase capacity and may complement investments in tax administration. Our approach bridges a long-standing divide between how scholars in public finance and political economy approach tax capacity building in developing countries.

中文摘要

关于发展中国家税收的实证经济学文献一直集中于第三方信息对税收执法的重要性。然而，尽管这无疑是一个长期目标，但由于经济在很大程度上是非正规的且国家能力低下，在许多发展中国家利用此类信息仍然遥不可及。本文考察了一个新兴的补充性文献，该文献侧重于加强国家能力的“筋腱”：税收行政。我们认为，对税务机关的组织结构、人事管理和任务管理进行改革，有潜力提高发展中国家的税收能力。我们还认为，改善国家合法性——公众对其征税权的普遍接受——的努力可以提高税收能力，并可能补充对税收行政的投资。我们的方法弥合了公共财政和政治经济学学者在处理发展中国家税收能力建设问题上长期存在的分歧。

Global Trade, Tariff Uncertainty and the U.S. Dollar

全球贸易、关税不确定性与美元

Ṣebnem Kalemli-Özcan, Can Soylu, Muhammed A. Yildirim

Abstract

We analyze how tariff uncertainty affects exchange rates, motivated by the U.S. dollar’s depreciation after the 2025 tariff announcements. Standard macro-trade models predict that unilateral tariffs appreciate the implementing country’s currency, but we show this result can be overturned by policy uncertainty. We build a two-country general equilibrium model with risk-averse agents and segmented financial markets, where tariff volatility enters uncovered interest parity through a risk-premium wedge. Higher tariff uncertainty increases precautionary savings and risk premia, leading to immediate currency depreciation even as tariffs rise. Quantitatively, the model replicates the size and timing of the observed dollar depreciation episode dynamics.

中文摘要

我们分析了关税不确定性如何影响汇率，其动机源于2025年关税公告后美元的贬值。标准的宏观贸易模型预测，单边关税会使实施国的货币升值，但我们表明，这一结果可能因政策不确定性而被推翻。我们构建了一个包含风险厌恶代理人和分割金融市场的两国一般均衡模型，在该模型中，关税波动通过风险溢价楔子进入无抛补利率平价。更高的关税不确定性会增加预防性储蓄和风险溢价，导致即使在关税上升时货币也立即贬值。在数量上，该模型复制了所观察到的美元贬值事件动态的规模和时机。

No. 60论文详情NBER w34727

Rational Disagreement

理性分歧

Nabil Al-Najjar, Harald Uhlig

Abstract

We propose rational disagreement as a formal framework for analyzing seemingly irrational behavior that can persist despite the wide availability of objective information in a steady-state. Agents are rational in that they correctly anticipate the distribution of aggregate outcomes, yet disagree about which specific individuals perform better than others. Notably, the subjective belief of any individual may be objectively correct. \nWe illustrate the key concepts with a simple entry game. We show how unordered individual outcome distributions can be identified solely from aggregate statistics. We then characterize the resulting game, define its Nash equilibria, and develop a statistical test for the null hypothesis of agreement. Finally, we situate our framework within the broader literature on Bayesian games, behavioral biases, and the rational expectations hypothesis.

中文摘要

我们提出理性分歧作为一个正式框架，用于分析那些尽管在稳态下客观信息广泛可得却仍能持续存在的看似非理性的行为。代理人是理性的，因为他们正确预期了总体结果的分布，但对于哪些特定个体表现优于其他个体却存在分歧。值得注意的是，任何个体的主观信念在客观上可能是正确的。我们用一个简单的进入博弈来说明关键概念。我们展示了如何仅从总体统计数据中识别出无序的个体结果分布。然后，我们刻画了由此产生的博弈，定义了其纳什均衡，并开发了一个用于检验一致性原假设的统计检验。最后，我们将我们的框架置于关于贝叶斯博弈、行为偏差和理性预期假说的更广泛文献中。

No. 61论文详情NBER w34726

The Contribution of College Majors to Gender and Racial Earnings Differences

大学专业对性别和种族收入差异的贡献

Scott A. Imberman, Michael F. Lovenheim, Patrick Massey, Kevin M. Stange, Rodney J. Andrews

Abstract

Gender and racial/ethnic gaps in labor market earnings remain large, even among college-goers. Cross-gender and race/ethnic differences in choice of and returns to college major are potentially important contributors. Following Texas public high school graduates for up to 20 years through college and the labor market, we assess gender and racial differences in college major choices and the consequences of these choices. Women and underrepresented minorities are less likely than men, Whites, and Asians to major in high earning fields like business, economics, engineering, and computer science, however we also show that they experience lower returns to these majors. Differences in major-specific returns relative to liberal arts explain about one quarter of the gender, White-Black, and White-Hispanic (but not White-Asian) earnings gaps among four-year college students and become larger contributors to earnings gaps than differential major distributions as workers age. We present suggestive evidence that differences in occupation choices within field are a key driver of the differences in returns across groups. The work shines light on the roles that college major choice and returns by gender and race contribute to inequality.

中文摘要

劳动力市场收入中的性别和种族/民族差距仍然很大，即使在大学就读群体中也是如此。大学专业选择及其回报在性别和种族/民族间的差异可能是重要的促成因素。我们追踪德克萨斯州公立高中毕业生长达20年，贯穿大学和劳动力市场，评估了大学专业选择中的性别和种族差异以及这些选择的后果。女性和代表性不足的少数族裔比男性、白人和亚裔更不可能选择高收入领域，如商业、经济学、工程学和计算机科学，然而我们也表明，他们在这些专业中获得的回报较低。相对于文科，专业特定回报的差异解释了四年制大学生中约四分之一的性别、白人与黑人、白人与西班牙裔（但不包括白人与亚裔）的收入差距，并且随着工人年龄增长，这些差异对收入差距的贡献变得比专业分布差异更大。我们提出了暗示性证据，表明领域内职业选择的差异是导致不同群体间回报差异的关键驱动因素。这项工作揭示了大学专业选择以及按性别和种族划分的回报在不平等中所起的作用。

No. 62论文详情NBER w34725

Senior Migration, Local Economic Development and Spatial Concentration

老年人口迁移、地方经济发展与空间集中

Marco A. Badilla Maroto, Benjamin Faber, Antoine B. Levy, Mathilde Muñoz

Abstract

We document that migration flows upon retirement are predominantly from richer, more urban to poorer, more rural regions. In theory, the local economic implications of senior in-migration are ambiguous, while empirically there is little existing evidence on whether attracting mobile seniors can be an effective tool to promote economic development among lagging regions. We combine a unique collection of microdata from France with a new empirical strategy to fill this gap. We find that senior inflows have significant positive effects on the local economy over the course of a decade, including increases in the working-age population, total employment, GDP, average incomes, fiscal revenues and housing construction. These effects are particularly pronounced among initially poorer regions. They are accompanied by an increase in the share of services in the local economy, driven by employment growth in health, food services and retail sectors. Combining these estimates with observed region-to-region net migration flows, we find that mobile seniors have become a significant force for reducing the concentration of employment and GDP across regions.

中文摘要

我们记录了退休时的迁移流动主要从较富裕、更城市化的地区流向较贫穷、更乡村化的地区。理论上，老年人口迁入对地方经济的影响是不确定的，而实证上，关于吸引流动老年人是否能成为促进落后地区经济发展的有效工具，现有证据很少。我们结合来自法国的独特微观数据集合与一种新的实证策略来填补这一空白。我们发现，老年人口流入在十年期间对地方经济产生了显著的积极影响，包括劳动年龄人口、总就业、GDP、平均收入、财政收入和住房建设的增加。这些影响在最初较贫穷的地区尤为显著。它们伴随着服务业在地方经济中份额的增加，这由健康、餐饮服务和零售行业的就业增长所驱动。将这些估计值与观察到的地区间净迁移流量相结合，我们发现流动老年人已成为减少就业和GDP在地区间集中的重要力量。

No. 63论文详情NBER w34724

Missing Black Men? The Impact of Non-Reporting on Estimates of Labor Market Outcomes for Black Men

失踪的黑人男性？不报告对黑人男性劳动力市场结果估计的影响

Adrienne Sabety, Ariella K. Spitzer

Abstract

Adult Black men persistently do not report to household-based surveys, with demographers estimating non-reporting rates of 7-14% from 1970-2020. We derive a method to account for incomplete data and show that non-reporting rates are up to 5.5 percentage points (pp) larger than prior estimates, with significant heterogeneity by year. We then show that Black men at risk of incarceration drive non-reporting. We use state-year variation in incarceration rates to estimate that 35-83% of the incarcerated population would have been non-reporting if not incarcerated. Adjusting for previously uncorrected non-reporting shows that the Black-white gap in high-school completion is 20-39% (3.0-5.9 pp) larger, college attendance is 8-18% (3.1-6.1 pp) larger, and earnings is 10-20% (2.8-5.7 pp) larger. In contrast, the gap in employment is 4-8% (0.6-1.6 pp) smaller than previously thought.

中文摘要

成年黑人男性持续不参与以家庭为基础的调查，人口学家估计1970年至2020年间的不报告率为7-14%。我们推导出一种方法来解释不完整数据，并表明不报告率比之前的估计高出多达5.5个百分点，且在不同年份存在显著异质性。然后，我们表明面临监禁风险的黑人男性是不报告的主要驱动力。我们利用州-年层面的监禁率变化来估计，如果不被监禁，35-83%的监禁人口本会是不报告的。对先前未纠正的不报告进行调整后显示，黑人与白人在高中毕业率上的差距比之前认为的大20-39%（3.0-5.9个百分点），大学入学率差距大8-18%（3.1-6.1个百分点），收入差距大10-20%（2.8-5.7个百分点）。相比之下，就业率差距比之前认为的小4-8%（0.6-1.6个百分点）。

No. 64论文详情NBER w34723

Modeling the Labor Implications of the Energy Transition

模拟能源转型的劳动力影响

Marc A.C. Hafstead, Roberton C. Williams III

Abstract

The energy transition away from fossil fuels toward alternative energy sources will, like every significant economic transition, disrupt existing economic relationships and markets. Disruption in the labor market is of particular concern due to the distributional and political importance of energy jobs and the potential concentration of risks on workers in carbon-intensive sectors and regions that are particularly reliant on fossil-fuel industries. We look at modeling the labor implications of the energy transition. We outline a conceptual framework for analyzing the labor-market risks, focusing on obstacles to labor-market adjustments during the transition. We then review empirical research on such barriers to labor-market adjustments, with a focus on evidence that can inform modeling efforts. We also survey the literature on ex-ante modeling of the effects of the energy transition on labor markets, identifying both the challenges and opportunities for new research in this field.

中文摘要

从化石燃料向替代能源的能源转型，将像每一次重大的经济转型一样，扰乱现有的经济关系和市场。劳动力市场的扰乱尤其令人担忧，因为能源工作具有分配和政治重要性，且风险可能集中在碳密集型行业和特别依赖化石燃料产业的地区的工人身上。我们着眼于模拟能源转型的劳动力影响。我们概述了一个用于分析劳动力市场风险的概念框架，重点关注转型期间劳动力市场调整的障碍。然后，我们回顾了关于此类劳动力市场调整障碍的实证研究，重点关注能够为建模工作提供信息的证据。我们还调查了关于能源转型对劳动力市场影响的事前建模的文献，指出了该领域新研究面临的挑战和机遇。

No. 65论文详情NBER w34722

Speculative Growth and the AI "Bubble"

投机性增长与人工智能“泡沫”

Ricardo J. Caballero

Abstract

AI technology can generate speculative-growth equilibria. These are rational but fragile: elevated valuations support rapid capital accumulation, yet persist only as long as beliefs remain coordinated. Because AI capital is labor-like, it expands effective labor and dampens the normal decline in the marginal product of capital as the capital stock grows. The gains from this expansion accrue disproportionately to capitalists, whose saving rate rises with wealth, raising aggregate saving. Building on Caballero et al (2006), I show that these features generate a funding feedback—rising capitalist wealth lowers the required return—that can produce multiple equilibria. With intermediate adjustment costs, elevated valuations are the mechanism that sustains a transition toward a high-capital equilibrium; a loss of confidence can precipitate a self-fulfilling crash and reversal.

中文摘要

人工智能技术可以产生投机性增长均衡。这些均衡是理性的但也是脆弱的：高估值支撑着快速的资本积累，但只有当信念保持协调一致时才能持续存在。由于人工智能资本类似于劳动力，它扩大了有效劳动力，并抑制了随着资本存量增长而出现的资本边际产出的正常下降。这种扩张带来的收益不成比例地归于资本家，其储蓄率随财富增加而上升，从而提高了总储蓄。基于Caballero等人（2006）的研究，我表明这些特征会产生一种资金反馈——资本家财富上升降低了所需回报率——这可能导致多重均衡。在存在中等调整成本的情况下，高估值是维持向高资本均衡过渡的机制；信心的丧失可能引发自我实现的崩盘和逆转。

No. 66论文详情NBER w34721

Migration and the Making of the English Middle Class

移民与英国中产阶级的形成

Vasiliki Fouka, Theo Serlin

Abstract

When do people identify with their class? Evidence from social psychology shows that individuals are more likely to identify with a group if they are similar to its members. We study early 20th century Britain and show that regional cultural heterogeneity combined with internal migration influenced class identity. We develop and validate a measure of class identity using naming decisions. Exploiting within-household variation, we show that migration patterns that increased the local share of culturally-distant workers reduced working class identification. Where migration increased the cultural distance of the working class, workers were less likely to join unions, voters were less likely to support the nascent Labour Party, and parliamentary candidates were less likely to target working class voters. By 1911, slower in-migration and rising local population growth reduced working class distance in urban areas, which also became strongholds of support for Labour. Migration alters social identity and creates political cleavages.

中文摘要

人们何时认同自己的阶级？来自社会心理学的证据表明，如果个体与某个群体的成员相似，他们更有可能认同该群体。我们研究了20世纪初的英国，并表明区域文化异质性与内部移民共同影响了阶级认同。我们利用命名决策开发并验证了一种阶级认同的衡量标准。利用家庭内部的差异，我们表明，增加当地文化背景相异工人比例的移民模式降低了工人阶级认同。在移民增加了工人阶级文化距离的地方，工人加入工会的可能性更低，选民支持新兴工党的可能性更低，议会候选人针对工人阶级选民的可能性也更低。到1911年，较慢的迁入人口和不断上升的本地人口增长减少了城市地区的工人阶级距离，这些城市地区也成为了工党的支持堡垒。移民改变了社会认同并造成了政治分裂。

No. 67论文详情NBER w34720

Creating High-Opportunity Neighborhoods: Evidence from the HOPE VI Program

创造高机会社区：来自HOPE VI项目的证据

Raj Chetty, Rebecca Diamond, Thomas B. Foster, Lawrence F. Katz, Sonya Porter, Matthew Staiger, Laura Tach

Abstract

We study whether low-economic-mobility neighborhoods can be transformed into high-mobility areas by analyzing the HOPE VI program, which invested $\$17$ billion to revitalize 262 distressed public housing developments. We estimate the program’s impacts using a matched difference-in-differences design, comparing outcomes in revitalized developments to observably similar control developments using anonymized tax records. HOPE VI reduced neighborhood poverty rates by attracting higher-income families to revitalized neighborhoods, but had no causal impact on the earnings of adults living in public housing units. Children raised in revitalized public housing units earned more, were more likely to attend college, and were less likely to be incarcerated. Using a movers exposure design and sibling comparisons, we show that these improvements were driven by changes in neighborhoods’ causal effects on children’s outcomes. The improvements in neighborhood causal effects were driven in large part by changes in social interaction: HOPE VI increased interaction between public housing residents and peers in surrounding neighborhoods and increased earnings more for subgroups with higher-income peers. Many low-income families in the U.S. currently live in neighborhoods that are as socially isolated as the HOPE VI developments were prior to revitalization. We conclude that it is feasible to create high-opportunity neighborhoods and that connecting socially isolated areas to surrounding communities is a cost-effective approach to doing so.

中文摘要

我们通过分析HOPE VI项目来研究低经济流动性社区能否被改造成高流动性区域，该项目投资170亿美元用于振兴262个陷入困境的公共住房开发项目。我们使用匹配的双重差分设计来估计该项目的影响，利用匿名税务记录将振兴后的开发项目的结果与可观察特征相似的对照开发项目进行比较。HOPE VI通过吸引高收入家庭到振兴后的社区来降低社区贫困率，但对居住在公共住房单元中的成年人的收入没有因果影响。在振兴后的公共住房单元中长大的孩子收入更高，上大学的可能性更大，被监禁的可能性更小。利用迁移者暴露设计和兄弟姐妹比较，我们表明这些改善是由社区对儿童结果的因果效应的变化驱动的。社区因果效应的改善在很大程度上是由社会互动的变化驱动的：HOPE VI增加了公共住房居民与周边社区同龄人之间的互动，并且对于拥有更高收入同龄人的子群体，其收入增长更大。美国许多低收入家庭目前居住的社区，其社会隔离程度与HOPE VI项目振兴前的开发项目相当。我们得出结论，创造高机会社区是可行的，并且将社会隔离区域与周边社区连接起来是一种成本效益高的方法。

No. 68论文详情NBER w34719

Financial Crises: History, Theory and New Insights

金融危机：历史、理论与新见解

Eric Hilt

Abstract

This review essay discusses the history, causes and consequences of financial crises. In recent years scholars have assembled new sources of data and utilized new empirical designs to analyze crises, shedding light on old questions and producing new insights. This essay highlights those new insights, and uses the historical record of crises in the United States to put those insights into perspective. I begin with a discussion of the defining characteristics of financial crises and their evolution, both in the U.S. and in the rest of the world. I then revisit the chronology of crises in the U.S. since 1870. Data on bank failure rates and large-bank equity losses suggest that some panics were not full-blown financial crises, and also identify episodes when no panic occurred that could potentially be considered crises. I then turn to two categories of theoretical models developed to analyze the mechanisms responsible for crises. The first focuses on asset price bubbles, which have been associated with many crises. The second is focused on the dynamics of bank runs and panics, which have been especially common in the United States. Finally, I present an overview of the effects of crises and the mechanisms transmitting financial distress in the banking system into the rest of the economy.

中文摘要

这篇综述文章讨论了金融危机的历史、原因和后果。近年来，学者们整理了新的数据来源并利用新的实证设计来分析危机，为旧问题提供了新见解并产生了新洞见。本文重点介绍了这些新见解，并利用美国危机的历史记录将这些见解置于背景中。我首先讨论了金融危机的定义特征及其在美国和世界其他地区的演变。然后，我重新审视了自1870年以来美国危机的年表。关于银行倒闭率和大银行股权损失的数据表明，一些恐慌并非全面的金融危机，同时也识别出一些没有发生恐慌但可能被视为危机的时期。接着，我转向两类用于分析危机机制的理论模型。第一类侧重于资产价格泡沫，许多危机都与资产价格泡沫有关。第二类侧重于银行挤兑和恐慌的动态，这在美国尤其常见。最后，我概述了危机的影响以及将银行体系中的金融困境传导至经济其他部门的机制。

No. 69论文详情NBER w34718

Structural Change and Jobless Development

结构变迁与无就业发展

Franziska L. Ohnsorge, Richard Rogerson, Zoe Xie

Abstract

Benchmark models of structural transformation focus on the reallocation of employment across sectors while assuming that overall employment stays constant. We show that this assumption does not match facts for developing economies. We study a panel of 48 mostly developing economies over the period 1990--2018 and document a strong positive relationship between the share of the population employed in agriculture and the overall employment rate. That is, the early part of the development process is associated with a substantial decline in the total employment rate. Motivated by this finding, we extend a benchmark model of structural change featuring Stone-Geary preferences to allow for endogenous labor supply. We show that this model can account for the patterns we document in the data both qualitatively and quantitatively. We use a calibrated version of our model to study the employment dynamics in several developing economies and show that structural change is a quantitatively important source of employment changes during the early stages of development.

中文摘要

结构转型的基准模型侧重于就业在各部门间的重新配置，同时假设总体就业保持不变。我们表明这一假设与发展中经济体的实际情况不符。我们研究了1990-2018年间48个主要是发展中经济体的面板数据，并记录了农业就业人口占总人口比例与总体就业率之间的强正相关关系。也就是说，发展过程的早期阶段与总就业率的显著下降相关。受此发现启发，我们扩展了一个具有Stone-Geary偏好的结构变迁基准模型，以允许内生的劳动力供给。我们表明，该模型在定性和定量上都能解释我们在数据中记录的模式。我们使用校准后的模型来研究几个发展中经济体的就业动态，并表明结构变迁是发展早期阶段就业变化的一个数量上重要的来源。

No. 70论文详情NBER w34717

Global Imbalances and Power Imbalances

全球失衡与权力失衡

Christopher Clayton, Matteo Maggiori, Jesse Schreger

Abstract

We discuss the conditions under which global imbalances, such as China being a large foreign creditor and the United States being a large foreign debtor, might also generate power imbalances. We highlight possible theoretical channels and empirical measures that the future literature could investigate in a full treatment of this topic.

中文摘要

我们讨论了全球失衡（例如中国是大型外国债权国而美国是大型外国债务国）也可能产生权力失衡的条件。我们强调了未来文献在对这一主题进行全面处理时可以研究的可能理论渠道和实证衡量标准。

No. 71论文详情NBER w34716

Gender Norms and the Labor Market

性别规范与劳动力市场

Patricia Cortés, Jisoo Hwang, Jessica Pan, Uta Schönberg

Abstract

Despite substantial convergence in men’s and women’s economic roles, gender gaps in labor market outcomes persist across countries. This article provides a unified framework for understanding how gender norms shape economic behavior, distinguishing between internalized norms—preferences and beliefs tied to gender identity—and external norms arising from peer pressure and social coordination. We first document cross-country and within-country variation in gender attitudes, alongside gradual but uneven shifts toward more egalitarian views. We then review empirical evidence on the origins, persistence, and transmission of gender norms, and their effects on human capital accumulation, labor supply, wages, and policy take-up. The review highlights both the durability of gender norms and the mechanisms through which policies, institutions, and media can induce norm change, with implications for the design of effective interventions.

中文摘要

尽管男性和女性的经济角色已大幅趋同，但各国劳动力市场结果中的性别差距依然存在。本文提供了一个统一的框架来理解性别规范如何塑造经济行为，区分了内化规范——与性别认同相关的偏好和信念——以及源于同伴压力和社会协调的外部规范。我们首先记录了性别态度的跨国和国内差异，以及向更平等观念逐渐但不均衡的转变。然后，我们回顾了关于性别规范的起源、持续性和传播，及其对人力资本积累、劳动力供给、工资和政策采纳影响的实证证据。这篇综述强调了性别规范的持久性，以及政策、制度和媒体可以引发规范变化的机制，这对设计有效的干预措施具有启示意义。

No. 72论文详情NBER w34715

You Only Live Twice: Financial Inflows and Growth in a Westward-Facing Ukraine

你只活两次：面向西方的乌克兰的金融流入与增长

Yuriy Gorodnichenko, Maurice Obstfeld

Abstract

The monumental task of rebuilding postwar Ukraine requires early planning and identification of growth strategies. The earlier accession of Eastern European countries to the European Union and NATO offers a template that relies on massive foreign direct investment and public structural funds. This approach helps to raise incomes directly and can create a virtuous circle where capital deepening facilitates technological upgrades and repatriation of war refugees, which in turn stimulate more investment. We show theoretically that the government can refine this strategy by internalizing positive externalities from having a higher capital stock: Investment in physical capital relaxes borrowing constraints (thus allowing more capital inflows) and raises wages (thus encouraging more Ukrainian refugees to return home).

中文摘要

重建战后乌克兰的艰巨任务需要早期规划和确定增长战略。东欧国家早期加入欧盟和北约提供了一个模板，该模板依赖于大量的外国直接投资和公共结构基金。这种方法有助于直接提高收入，并可以创造一个良性循环，其中资本深化促进技术升级和战争难民遣返，进而刺激更多投资。我们从理论上表明，政府可以通过内化拥有更高资本存量的正外部性来完善这一战略：对实物资本的投资放松了借贷约束（从而允许更多资本流入）并提高了工资（从而鼓励更多乌克兰难民返回家园）。

Measuring Efficiency and Equity Framing in Economics Research: LLM-Based Evidence from 1950 to 2021

经济学研究中的效率与公平框架衡量：基于1950年至2021年LLM的证据

Sebastian Galiani, Ramiro H. Gálvez, Franco Mettola La Giglia, Raul A. Sosa

Abstract

We measure how frontier research frames what is normatively at stake along the efficiency and equity dimension. We develop and validate an LLM-based measurement pipeline and apply it to 27,464 full-text journal articles from 1950 to 2021. Efficiency focused framing rises through the late 1980s, then declines as equity related framing expands after 1990, especially in applied work and policy evaluations. By 2021, papers with an equity component are about as common as papers framed purely around efficiency. President transmittal letters in the Economic Report of the President show a similar post 1990 shift toward equity, providing an external benchmark.

中文摘要

我们衡量了前沿研究如何在效率与公平维度上构建规范性议题。我们开发并验证了一个基于LLM的衡量流程，并将其应用于1950年至2021年间27,464篇全文期刊文章。以效率为中心的框架在1980年代末期上升，随后在1990年之后，随着与公平相关的框架扩展而下降，尤其是在应用工作和政策评估中。到2021年，包含公平成分的论文与纯粹围绕效率构建的论文数量大致相当。《总统经济报告》中的总统提交信也显示出1990年后向公平的类似转变，这提供了一个外部基准。

No. 74论文详情NBER w34713

Teaching Economics to the Machines

向机器教授经济学

Hui Chen, Yuhan Cheng, Yanchu Liu, Ke Tang

Abstract

Structural economic models, while parsimonious and interpretable, often exhibit poor data fit and limited forecasting performance. Machine learning models, by contrast, offer substantial flexibility but are prone to overfitting and weak out-of-distribution generalization. We propose a theory-guided transfer learning framework that integrates structural restrictions from economic theory into machine learning models. The approach pre-trains a neural network on synthetic data generated by a structural model and then fine-tunes it using empirical data, allowing potentially misspecified economic restrictions to inform and regularize learning on empirical data. Applied to option pricing, our model substantially outperforms both structural and purely data-driven benchmarks, with especially large gains in small samples, under unstable market conditions, and when model misspecification is limited. Beyond performance, the framework provides diagnostics for improving structural models and introduces a new model-comparison metric based on data-model complementarity.

中文摘要

结构性经济模型虽然简洁且可解释，但通常表现出较差的数据拟合和有限的预测性能。相比之下，机器学习模型提供了极大的灵活性，但容易过拟合且泛化能力弱。我们提出了一个理论引导的迁移学习框架，将经济理论的结构性约束整合到机器学习模型中。该方法首先在由结构性模型生成的合成数据上预训练一个神经网络，然后使用经验数据对其进行微调，从而允许可能被错误设定的经济约束来告知和正则化对经验数据的学习。应用于期权定价时，我们的模型显著优于结构性基准和纯数据驱动基准，在小样本、市场条件不稳定以及模型误设有限的情况下，收益尤其巨大。除了性能提升外，该框架还提供了改进结构性模型的诊断方法，并引入了一种基于数据-模型互补性的新模型比较指标。

No. 75论文详情NBER w34712

A Model of Artificial Jagged Intelligence

人工锯齿智能模型

Joshua S. Gans

Abstract

Generative AI systems often display highly uneven performance across tasks that appear “nearby”: they can be excellent on one prompt and confidently wrong on another with only small changes in wording or context. We call this phenomenon Artificial Jagged Intelligence (AJI). This paper develops a tractable economic model of AJI that treats adoption as an information problem: users care about local reliability, but typically observe only coarse, global quality signals. In a baseline one-dimensional landscape, truth is a rough Brownian process, and the model “knows” scattered points drawn from a Poisson process. The model interpolates optimally, and the local error is measured by posterior variance. We derive an adoption threshold for a blind user, show that experienced errors are amplified by the inspection paradox, and interpret scaling laws as denser coverage that improves average quality without eliminating jaggedness. We then study mastery and calibration: a calibrated user who can condition on local uncertainty enjoys positive expected value even in domains that fail the blind adoption test. Modelling mastery as learning a reliability map via Gaussian process regression yields a learning-rate bound driven by information gain, clarifying when discovering “where the model works” is slow. Finally, we study how scaling interacts with discoverability: when calibrated signals and user mastery accelerate the harvesting of scale improvements, and when opacity can make gains from scaling effectively invisible.

中文摘要

生成式AI系统通常在看似“邻近”的任务上表现出高度不均衡的性能：它们可能在一个提示上表现出色，而在措辞或上下文仅有微小变化的另一个提示上却自信地犯错。我们将这种现象称为人工锯齿智能（AJI）。本文开发了一个易于处理的经济学模型来解释AJI，将采用视为一个信息问题：用户关心局部可靠性，但通常只能观察到粗略的全局质量信号。在一个基准的一维景观中，真实情况是一个粗糙的布朗过程，而模型“知道”从泊松过程中抽取的散点。模型进行最优插值，局部误差由后验方差衡量。我们推导出一个盲用用户的采用阈值，表明经验误差因检查悖论而被放大，并将规模法则解释为更密集的覆盖，这提高了平均质量但并未消除锯齿性。然后我们研究掌握和校准：一个能够根据局部不确定性进行条件判断的校准用户，即使在未通过盲用采用测试的领域也能获得正的期望值。将掌握建模为通过高斯过程回归学习可靠性图，会得到一个由信息增益驱动的学习率边界，阐明了何时发现“模型在何处有效”是缓慢的。最后，我们研究规模如何与可发现性相互作用：何时校准信号和用户掌握能加速规模改进的收获，以及何时不透明性会使规模带来的收益实际上不可见。

No. 76论文详情NBER w34711

Business Concentration around the World: 1900-2020

全球商业集中度：1900-2020年

Yueran Ma, Mengdi Zhang, Kaspar Zimmermann

Abstract

We collect new data to document the long-run evolution of the firm size distribution in ten market-based economies in Asia, Europe, North America, and Oceania, where we can obtain comprehensive coverage of the population of firms. Around the world, we observe prevalent increases in the concentration of sales, net income, and equity capital over the past century. These trends hold in the aggregate and at the industry level. Meanwhile, employment concentration has been stable over the long run in most cases. The evidence shows that the rising dominance of large firms is a pervasive phenomenon, not limited to the recent decades or the United States, and that large firms often achieve greater scale without proportionally more workers.

中文摘要

我们收集了新数据，以记录亚洲、欧洲、北美和大洋洲十个市场经济体中企业规模分布的长期演变，在这些地区我们可以获得企业总体的全面覆盖。在全球范围内，我们观察到过去一个世纪中销售额、净收入和股权资本的集中度普遍上升。这些趋势在总体层面和行业层面都存在。与此同时，在大多数情况下，就业集中度在长期内保持稳定。证据表明，大企业日益占据主导地位是一种普遍现象，并不仅限于最近几十年或美国，而且大企业通常在不按比例增加工人的情况下实现了更大的规模。

No. 77论文详情NBER w34710

FinTech and Customer Capital

金融科技与客户资本

Bianca He, Lauren Mostrom, Amir Sufi

Abstract

Financial Technology (“FinTech”) firms invest significantly more in customer capital relative to traditional financial firms, and such investment builds valuable customer capital. Higher investment by FinTech firms is not accounted for by sectoral focus or differences in firm age. Reasons for higher customer capital investment are explored, including the need to build trust with customers, the focus on downstream segments of the financial marketplace, the operation of platform-based business models, and a heavier reliance on valuable customer data.

中文摘要

金融科技（FinTech）公司相对于传统金融公司在客户资本上的投资显著更多，并且这种投资建立了有价值的客户资本。金融科技公司更高的投资并非由行业重点或公司年龄差异所解释。我们探讨了客户资本投资更高的原因，包括需要建立客户信任、专注于金融市场的下游环节、运营基于平台的商业模式，以及对有价值的客户数据的更大依赖。

No. 78论文详情NBER w34709

AI in Charge: Large-Scale Experimental Evidence on Electric Vehicle Charging Demand

AI负责：关于电动汽车充电需求的大规模实验证据

Robert D. Metcalfe, Andrew Schein, Cohen R. Simpson, Yixin Sun

Abstract

One of the promising opportunities offered by AI to support the decarbonization of electricity grids is to align demand with low-carbon supply. We evaluated the effects of one of the world’s largest AI managed EV charging tariffs (a retail electricity pricing plan) using a large-scale natural field experiment. The tariff dynamically controlled vehicle charging to follow real-time wholesale electricity prices and coordinate and optimize charging for the grid and the consumer through AI. We randomized financial incentives to encourage enrollment onto the tariff. Over more than a year, we found that the tariff led to a 42% reduction in household electricity demand during peak hours, with 100% of this demand shifted to lower-cost and lower-carbon-intensity periods. The tariff generated substantial consumer savings, while demonstrating potential to lower producer costs, energy system costs, and carbon emissions through significant load shifting. Overrides of the AI algorithm were low, suggesting that this tariff was likely more efficient than a real-time-pricing tariff without AI, given our theoretical framework. We found similar plug-in and override behavior in several markets, including the UK, US, Germany, and Spain, implying the potential for comparable demand and welfare effects. Our findings highlight the potential for scalable AI managed charging and its substantial welfare gains for the electricity system and society. We also show that experimental estimates differed meaningfully from those obtained via non-randomized difference-in-differences analysis, due to differences in the samples in the two evaluation strategies, although we can reconcile the estimates with observables.

中文摘要

AI为支持电网脱碳提供的有前景的机会之一是将需求与低碳供应对齐。我们通过一项大规模自然现场实验，评估了世界上最大的AI管理电动汽车充电电价之一（一种零售电价计划）的效果。该电价通过AI动态控制车辆充电，以跟踪实时批发电价，并为电网和消费者协调和优化充电。我们随机分配了经济激励以鼓励加入该电价。在超过一年的时间里，我们发现该电价导致高峰时段家庭用电需求减少了42%，并且100%的需求被转移到了成本更低、碳强度更低的时段。该电价产生了可观的消费者节省，同时通过显著的需求转移展示了降低生产者成本、能源系统成本和碳排放的潜力。对AI算法的覆盖操作很少，这表明根据我们的理论框架，该电价可能比没有AI的实时电价更有效率。我们在包括英国、美国、德国和西班牙在内的多个市场发现了类似的插电和覆盖行为，这意味着可能存在类似的需求和福利效应。我们的发现突显了可扩展的AI管理充电的潜力及其为电力系统和社会带来的巨大福利收益。我们还表明，实验估计与非随机双重差分分析获得的估计存在显著差异，这是由于两种评估策略中样本的差异造成的，尽管我们可以通过可观测变量来调和这些估计。

Pricing Residential Mortgage Credit Risk in the Post-GFC Era

后全球金融危机时代的住宅抵押贷款信用风险定价

Agostino Capponi, Stijn Van Nieuwerburgh, Xinkai Wu

Abstract

Following the Great Financial Crisis (GFC), the Credit Risk Transfer (CRT) bond market emerged as a new asset class in U.S. mortgage market. We develop an asset pricing framework for CRTs consistent with Treasury, corporate bond, and housing markets. Our analysis reveals that the Government-Sponsored Enterprises compensate investors approximately fairly on average, though they overpay for low-risk tranches and underpay for high-risk ones. Additionally, the post-GFC guarantee fee increases broadly align with underlying credit risk. We find significant reverse cross-subsidization, where high-credit-risk borrowers subsidize low-risk ones. The 2023 reform partially corrected this cross-subsidization.

中文摘要

在全球金融危机（GFC）之后，信用风险转移（CRT）债券市场作为美国抵押贷款市场的一个新资产类别出现。我们开发了一个与国债、公司债券和住房市场一致的CRT资产定价框架。我们的分析揭示，政府赞助企业平均而言对投资者的补偿大致公平，尽管它们为低风险档支付过高，而为高风险档支付不足。此外，后GFC时期的担保费增加与潜在的信用风险大致一致。我们发现存在显著的反向交叉补贴，即高信用风险借款人补贴低风险借款人。2023年的改革部分纠正了这种交叉补贴。

No. 80论文详情NBER w34707

Never Enough: Dynamic Status Incentives in Organizations

永无止境：组织中的动态地位激励

Leonardo Bursztyn, Ewan Rawcliffe, Hans-Joachim Voth

Abstract

We study the ability of a firm to elicit repeated effort from workers by creating a “rat race” of hierarchical status-based incentives. We examine performance using data on over 5,000 German air force pilots during World War II. Pilots’ effort is hard to monitor; motivation is key to success. Fighter pilot performance increases markedly as they approach eligibility for a medal before falling off upon receipt of the award. The same effort path repeats itself as the pilot nears the next higher-prestige medal. Status-conscious pilots also exert more effort when new medals are introduced. We show that medals serve as substitutes for other forms of status. Medal cachet declines over time as lower-ability pilots receive them, making the introduction of new medals desirable. These results suggest that a tiered, expanding system of status-based incentives can repeatedly leverage worker status concerns to extract effort.

中文摘要

我们研究了企业通过创建基于层级地位的“军备竞赛”式激励来促使工人持续努力的能力。我们利用二战期间超过5000名德国空军飞行员的数据来检验绩效。飞行员的努力难以监控；动力是成功的关键。战斗机飞行员的绩效在他们接近获得勋章资格时显著提高，而在获得奖项后下降。当飞行员接近下一个更高声望的勋章时，同样的努力路径会重复出现。当引入新勋章时，有地位意识的飞行员也会付出更多努力。我们表明，勋章作为其他形式地位的替代品。随着能力较低的飞行员获得勋章，勋章的价值会随时间下降，这使得引入新勋章变得可取。这些结果表明，一个分层的、不断扩展的地位激励体系可以反复利用工人的地位关切来榨取努力。

Marginal Admission to Elite High Schools: Long-run Effects on Labor Market Outcomes

精英高中的边缘录取：对劳动力市场结果的长期影响

Francisco J. Cabrera-Hernández, Andrew Dustan, Daniel Osuna Gomez, María Padilla-Romo

Abstract

We estimate the long-run effects of marginal admission to elite public high schools on students' labor supply in the context of Mexico City's centralized high school admission system. Using a regression discontinuity approach, we compare students whose placement exam scores are just above and just below the elite admission threshold. We find that five and ten years after the admission exam, marginally admitted students are less likely to be employed in the formal private sector, and, if employed, they earn lower wages. However, these employment and wage gaps close after 15 years. Moreover, we find that marginal admission to elite high schools leads to delayed entry into the formal labor market, and, at least in the short run, students in elite high schools seem to sort into lower-productivity firms and industries.

中文摘要

我们估算了在墨西哥城集中高中招生体系背景下，边缘录取进入精英公立高中对学生劳动力供给的长期影响。使用断点回归方法，我们比较了分班考试成绩刚好高于和刚好低于精英录取门槛的学生。我们发现，在入学考试后五年和十年，边缘录取的学生在正规私营部门就业的可能性较低，并且如果就业，他们的工资也较低。然而，这些就业和工资差距在15年后消失。此外，我们发现，边缘录取进入精英高中会导致进入正规劳动力市场的延迟，并且至少在短期内，精英高中的学生似乎会流向生产率较低的企业和行业。
