How Adaptable Are American Workers to AI-Induced Job Displacement?

美国工人对人工智能引发的岗位替代的适应能力有多强？

Sam J. Manning, Tomás Aguirre

Abstract

We construct an occupation-level adaptive capacity index that measures a set of worker characteristics relevant for navigating job transitions if displaced, covering 356 occupations that represent 95.9% of the U.S. workforce. We find that AI exposure and adaptive capacity are positively correlated: many occupations highly exposed to AI contain workers with relatively strong means to manage a job transition. Of the 37.1 million workers in the top quartile of AI exposure, 26.5 million are in occupations that also have above-median adaptive capacity, leaving them comparatively well-equipped to handle job transitions if displacement occurs. At the same time, 6.1 million workers (4.2% of the workforce in our sample) work in occupations that are both highly exposed and where workers have low expected adaptive capacity. These workers are concentrated in clerical and administrative roles. Importantly, AI exposure reflects potential changes to work tasks, not inevitable displacement; only some of the changes brought on by AI will result in job loss. By distinguishing between highly exposed workers with relatively strong means to adjust and those with limited adaptive capacity, our analysis shows that exposure measures alone can obscure both areas of resilience to technological change and concentrated pockets of elevated vulnerability if displacement were to occur.

中文摘要

我们构建了一个职业层面的适应能力指数，该指数衡量了工人在被替代后应对工作转型所需的一系列相关特征，涵盖了代表美国劳动力95.9%的356个职业。我们发现，人工智能暴露度与适应能力呈正相关：许多人工智能暴露度高的职业中的工人，拥有相对较强的应对工作转型的手段。在人工智能暴露度处于最高四分位数的3710万工人中，有2650万工人所在的职业也具有高于中位数的适应能力，这使得他们在发生替代时相对更有能力应对工作转型。与此同时，有610万工人（占我们样本中劳动力的4.2%）从事的职业既具有高暴露度，又具有低预期适应能力。这些工人集中在文职和行政岗位。重要的是，人工智能暴露度反映了工作任务可能发生的变化，而非必然的替代；人工智能带来的变化中只有一部分会导致失业。通过区分高暴露度但拥有相对较强调整手段的工人与适应能力有限的工人，我们的分析表明，仅凭暴露度指标可能会掩盖技术变革中的韧性领域，以及在发生替代时脆弱性高度集中的区域。

No. 83论文详情NBER w34704

Tenure-Dependent Severance Costs and Labor Market Dynamics over the Life Cycle

与任期相关的解雇成本与生命周期中的劳动力市场动态

Calebe Figueiredo, Neville Francis

Abstract

We study the labor market effects of tenure-dependent severance pay systems that tie firing costs to workers’ accumulated earnings histories. We develop an overlapping-generations search-and-matching model in which firms face increasing separation costs over the employment relationship. Using administrative employer–employee data from Brazil, we estimate the model and show that tenure-dependent severance costs induce labor hoarding among low-productivity, long-tenured workers who would not be hired if unemployed. These distortions are strongest late in the life cycle, when firms optimally delay separation to avoid severance obligations, while simultaneously imposing higher hiring thresholds on older unemployed workers with shorter continuation values. These forces imply that tenure-based severance policies protect employment histories rather than productivity, shaping labor market dynamics over the life cycle and generating allocative inefficiencies.

中文摘要

我们研究了与任期相关的遣散费制度（该制度将解雇成本与工人累积的收入历史挂钩）对劳动力市场的影响。我们开发了一个世代交叠的搜索匹配模型，在该模型中，企业在雇佣关系存续期间面临递增的分离成本。利用巴西的行政雇主-雇员数据，我们估计了该模型，并表明与任期相关的解雇成本会导致企业对低生产率、长任期工人的劳动力囤积，而这些工人如果失业则不会被雇佣。这些扭曲在生命周期后期最为严重，此时企业为了规避遣散费义务而最优地延迟分离，同时，对于续存价值较短的年长失业工人，企业会施加更高的雇佣门槛。这些力量意味着基于任期的遣散政策保护的是就业历史而非生产率，从而塑造了生命周期中的劳动力市场动态并产生了配置效率低下。

No. 84论文详情NBER w34703

Aggregate Productivity with Discrete Choice

具有离散选择的总体生产率

David Baqaee, Ariel Burstein

Abstract

This paper quantifies aggregate productivity in general equilibrium economies where agents with heterogeneous preferences make discrete choices between locations and occupations. We show how the conventional tools of welfare economics, like cost-benefit analysis, can be extended to these settings. We measure the change in aggregate productivity as the maximum reduction in total factor productivity such that it is possible to make every household at least indifferent to their status quo allocation. Aggregate productivity rises if primary factors can be saved while keeping every household at least indifferent. We characterize this measure of efficiency in terms of compensated supply and demand curves. We show that, to a first-order approximation, the elasticity of aggregate productivity to productivity shocks is given by sales shares (regardless of preferences and technologies). We also provide second-order approximations in terms of elasticities of uncompensated supply and demand curves. We contrast our approach with some popular alternative measures of aggregate efficiency and welfare: real GDP, the cross-sectional average of utilities, and the sum of compensating variations, and show that these alternative measures have serious flaws.

中文摘要

本文量化了在一般均衡经济体中，当具有异质性偏好的主体在地点和职业之间做出离散选择时的总体生产率。我们展示了如何将福利经济学的传统工具（如成本效益分析）扩展到这些设定中。我们将总体生产率的变化衡量为全要素生产率的最大可能减少量，使得在保持每个家庭至少对其现状分配无差异的情况下，这种减少是可行的。如果能够在保持每个家庭至少无差异的同时节省初级要素，则总体生产率上升。我们根据补偿性供给和需求曲线来刻画这一效率度量。我们表明，在一阶近似下，总体生产率对生产率冲击的弹性由销售份额给出（无论偏好和技术如何）。我们还根据非补偿性供给和需求曲线的弹性提供了二阶近似。我们将我们的方法与一些流行的替代性总体效率和福利度量指标（实际GDP、效用的横截面平均值以及补偿变差之和）进行了对比，并表明这些替代性指标存在严重缺陷。

No. 85论文详情NBER w34702

Kalshi and the Rise of Macro Markets

Kalshi与宏观市场的兴起

Anthony M. Diercks, Jared Dean Katz, Jonathan H. Wright

Abstract

Prediction markets offer a new market-based approach to measuring macroeconomic expectations in real-time. We evaluate the accuracy of prediction market-implied forecasts from Kalshi, the largest federally regulated prediction market overseen by the CFTC. We compare Kalshi with more traditional survey and market-implied forecasts, examine how expectations respond to macroeconomic and financial news, and how policy signals are interpreted by market participants. Our results suggest that Kalshi markets provide a high-frequency, continuously updated, distributionally rich benchmark that is valuable to both researchers and policymakers.

中文摘要

预测市场提供了一种新的基于市场的方法，用于实时衡量宏观经济预期。我们评估了来自Kalshi（由CFTC监管的最大的联邦监管预测市场）的预测市场隐含预测的准确性。我们将Kalshi与更传统的调查和市场隐含预测进行比较，考察预期如何对宏观经济和金融新闻做出反应，以及市场参与者如何解读政策信号。我们的结果表明，Kalshi市场提供了一个高频、持续更新、分布信息丰富的基准，这对研究人员和政策制定者都很有价值。

No. 86论文详情NBER w34701

Research to Improve the Quality, Impact, and Value of Home and Community-Based Services

提高家庭和社区服务质量的、影响力和价值的研究

Jacob M. Sims Speyer, Ari Ne'eman, Norma B. Coe, Ellen Meara

Abstract

Nearly eight million Americans use Medicaid home and community-based services (HCBS) to support long-term services and supports for people with disabilities. Recent legislative changes to Medicaid will require states to make difficult choices about how best to meet these long-term services and supports needs. This paper first characterizes the unique goals of HCBS, which differ from those of traditional medical care services, and the state-federal financing and administrative structure of HCBS. Next, based on a review of the literature and input from a panel of experts in HCBS policy and research, we summarize existing evidence and knowledge gaps regarding the quality and cost implications of HCBS at the federal, state, and direct service provision levels. Based on gaps in the evidence, we propose a research agenda related to state-federal incentives, state program choices regarding HCBS financing and delivery models, and the settings and supports for direct service provision. Finally, we describe existing and novel data sources and other opportunities that could accelerate research to fill these evidence gaps and support states and others in designing, implementing, and delivering sustainable, high-quality HCBS.

中文摘要

近800万美国人使用医疗补助家庭和社区服务（HCBS）来支持残疾人的长期服务和支持。最近医疗补助的立法变更将要求各州就如何最好地满足这些长期服务和支持需求做出艰难选择。本文首先描述了HCBS的独特目标（这些目标不同于传统医疗保健服务的目标）以及HCBS的州-联邦融资和行政结构。接下来，基于文献回顾和HCBS政策与研究专家小组的意见，我们总结了关于HCBS在联邦、州和直接服务提供层面的质量和成本影响的现有证据和知识空白。基于证据中的空白，我们提出了一个与州-联邦激励措施、州在HCBS融资和交付模式方面的项目选择以及直接服务提供的环境和支持相关的研究议程。最后，我们描述了现有的和新颖的数据源以及其他机会，这些可以加速研究以填补这些证据空白，并支持各州及其他相关方设计、实施和交付可持续的、高质量的HCBS。

No. 87论文详情NBER w34700

The Distributional Effects of Cost-Sharing in a Universal Healthcare System

全民医保体系中费用分摊的分配效应

Simon S. Bensnes, Ingrid Huitfeldt, Victoria Marone

Abstract

Patient cost-sharing is used as a tool to limit over-utilization of insured healthcare services in almost all high-income countries. We study its distributional consequences in the context of a publicly-funded universal health insurance system, where consumers (as tax-payers) are residual claimants on insurer spending. We highlight the distinction between consumers' elasticity of demand for healthcare services—which moderates how cost-sharing rules affect healthcare utilization—and their baseline level of demand—which moderates how cost-sharing rules affect out-of-pocket costs. Using detailed administrative data on the Norwegian national health insurance scheme, we study a 2010 policy change that raised the age threshold for cost-sharing exemption, thereby increasing patient cost-sharing substantially for adolescents. We find that females and native-born Norwegians have higher average utilization and thus have more at stake financially from cost-sharing, but are relatively less responsive to cost-sharing. In contrast, lower-income individuals as well as individuals with a chronic health condition have both higher average healthcare utilization as well as higher responsiveness. Cost-sharing therefore places a larger burden on these groups both in terms of the financial cost of out-of-pocket spending and in terms of reduced quantities of healthcare used.

中文摘要

在几乎所有高收入国家，患者费用分摊都被用作限制保险医疗服务过度使用的工具。我们在公共资助的全民健康保险体系背景下研究其分配后果，在该体系中，消费者（作为纳税人）是保险公司支出的剩余索取者。我们强调了消费者对医疗服务的需求弹性（它调节费用分摊规则如何影响医疗保健利用）与其基线需求水平（它调节费用分摊规则如何影响自付费用）之间的区别。利用挪威国家健康保险计划的详细行政数据，我们研究了2010年一项提高费用分摊豁免年龄门槛的政策变化，该变化显著增加了青少年的患者费用分摊。我们发现，女性和挪威本土出生的居民平均利用率更高，因此在费用分摊方面有更多的财务风险，但对费用分摊的相对反应较小。相比之下，低收入个体以及患有慢性病的个体，其平均医疗保健利用率和反应性都更高。因此，费用分摊给这些群体带来了更大的负担，无论是在自付支出的财务成本方面，还是在减少的医疗保健使用量方面。

No. 88论文详情NBER w34699

Monopsony, Markdowns, and Minimum Wages

买方垄断、加价折让与最低工资

Ester Faia, Benjamin Lochner, Benjamin Schoefer

Abstract

This paper presents the first direct test of two interlinked predictions at the core of the monopsony theory of the labor market: (i) that firms exploit wage-setting power by marking down wages below the marginal revenue product of labor, and (ii) that exogenous wage constraints, if binding, eliminate markdowns. Our research design revisits the 2015 introduction of a high minimum wage in Germany. Drawing on a monopsony model, we derive an empirically tractable difference-in-differences specification that provides a quantitative benchmark for the firm-level markdown response. Our main result is that empirical markdowns respond only 0–25% as much as the monopsony model would have predicted. Hence, at least for the labor market segment we study, (i) markdowns largely reflect other distortions than monopsony, (ii) markdowns are mismeasured, (iii) minimum wages induce widespread labor shortages, or (iv) the standard monopsony model does not provide a full, realistic account of the labor market.

中文摘要

本文首次对劳动力市场买方垄断理论核心的两个相互关联的预测进行了直接检验：（i）企业通过将工资压低至劳动力边际收益产品以下来利用工资设定权力，以及（ii）外生的工资约束如果具有约束力，则会消除加价折让。我们的研究设计重新审视了2015年德国引入高最低工资的情况。基于一个买方垄断模型，我们推导出一个经验上可处理的倍差法设定，该设定为企业层面的加价折让反应提供了一个定量基准。我们的主要结果是，经验加价折让的反应程度仅为买方垄断模型预测值的0-25%。因此，至少对于我们研究的劳动力市场细分部分而言，（i）加价折让在很大程度上反映了买方垄断以外的其他扭曲，（ii）加价折让被错误衡量，（iii）最低工资导致了普遍的劳动力短缺，或者（iv）标准的买方垄断模型并未对劳动力市场提供一个完整、现实的解释。

No. 89论文详情NBER w34698

SNAP Work Requirements, Administrative Burden and Procedural Denials

SNAP 工作要求、行政负担与程序性拒绝

Jason B. Cook, Elizabeth Cox, Chloe N. East

Abstract

Work requirements are often criticized for imposing administrative burdens that reduce access to benefits, yet prior research has struggled to isolate this mechanism from other sources of disenrollment. This paper provides direct evidence by examining procedural denials in the Supplemental Nutrition Assistance Program (SNAP). We study work requirements for Able-Bodied Adults Without Dependents (ABAWDs) and exploit age-based exemptions that apply to individuals aged 50 and older. Using administrative data and difference-in-differences models leveraging waiver periods, we find that work requirements significantly increase procedural and overall denials. Our results indicate that these policies deter participation through imposed administrative burdens.

中文摘要

工作要求常被批评为施加了行政负担，从而减少了福利的获取，然而先前的研究难以将这一机制与其他导致退出注册的因素区分开来。本文通过考察补充营养援助计划（SNAP）中的程序性拒绝提供了直接证据。我们研究了针对无受抚养人的健全成年人（ABAWDs）的工作要求，并利用了适用于50岁及以上个体的基于年龄的豁免。利用行政数据和利用豁免期的双重差分模型，我们发现工作要求显著增加了程序性拒绝和总体拒绝。我们的结果表明，这些政策通过施加的行政负担阻碍了参与。

No. 90论文详情NBER w34697

Party Pressure and Representation

政党压力与代表性

Chad W. Kendall

Abstract

I study how political parties affect representation in the U.S. House. To do so, I account for party pressure on the votes of members in an otherwise standard spatial model that uses roll call voting patterns to identify member ideologies. I simultaneously estimate voter ideologies from survey responses, leveraging their responses on issues before Congress to bridge voters and members into the same ideological space. I find that, relative to a model without party pressure, member ideologies and those of their constituents are much more closely aligned. The results imply that, in terms of actual votes, parties drive a wedge between members and those they represent. I provide evidence that parties do so strategically, balancing the need for legislative wins and the electoral concerns of their members.

中文摘要

我研究政党如何影响美国众议院的代表性。为此，我在一个原本标准的空间模型中考虑了政党对议员投票的压力，该模型利用唱名投票模式来识别议员意识形态。我同时通过调查回应估计选民意识形态，利用他们对国会审议议题的回应，将选民和议员置于同一意识形态空间。我发现，相对于没有政党压力的模型，议员意识形态与其选民的意识形态更加紧密地一致。结果表明，就实际投票而言，政党在议员与其所代表的人之间制造了隔阂。我提供的证据表明，政党是策略性地这样做，平衡了对立法胜利的需求与其成员的选举关切。

No. 91论文详情NBER w34696

Why is the Mental Health of the Youngest American Workers in Decline?

为什么最年轻的美国工人心理健康状况在恶化？

David G. Blanchflower, Alex Bryson

Abstract

The worsening mental health of young workers in the United States drives the disappearance of the U-shape in wellbeing and the hump-shape in illbeing in the last decade. Illbeing declines in age among workers but is hump-shaped among non-workers across all US states. This has been the case for some time and is apparent in our analyses of two large US datasets with long time runs - the Behavioral Risk Survey System 1993-2025 and the National Health Interview Survey of 1997-2024. Although the mental health of workers and non-workers has been declining it has been deteriorating most quickly among young workers, leading to a steepening in the age gradient of mental illbeing for workers. Improvements in worker wellbeing (and declines in worker illbeing) with age are mirrored in age differences in reported working conditions in the American Job Quality Survey of 2025: six measures of job quality rise with age. Declines in mental health are most pronounced among the youngest workers ages 18-22 who are likely drawn from lower socio-economic classes and report the greatest difficulties making ends meet.

中文摘要

美国年轻工人心理健康的恶化，是过去十年中幸福感U型曲线和不良健康感倒U型曲线消失的原因。在所有美国州，工人中的不良健康感随年龄增长而下降，但在非工人中呈倒U型。这种情况已持续一段时间，并且在我们对两个具有长时间跨度的美国大型数据集——1993-2025年的行为风险监测系统和1997-2024年的全国健康访谈调查——的分析中显而易见。尽管工人和非工人的心理健康状况都在下降，但年轻工人的恶化速度最快，导致工人心理不良健康感的年龄梯度变得更加陡峭。工人幸福感随年龄增长而改善（以及工人不良健康感下降）与2025年美国工作质量调查中报告的工作条件年龄差异相呼应：六项工作质量指标随年龄增长而上升。心理健康状况下降在18-22岁的最年轻工人中最为显著，他们可能来自较低的社会经济阶层，并且报告在维持生计方面面临最大困难。

No. 92论文详情NBER w34695

Hitting Rock Bottom: Economic Hardship and Cheating

跌入谷底：经济困难与欺骗行为

Livia Alfonsi, Michal Bauer, Julie Chytilová, Edward Miguel

Abstract

This paper investigates whether economic hardship undermines preferences for honesty. We use controlled, high-stake measures of cheating for private benefit in a large sample of 5,664 Kenyans, exploiting three complementary sources of variation: experimentally manipulated monetary incentives to cheat, a randomized increase in the salience of one’s own financial situation, and the Covid‐19 income shock (exploiting randomized survey timing, with respondents interviewed before vs. during the crisis). We find that cheating behavior is highly responsive to financial incentives in the experiment. Covid-19 economic hardship—marked by a 51% drop in monthly earnings—leads to a sharp increase in the prevalence of cheating, and the effect increases gradually with prolonged hardship. The effects are largest among the most economically impacted and are amplified when the salience of one’s own financial situation is experimentally increased. The results demonstrate that while most individuals exhibit a strong preference against cheating under normal conditions (in line with the existing body of work), economic forces can account for a substantial share of variation in dishonesty: the estimated cheating rate rises from 29% under low stakes in normal times to 86% under high stakes during the crisis.

中文摘要

本文研究经济困难是否会削弱对诚实的偏好。我们在一个包含5,664名肯尼亚人的大样本中，使用了受控的、高风险的为私利而欺骗的衡量指标，利用了三种互补的变异来源：实验操纵的欺骗金钱激励、随机增加个人财务状况的显著性，以及新冠疫情收入冲击（利用随机化的调查时间，受访者在危机前与危机期间接受采访）。我们发现，在实验中，欺骗行为对金钱激励高度敏感。新冠疫情经济困难——以月收入下降51%为标志——导致欺骗发生率急剧上升，并且这种效应随着困难的持续而逐渐增强。影响在经济上受影响最严重的群体中最大，并且当个人财务状况的显著性被实验性提高时，这种影响会被放大。结果表明，尽管大多数个体在正常情况下表现出强烈的反欺骗偏好（与现有研究一致），但经济因素可以解释不诚实行为中的很大一部分变异：估计的欺骗率从正常时期低风险下的29%上升到危机期间高风险下的86%。

No. 93论文详情NBER w34694

The Geography of Science

科学的地理分布

Abhishek Nagaraj, Randol Yao

Abstract

Science has long been concentrated in the Western world, but the global research landscape is undergoing a profound reorganization. Using data on 44 million publications from 1980 to 2022, we document the geography of science in terms of who produces it, what it studies, and where it diffuses. The share of publications produced in the United States has fallen from 40% in 1980 to 15% in 2022, while China’s share has risen from near-zero to 32%. This pattern extends even to elite outlets, with China now producing over 35% of top-journal publications. Notably, this is driven not only by an expanding researcher base but also—to a large extent—by increases in individual productivity. This growth varies by fields: China leads in the Engineering and Physical Sciences (such as Chemistry), while the US retains its lead in Biomedical and Health Sciences. Moreover, China’s expanding leadership in scientific production has not translated into a commensurate shift in global diffusion and integration. Elite research remains disproportionately focused on US topics (40% of breakthrough publications), and citations to Chinese research disproportionately come from within China rather than from other regions, even for top-tier science. Similar to China, other middle- and low-income countries (including India, Russia, and Brazil) have also expanded output producing as much research as high-income European Union countries combined (about 21% overall) but they remain underrepresented in top-tier journals. Overall, our findings highlight both the democratization and fragmentation of global science, raising important questions about the future of the global scientific enterprise.

中文摘要

科学长期以来集中在西方世界，但全球研究格局正在经历深刻的重新组织。利用1980年至2022年间4400万篇出版物的数据，我们从谁生产科学、研究什么以及在哪里传播三个方面记录了科学的地理分布。美国生产的出版物份额从1980年的40%下降到2022年的15%，而中国的份额从接近零上升到32%。这种模式甚至延伸到精英期刊，中国现在生产超过35%的顶级期刊出版物。值得注意的是，这不仅是由于研究人员基础的扩大，而且在很大程度上是由于个人生产力的提高。这种增长因领域而异：中国在工程和物理科学（如化学）领域领先，而美国在生物医学和健康科学领域保持领先。此外，中国在科学生产方面不断扩大的领导地位并未转化为全球传播和整合方面的相应转变。精英研究仍然不成比例地关注美国主题（占突破性出版物的40%），并且对中国研究的引用不成比例地来自中国内部而非其他地区，即使对于顶级科学也是如此。与中国类似，其他中低收入国家（包括印度、俄罗斯和巴西）也扩大了产出，其研究总量与高收入欧盟国家总和相当（约占整体的21%），但它们在顶级期刊中的代表性仍然不足。总体而言，我们的发现突显了全球科学的民主化和碎片化，引发了对全球科学事业未来的重要问题。

No. 94论文详情NBER w34693

Customer Overlap and Diversion Ratios

客户重叠与转移率

Liran Einav, Mariana D. Guido, Peter J. Klenow

Abstract

We define the concept of customer overlap of product j with product k as the share of j's customers who buy k. We then argue that, in appropriate contexts, customer overlaps are an excellent proxy for diversion ratios, a useful and popular way to summarize competition between sellers of substitute products. Unlike diversion ratios, which are often challenging to estimate, customer overlaps are straightforwardly observed in many data sets. We show theoretically, and then validate empirically, the close connection between customer overlaps and diversion ratios. We then illustrate the potential use of customer overlap in contexts where estimation of diversion ratios could be prohibitive.

中文摘要

我们将产品j与产品k的客户重叠定义为购买产品k的j客户所占的份额。然后我们论证，在适当的背景下，客户重叠是转移率的一个极好的代理变量，转移率是总结替代品卖家之间竞争的一种有用且流行的方法。与通常难以估计的转移率不同，客户重叠在许多数据集中可以直接观察到。我们从理论上证明，然后通过实证验证，客户重叠与转移率之间的紧密联系。然后，我们说明了在估计转移率可能成本高昂的背景下，客户重叠的潜在用途。

No. 95论文详情NBER w34692

Skipping the Factory: Service-Led Growth and Structural Transformation in the Developing World

跳过工厂：发展中国家的服务业主导增长与结构转型

Michael Peters, Youdan Zhang, Fabrizio Zilibotti

Abstract

In today’s developing world, many economies appear to bypass industrialization and transition directly from agriculture to services. The largest rise in service employment has occurred in non-tradable consumer services, such as retail and hospitality, especially in urban areas, where many cities resemble consumer hubs built around local demand. These patterns of growth raise fundamental questions: Can service-led growth sustain a growth of living standards over time? Is service-led growth inherently biased toward affluent urban consumers? What role should policy play? We propose a parsimonious general equilibrium framework that incorporates non-homothetic preferences and locally non-tradable consumer services. Our framework bridges macro and micro perspectives, and enables counterfactual and welfare analysis that accounts for both individual and spatial heterogeneity. We relate our framework to the recent literature and suggest several extensions and directions of future research.

中文摘要

在当今的发展中世界，许多经济体似乎绕过了工业化，直接从农业过渡到服务业。服务业就业的最大增长发生在非贸易性消费服务业，如零售和酒店业，尤其是在城市地区，许多城市看起来像是围绕本地需求建立的消费中心。这些增长模式引发了根本性问题：服务业主导的增长能否长期维持生活水平的提升？服务业主导的增长是否天生偏向富裕的城市消费者？政策应发挥什么作用？我们提出了一个简约的一般均衡框架，该框架包含了非位似偏好和本地非贸易性消费服务。我们的框架连接了宏观和微观视角，并能够进行反事实和福利分析，同时考虑个体和空间异质性。我们将我们的框架与近期文献联系起来，并提出了未来研究的若干扩展和方向。

No. 96论文详情NBER w34691

Ricardian Non-Equivalence

李嘉图非等价

Martin S. Eichenbaum, Joao Guerreiro, Jana Obradovic

Abstract

This paper presents new survey evidence on how household spending changes in response to fiscal transfers. Our key finding is that the planned propensity to spend out of transfers equals the marginal propensity to consume (MPC). This result implies that households do not incorporate future tax liabilities into their spending plans. The canonical HANK model cannot account for our survey results because people in that model are overly sensitive to future tax liabilities. We develop an extended HANK model in which households are partially inattentive to future tax liabilities and to the general-equilibrium consequences of fiscal policy. This inattention dampens forward-looking intertemporal MPCs, bringing the model into line with our survey evidence. We use the model to analyze the aggregate effects of fiscal policy changes and find that both transfer and government spending multipliers are larger in the inattentive HANK model than in the canonical HANK framework.

中文摘要

本文提供了关于家庭支出如何响应财政转移支付变化的新调查证据。我们的关键发现是，计划从转移支付中支出的倾向等于边际消费倾向（MPC）。这一结果意味着家庭没有将未来的税收负担纳入其支出计划。标准的HANK模型无法解释我们的调查结果，因为该模型中的人对未来税收负担过于敏感。我们开发了一个扩展的HANK模型，其中家庭对未来税收负担以及财政政策的一般均衡后果部分地不关注。这种不关注抑制了前瞻性的跨期MPC，使模型与我们的调查证据一致。我们使用该模型分析财政政策变化的总体效应，发现与标准的HANK框架相比，在不关注的HANK模型中，转移支付和政府支出乘数都更大。

No. 97论文详情NBER w34690

AI-Enhanced Handheld ECGs to Screen for Prior Myocardial Infarction in Rural India

AI增强手持心电图在印度农村筛查既往心肌梗死中的应用

Jenny Wang, Alexander Schubert, Nikhil Kanakamedala, Madeline McKelway, Luke Messac, Cyrus Reginald, Frank Schilbach, T.S. Selvavinayagam, Girija Vaidyanathan, Esther Duflo, Ziad Obermeyer

Abstract

Efforts to move care out of hospitals and into the community face a hard constraint: while most medications can be delivered anywhere, diagnosis is still mostly trapped inside the formal health system—clinics, hospitals, and the people and machines inside them. This is especially binding in low- and middle-income countries due to distance, cost, and limited health system capacity. Low-cost data collection devices (e.g., handheld electrocardiograms (ECGs), retinal cameras) are promising, but do not solve the bottleneck: their outputs still require expert interpretation. Artificial intelligence (AI) could turn these raw signals into actionable outputs at scale, but most medical AI is trained in high-income settings and deteriorates in different populations and settings. We assemble a new dataset in rural Tamil Nadu, India that links low-cost device signals to hospital-grade reference testing. We use it to build a proof-of-concept screening tool: an algorithm that predicts the result of a hospital-based reference-standard test (regional wall motion abnormality on echocardiography), using only data from a handheld ECG device (cost: $\$60$). This would allow targeting of secondary prevention medications—high-dose statins, antiplatelet agents, and beta blockers—proven to be cost-effective in both high- and low-resource settings. We evaluate predictive performance and cost-effectiveness of such screening, benchmarking against common clinical risk scores (including the American Heart Association 10-year risk score). In a held-out test set, our model identifies subgroups with rates high enough to make screening very cost-effective: the top 2.5% have a 9.3% rate of evidence consistent with prior heart attack—about six times the base rate—delivering benefits at US$\$1,999$ per life-year saved. The model also flags high-yield patients who would be missed by standard clinical scores, underscoring the limits of transporting Western-derived risk tools to low- and middle-income settings. To enable extensions to other conditions in the dataset, we make all data freely available for research.

中文摘要

将医疗服务从医院转移到社区的努力面临一个硬性约束：虽然大多数药物可以在任何地方提供，但诊断仍然主要局限于正式卫生系统内部——诊所、医院以及其中的人员和设备。由于距离、成本和有限的卫生系统能力，这一点在中低收入国家尤为突出。低成本数据采集设备（例如手持心电图机、视网膜相机）前景广阔，但并未解决瓶颈问题：它们的输出仍然需要专家解读。人工智能可以将这些原始信号大规模转化为可操作的结果，但大多数医学人工智能是在高收入环境中训练的，在不同人群和环境中性能会下降。我们在印度泰米尔纳德邦农村地区收集了一个新的数据集，将低成本设备信号与医院级参考测试联系起来。我们利用它构建了一个概念验证筛查工具：一种仅使用手持心电图设备（成本：60美元）的数据来预测基于医院的参考标准测试结果（超声心动图显示的局部室壁运动异常）的算法。这将有助于针对性地使用二级预防药物——高剂量他汀类药物、抗血小板药物和β受体阻滞剂——这些药物在高低资源环境中均被证明具有成本效益。我们评估了此类筛查的预测性能和成本效益，并以常见的临床风险评分（包括美国心脏协会10年风险评分）作为基准。在保留的测试集中，我们的模型识别出的亚组其比率高到足以使筛查非常具有成本效益：前2.5%的人群中，有9.3%的人存在与既往心脏病发作一致的证据——约为基础比率的六倍——每挽救一个生命年可带来1,999美元的收益。该模型还标记了标准临床评分会遗漏的高收益患者，这突显了将西方衍生的风险工具移植到中低收入环境中的局限性。为了能够将研究扩展到数据集中的其他疾病，我们免费提供所有数据供研究使用。

No. 98论文详情NBER w34689

Financial Globalization: Risk Sharing or Risk Exposure?

金融全球化：风险分担还是风险暴露？

Enrique G. Mendoza, Vincenzo Quadrini

Abstract

We study how the increased cross-country ownership of financial assets between advanced and emerging economies impacted their financial and macroeconomic volatility. While cross-country ownership improved risk-sharing and reduced volatility associated with financial crises, it also increased the exposure of countries to foreign crises, leading to higher international co-movement. Through quantitative applications of a two-region model representative of advanced and emerging economies, we find that financial globalization reduced volatility worldwide, but significantly more in emerging economies.

中文摘要

我们研究了发达经济体和新兴经济体之间跨境金融资产所有权增加如何影响其金融和宏观经济波动性。虽然跨境所有权改善了风险分担并降低了与金融危机相关的波动性，但它也增加了各国对外国危机的暴露，导致更高的国际联动性。通过应用代表发达经济体和新兴经济体的两区域模型的定量分析，我们发现金融全球化降低了全球范围内的波动性，但在新兴经济体中降低得更为显著。

No. 99论文详情NBER w34688

Capital Flows in a World Starved for Liquidity: Analysis and Policy Implications

流动性匮乏世界中的资本流动：分析与政策含义

Enrique G. Mendoza, Vincenzo Quadrini

Abstract

We propose a framework for studying financial and macroeconomic dynamics in an environment where liquid assets have a productive use but their supply is limited (i.e., the economy is starved for liquidity). The private demand for financial assets arises from the need to hold them for production. The private supply of financial assets is limited and unstable because of borrowing constraints and default risk. We discuss open-economy applications that analyze the accumulation of foreign reserves by emerging economies, the increase in public debt issued by advanced economies, the rapid growth of emerging economies, structural changes in financial markets, and financial globalization. A key result is that most of these developments led to a decline in interest rates and an increase in global macroeconomic volatility, driven by riskier borrower portfolios.

中文摘要

我们提出了一个框架，用于研究在流动性资产具有生产性用途但其供给有限（即经济处于流动性匮乏状态）的环境中的金融和宏观经济动态。对金融资产的私人需求源于持有它们用于生产的需要。由于借贷约束和违约风险，金融资产的私人供给是有限且不稳定的。我们讨论了开放经济应用，分析了新兴经济体的外汇储备积累、发达经济体公共债务的增加、新兴经济体的快速增长、金融市场的结构性变化以及金融全球化。一个关键结果是，这些发展中的大多数导致了利率下降和全球宏观经济波动性增加，其驱动因素是借款人投资组合风险的增加。

No. 100论文详情NBER w34687

How Restrictive is U.S. Trade Policy?

美国贸易政策的限制性有多强？

Michael E. Waugh

Abstract

This short note computes Trade Restrictiveness Index measures for current U.S. trade policy. Building on the ideas of Anderson and Neary (1996, 2005), the Trade Restrictiveness Index is the uniform tariff that leaves the U.S. consumer as well off as under actual policy. As of October 2025, U.S. trade policy is twice as restrictive as headline tariff numbers suggest. The Trade Restrictiveness Index is 23 percent, which stands in contrast to the 11 percent average tariff rate. Trade policy towards Canada and Mexico is two to three times more restrictive than average tariff rates suggest. Sectoral analysis shows that the restrictiveness is concentrated in vehicles, machinery, and electrical equipment.

中文摘要

这篇短文计算了当前美国贸易政策的贸易限制指数。基于Anderson和Neary（1996, 2005）的思想，贸易限制指数是指使美国消费者福利水平与实际政策下相同的统一关税。截至2025年10月，美国贸易政策的限制性是其总体关税数字所显示的两倍。贸易限制指数为23%，这与11%的平均关税税率形成鲜明对比。对加拿大和墨西哥的贸易政策的限制性是平均关税税率所显示的两到三倍。行业分析表明，限制性主要集中在车辆、机械和电气设备领域。

No. 101论文详情NBER w34686

Subcontracting in Federal Spending: Micro and Macro Implications

联邦支出中的分包：微观与宏观含义

Geumbi Park, Xiaoqing Zhou, Sarah Zubairy

Abstract

This paper studies the critical but underexplored role of subcontracting in shaping the spatial and firm-level effects of federal government spending. Using newly available data on defense subcontract awards linked to establishment-level data from NETS, we examine prime–subcontractor relationships across regions, industries, and over time. We document three key facts. First, subcontracting reallocates a substantial share of federal dollars across geographic areas, weakening the link between the location of prime contracts and where spending ultimately occurs. Second, subcontracting shifts spending across industries, notably from service-sector primes to manufacturing subcontractors. Third, large firms dominate subcontracting networks, including by receiving subcontracts from smaller primes. Accounting for geographic reallocation implies that conventional estimates understate local fiscal multipliers by about 20%. Furthermore, local multipliers are smaller for subcontracting than for prime contracting, partly because subcontracted spending is concentrated among large manufacturing firms that exhibit more muted employment responses. Establishment-level evidence further shows that subcontracting generates weaker employment effects, even conditional on firm size and industry, reflecting the less stable nature of subcontracting relationships. Overall, our findings show that subcontracting fundamentally reshapes the transmission of procurement spending through the private sector, with important implications for the local and aggregate effects of federal spending.

中文摘要

本文研究了分包在塑造联邦政府支出的空间和企业层面影响中至关重要但未被充分探索的作用。利用新获得的与NETS企业层面数据相关联的国防分包合同数据，我们考察了跨区域、跨行业和跨时间的总承包商-分包商关系。我们记录了三个关键事实。首先，分包将相当大份额的联邦资金重新分配到不同地理区域，削弱了总合同所在地与最终支出地点之间的联系。其次，分包将支出转移到不同行业，特别是从服务行业的总承包商转移到制造业的分包商。第三，大公司在分包网络中占主导地位，包括从小型总承包商那里获得分包合同。考虑地理重新分配意味着传统估计将地方财政乘数低估了约20%。此外，分包的地方乘数小于总承包，部分原因是分包支出集中在那些就业反应较为平缓的大型制造业企业。企业层面的证据进一步表明，即使在控制企业规模和行业的情况下，分包产生的就业效应也较弱，这反映了分包关系的不稳定性。总体而言，我们的研究结果表明，分包从根本上重塑了采购支出通过私营部门的传导，对联邦支出的地方和总体效应具有重要影响。

No. 102论文详情NBER w34685

Unlocking Occupational Opportunity: The Labor Market Effects of DACA

解锁职业机会：DACA的劳动力市场效应

Aimee Chin, Kalena Cortes, Camila Morales

Abstract

U.S. laws make it illegal for employers to knowingly hire undocumented migrants. This legal constraint affects which firms will employ unauthorized workers and what jobs undocumented migrants can expect to get. As a result, unauthorized migrants are more likely to end up in jobs that have a lower risk of detection of immigration status and are less desirable. The Deferred Action for Childhood Arrivals (DACA) policy, which began in August 2012, gave temporary legal authorization to work in the U.S. to a subset of undocumented migrants – those who arrived in the U.S. as children meeting certain other eligibility criteria. In this paper, we use a difference-in-differences strategy to estimate the effect of DACA on the occupational outcomes of young adults who arrived in the U.S. as children. Applying this strategy to individual-level data from the American Community Survey, we find that DACA eligibility decreases the likelihood that noncitizen childhood immigrants hold traditional immigrant jobs or jobs with a high risk of injury, and increases the likelihood of holding a government job or jobs that require occupational licensing. On the whole, DACA eligibility shifts noncitizen childhood immigrants to occupations that are higher-paying and employ more educated workers. These findings are consistent with legal barriers constraining undocumented childhood migrants from taking the jobs they are interested in and have the skills for. These workers are shunted to jobs they find less desirable and there are societal losses from the misallocation of talent.

中文摘要

美国法律规定，雇主故意雇佣无证移民是违法的。这一法律约束影响了哪些公司会雇佣无证工人，以及无证移民可以期望获得什么样的工作。因此，无证移民更有可能最终从事那些移民身份被发现的概率较低且不太理想的工作。始于2012年8月的“童年入境暂缓遣返”政策，给予了一部分无证移民——即那些在儿童时期抵达美国并满足其他特定资格标准的移民——在美国的临时合法工作授权。在本文中，我们使用双重差分策略来估计DACA对儿童时期抵达美国的年轻成年人职业结果的影响。将该策略应用于美国社区调查的个人层面数据，我们发现，DACA资格降低了非公民童年移民从事传统移民工作或高受伤风险工作的可能性，并增加了他们从事政府工作或需要职业许可的工作的可能性。总体而言，DACA资格使非公民童年移民转向收入更高、雇佣更多受过教育工人的职业。这些发现与法律障碍限制了无证童年移民从事他们感兴趣且具备技能的工作这一观点一致。这些工人被分流到他们认为不太理想的工作岗位，并且由于人才错配而产生了社会损失。

Community College Bachelor’s Degrees: How CCB Graduates’ Earnings Compare to AAs and BAs

社区学院学士学位：CCB毕业生与AA和BA毕业生的收入比较

Riley K. Acton, Camila Morales, Kalena Cortes, Julia A. Turner, Lois Miller

Abstract

We provide the first descriptive analysis of the economic value of Community College Baccalaureate (CCB) degrees by examining graduates’ early-career earnings, the costs of completing these programs, and the alignment between field of study and subsequent employment. Using administrative data and controlling for institution and field, we find that CCB graduates earn $\$4,000$ to $\$9,000$ more annually than Associate’s (AA) degree holders one year after graduation but experience average earnings penalties of roughly $\$2,000$ relative to traditional Bachelor’s (BA) recipients. These averages mask substantial heterogeneity: penalties are largest in Computer and Information Technology and Engineering Technology, whereas CCB graduates in Nursing, other Healthcare fields, Business, and Criminal Justice exhibit minimal or no penalties. To contextualize these returns, we analyze tuition and fee structures across CCB-granting institutions and identify two dominant pricing models—constant and escalating. Total CCB program costs fall between those of AA and BA degrees, with escalating structures increasing upper-division prices by about 40 percent. Finally, we examine field-to-industry match patterns and find that CCB graduates in fields with well-defined occupational pathways, such as Health Professions and Education, are highly concentrated in aligned industries, while graduates in more diffuse fields, such as Computer Science, are more broadly dispersed.

中文摘要

我们首次对社区学院学士学位的经济价值进行了描述性分析，考察了毕业生早期职业生涯的收入、完成这些项目的成本以及所学专业与后续就业之间的匹配程度。利用行政数据并控制机构和专业，我们发现，CCB毕业生在毕业一年后的年收入比副学士学位持有者高出4,000至9,000美元，但相对于传统的学士学位获得者，平均收入损失约为2,000美元。这些平均值掩盖了巨大的异质性：在计算机与信息技术以及工程技术领域，收入损失最大，而护理、其他医疗保健领域、商业和刑事司法领域的CCB毕业生则表现出极小或没有收入损失。为了将这些回报置于背景中，我们分析了授予CCB的机构的学费和杂费结构，并识别出两种主要的定价模式——恒定模式和递增模式。CCB项目的总成本介于AA和BA学位之间，其中递增模式使高年级课程的价格提高了约40%。最后，我们考察了专业与行业的匹配模式，发现拥有明确职业路径领域（如卫生专业和教育）的CCB毕业生高度集中在相关行业，而更广泛领域（如计算机科学）的毕业生则分布更为分散。

No. 104论文详情NBER w34683

How In-School Supervised Ed-Tech Support Produces Massive Learning Gains: A Khan Academy Field Experiment in India

校内监督下的教育技术支持如何产生巨大的学习收益：印度可汗学院实地实验

Philip Oreopoulos, Oliver Keyes-Krysakowski, Deepak Agarwal

Abstract

Computer-assisted learning (CAL) platforms frequently underperform at scale not because the technology is ineffective, but because schools face substantial implementation frictions: teachers and administrators must overcome initial technical hurdles, reorganize instructional routines, manage competing scheduling pressures, and do so while uncertain about the technology’s effectiveness—conditions that often lead to low and unproductive student engagement. This study explores whether strengthening implementation structure can raise both the quantity and quality of CAL usage in 83 residential government middle schools in Uttar Pradesh, India and, in turn, learning gains. All schools had access to Khan Academy, but randomly selected treatment schools received on-the-ground lab-in-charges whose sole responsibility was to ensure high-fidelity implementation by securing reliable connectivity, simplifying student rostering, protecting weekly practice time, supervising in-class use, coordinating content with teachers, and monitoring progress. The intervention increased platform usage from 7.2 to 47.4 minutes per week. Mathematics achievement rose by almost half a standard deviation over 31 weeks, with gains broad-based across achievement levels and question difficulty. These results show that the central constraint on effective and scalable CAL is not technology or content, but the presence of organizational structures that ensure sustained, productive instructional use.

中文摘要

计算机辅助学习平台在大规模推广时常常表现不佳，原因并非技术无效，而是学校面临巨大的实施摩擦：教师和管理人员必须克服最初的技术障碍、重组教学常规、管理相互竞争的日程压力，并且在不确定技术有效性的情况下进行这些操作——这些条件常常导致学生参与度低且效率低下。本研究探讨了加强实施结构是否能够提高印度北方邦83所公立寄宿制中学的计算机辅助学习使用数量和质量，并进而提高学习收益。所有学校都可以使用可汗学院，但随机选择的处理学校获得了现场实验室管理员，其唯一职责是通过确保可靠的网络连接、简化学生注册、保护每周练习时间、监督课堂使用、与教师协调内容以及监控进度来保证高保真度的实施。该干预措施将平台使用时间从每周7.2分钟增加到47.4分钟。在31周内，数学成绩提高了近半个标准差，且收益在不同成绩水平和问题难度上广泛存在。这些结果表明，有效且可扩展的计算机辅助学习的核心制约因素并非技术或内容，而是确保持续、高效教学使用的组织结构的存在。

No. 105论文详情NBER w34682

Re-Examining Geographic Variation in Health and Health Care

重新审视健康与医疗保健的地理差异

Amy Finkelstein, Matthew Gentzkow

Abstract

A large literature has documented widespread variation in health care spending per capita across areas of the United States without correspondingly better health outcomes. Recent work has used mover designs to estimate the causal impact of place on both health care spending and mortality. In this paper, we investigate whether places that increase health care spending also tend to be places that increase health. We find that they do not and discuss the implications.

中文摘要

大量文献记录了美国各地区人均医疗保健支出的广泛差异，而这些差异并未带来相应更好的健康结果。近期研究采用迁移者设计来估计地点对医疗保健支出和死亡率的因果影响。在本文中，我们调查了那些增加医疗保健支出的地点是否也往往是促进健康的地点。我们发现并非如此，并讨论了其含义。

No. 106论文详情NBER w34681

Firm Emissions and Credit Allocation

企业排放与信贷配置

Grace Weishi Gu, Galina Hale, Bhavyaa Sharma, Jinhong Wu

Abstract

Do banks help or hamper green transition? To answer this question, we analyze the dynamics of bank lending to firms in the US, EU, and separately Denmark in relation to the borrowers' emissions of CO2. We evaluate the allocation of bank loans across industries and within industries across firms, allowing for heterogeneity of firm emissions and changes in these emissions. To facilitate green transition, bank lending needs to flow to greener and greening firms, but not out of high-emission industries that need funding to transition to cleaner production methods. Using syndicated loan data, we find that for US borrowers, bank lending was likely hampering green transition, while in the EU bank lending is more likely to facilitate it. Zooming in on Denmark, for which we have data on the full universe of firms and banks, we find more significant credit reallocation to greener firms, especially within industries. However, the reallocation of funds to green firms is, to a large extent, a byproduct of green firms becoming bigger. We do not find any evidence consistent with banks active stewardship of green transition.

中文摘要

银行是促进还是阻碍了绿色转型？为了回答这个问题，我们分析了美国、欧盟以及单独针对丹麦的银行向企业发放贷款的动态，并与借款人的二氧化碳排放量相关联。我们评估了银行贷款在行业间以及行业内企业间的配置，考虑了企业排放的异质性和这些排放的变化。为了促进绿色转型，银行贷款需要流向更绿色和正在变绿的企业，但不能从需要资金转型为更清洁生产方式的高排放行业流出。使用银团贷款数据，我们发现对于美国借款人，银行贷款可能阻碍了绿色转型，而在欧盟，银行贷款更有可能促进绿色转型。聚焦于丹麦（我们拥有所有企业和银行的完整数据），我们发现信贷更多地重新配置给了更绿色的企业，尤其是在行业内部。然而，资金向绿色企业的重新配置在很大程度上是绿色企业规模扩大的副产品。我们没有发现任何证据表明银行在积极引导绿色转型。

No. 107论文详情NBER w34680

Platform Work: Evidence from Drivers in India, Indonesia, and Kenya

平台工作：来自印度、印度尼西亚和肯尼亚司机的证据

Achyuta Adhvaryu, Martin Atela, Valentina Brailovskaya, Priyanka Dua, Jenny Susan John, Pratibha Joshi, Rivandra Royono

Abstract

Using surveys and administrative data from representative samples of drivers working on three leading gig platforms in India, Indonesia, and Kenya, we document the composition, economic experiences, and labor market trajectories of platform workers. Combining platform-based earnings with operating cost data, we estimate earnings net of costs (in PPP-adjusted terms) in each context. We find that the flexible nature of platform work enables drivers to work substantially more than the full-time equivalent, generating higher monthly net earnings than low-skill or casual employment, despite comparable or lower hourly net earnings relative to these outside options. Drivers who exit platform work in India and Indonesia do so to take up better-paying full-time positions. In contrast, Kenyan drivers often exit involuntarily, returning to offline driving with adverse financial consequences. One-third of drivers across countries rely on platform work to supplement earnings during emergencies or slow work periods, suggesting that platform work may play an important role as a financial safety net.

中文摘要

利用来自印度、印度尼西亚和肯尼亚三个主要零工平台上工作的司机代表性样本的调查和行政数据，我们记录了平台工人的构成、经济经历和劳动力市场轨迹。结合平台收入与运营成本数据，我们估算了每个情境下扣除成本后的净收入（按购买力平价调整）。我们发现，平台工作的灵活性使司机能够工作远超全职等效时间，从而产生比低技能或临时工作更高的月净收入，尽管其小时净收入相对于这些外部选择相当或更低。在印度和印度尼西亚，退出平台工作的司机是为了从事薪酬更高的全职职位。相比之下，肯尼亚司机通常是非自愿退出，回到线下驾驶工作并面临不利的财务后果。各国约有三分之一的司机依赖平台工作来补充紧急情况或工作淡季的收入，这表明平台工作可能作为财务安全网发挥重要作用。

No. 108论文详情NBER w34679

Transformed Intermediation: Credit Risk to NBFIs, Liquidity Risk to Banks

转型的中介：非银行金融机构的信用风险与银行的流动性风险

Viral V. Acharya, Nicola Cetorelli, Bruce Tuckman

Abstract

We argue that the rapid asset growth of nonbank financial intermediaries (NBFIs) relative to banks is the outcome of transformations of risks between banks and NBFIs that increase the interconnectedness of the two sectors. These transformations are consistent with avoiding tighter, post-GFC bank regulation while harnessing the funding and liquidity advantages of bank deposit franchises and access to safety nets. Specifically, we show that banks fund NBFIs through senior loans and credit lines, which NBFIs use for acquiring junior credit claims, warehouse financing, and liquidity management. We empirically demonstrate that shocks experienced by NBFIs spillover to the banks that provide them with credit lines, particularly in times of stress. We then describe a number of policy approaches that are consistent with our transformation view and conclude with suggestions for future research.

中文摘要

我们认为，非银行金融中介相对于银行的快速资产增长，是银行与非银行金融中介之间风险转型的结果，这种转型增加了两个部门的相互关联性。这些转型与规避后全球金融危机时期更严格的银行监管相一致，同时利用了银行存款特许经营权的融资和流动性优势以及获得安全网的机会。具体来说，我们表明银行通过优先贷款和信贷额度为非银行金融中介提供资金，非银行金融中介则将其用于获取次级信用债权、仓储融资和流动性管理。我们实证证明，非银行金融中介遭受的冲击会溢出到为其提供信贷额度的银行，尤其是在压力时期。然后，我们描述了一系列与我们的转型观点相一致的政策方法，并最后提出了未来研究的建议。

No. 109论文详情NBER w34678

Do GLP-1 Medications Pay for Themselves?

GLP-1 药物能收回成本吗？

Coady Wing, Sih-Ting Cai, Daniel W. Sacks, Kosali I. Simon

Abstract

Glucagon-like peptide-1 receptor agonists (GLP-1s) represent a major improvement in treatment of diabetes, obesity, and cardiovascular risk reduction, but they are also among the most expensive drugs in widespread use and the subject of significant policy debate. The high price of these drugs may overstate their net cost if the health improvements they produce lead to reduced downstream health care use and medical spending, that is, cost offsets. We estimate such offsets using insurance claims data, examining the effects of GLP-1 initiation on subsequent GLP-1 use and spending, and on other non-GLP-1 spending. We use a stacked difference-in-differences design, comparing patients initiating GLP-1 medication to not-yet-treated controls who initiate GLP-1s several months or years later, allowing us to control for underlying time trends and baseline characteristics. Overall, we do not find a reduction in downstream medical spending. Although GLP-1 initiation reduces spending on other diabetes medications, total non-GLP-1 spending increases, driven by higher outpatient health care use; GLP- 1 drug spending rises mechanically. For health care payers, the relevant cost of GLP-1 initiation therefore extends beyond the sticker price of the drug. We find similar results across subgroups of GLP1 initiators including those with prior cardiovascular disease and those without diabetes (consistent with obesity indication). Our main results examine spending responses over the first year after initiation. However, we also estimate longer run effects in a smaller sample and find no cost offsets even five years after GLP-1 initiation. Taken together, these results suggest that payers facing the costs of GLP-1 coverage are unlikely to see large savings from reduced spending on other care. If GLP-1 therapies ultimately yield cost savings, they are likely to occur only over longer horizons or through non-medical channels.

中文摘要

胰高血糖素样肽-1 受体激动剂代表了治疗糖尿病、肥胖症和降低心血管风险方面的重大进步，但它们也是广泛使用中最昂贵的药物之一，并且是重大政策辩论的主题。如果这些药物带来的健康改善导致后续医疗保健使用和医疗支出减少（即成本抵消），那么它们的高价可能高估了其净成本。我们使用保险索赔数据来估计此类抵消，考察开始使用 GLP-1 对后续 GLP-1 使用和支出以及其他非 GLP-1 支出的影响。我们采用堆叠双重差分设计，将开始使用 GLP-1 药物的患者与几个月或几年后才开始使用 GLP-1 的尚未接受治疗的对照组进行比较，从而能够控制潜在的时间趋势和基线特征。总体而言，我们没有发现后续医疗支出减少。尽管开始使用 GLP-1 减少了其他糖尿病药物的支出，但非 GLP-1 总支出增加了，这是由门诊医疗使用增加所驱动的；GLP-1 药物支出则机械地增加。因此，对于医疗支付方来说，开始使用 GLP-1 的相关成本超出了药物的标价。我们在 GLP-1 开始使用者的亚组中发现了类似的结果，包括那些既往有心血管疾病的人和没有糖尿病的人（与肥胖适应症一致）。我们的主要结果考察了开始使用后第一年的支出反应。然而，我们也在一个较小的样本中估计了长期效应，发现即使在开始使用 GLP-1 五年后也没有成本抵消。综合来看，这些结果表明，面临 GLP-1 覆盖成本的支付方不太可能通过减少其他护理支出来实现大量节省。如果 GLP-1 疗法最终能带来成本节约，那很可能只会在更长的时期内或通过非医疗渠道实现。

The Impact of Preschool Entry Age on Children’s Behavioral and Developmental Health in Medicaid

学前入学年龄对医疗补助计划中儿童行为与发育健康的影响

Maya Rossin-Slater, Adrienne Sabety, Aileen Wu

Abstract

We find that public preschools are a gateway to health and social services. Low-income children born shortly before their state’s school-entry cutoff date are more likely to receive school-based services, speech-language pathology, occupational or physical therapy, and vision and dental services at ages three and four, compared to children born after the cutoff. They are also more likely to receive financial support through Supplemental Security Income. These findings suggest that preschool enrollment connects low-income children to the health and social service system in ways that extend beyond the classroom.

No. 111论文详情NBER w34676

Corporate Intent

企业意图

Augustin Landier, Parinitha R. Sastry, David Thesmar

Abstract

Do investors care about why a firm behaves responsibly, over and above what the firm does and how much cash it earns? In our main experiment, participants value shares in companies that reduce pollution relative to peers, while CEOs articulate the company’s intentions: prosocial or for-profit. Investors are willing to pay more for shares in a company that takes a given prosocial action if it is motivated by social concern rather than profit maximization. This "intention premium" is distinct from the valuation effects of cash flows and environmental externalities. Respondents who are deontological, politically liberal, female, or less individualistic value the company’s intent the most. Additionally, and somewhat surprisingly, respondents view favorably firms that embrace both profit and social objectives, without ranking them. Overall, our findings temper claims that when there is no financial trade-off between doing good and doing well, shareholder value and stakeholder value maximization are equivalent.

No. 112论文详情NBER w34675

Experiences, Expectations, and Asset Prices

经历、预期与资产价格

Stefan Nagel

Abstract

In models with subjective beliefs, the dynamics of investor beliefs are central to explaining asset price movements. Allowing subjective beliefs to deviate from full-information rational expectations requires a model of how investors form beliefs. I review recent research that explores experience-based belief formation. The experience-based model closely resembles Bayesian updating but allows individuals to overweight data observed during their own lifetimes when forming beliefs about the parameters of the data-generating process. Because individuals of different age learn from different histories, the model predicts heterogeneity between age groups that evolves over time with the path of realized data individuals have experienced, closely mirroring the age-related variation observed in survey microdata. At the aggregate level, experience-based expectations formation can explain asset price dynamics. In the stock market, learning from experience about long-run cash flow growth generates valuation cycles and return predictability. Experience-based formation of long-term inflation expectations can explain secular changes of real interest rates. I conclude by outlining directions for future research.

中文摘要

在具有主观信念的模型中，投资者信念的动态变化对于解释资产价格变动至关重要。允许主观信念偏离完全信息理性预期需要建立一个投资者如何形成信念的模型。我回顾了近期探索基于经历信念形成的研究。基于经历的模型与贝叶斯更新非常相似，但允许个体在形成关于数据生成过程参数的信念时，过度加权其一生中观察到的数据。由于不同年龄的个体从不同的历史中学习，该模型预测了年龄组之间的异质性，这种异质性随着个体所经历的实际数据路径而随时间演变，这与调查微观数据中观察到的与年龄相关的变化高度吻合。在总体层面，基于经历的预期形成可以解释资产价格动态。在股票市场中，从经历中学习长期现金流增长会产生估值周期和回报可预测性。基于经历形成的长期通胀预期可以解释实际利率的长期变化。最后，我概述了未来研究的方向。

No. 113论文详情NBER w34674

The Economics of Scaling Early Childhood Programs: Lessons from The Chicago School

早期儿童项目规模化经济学：来自芝加哥学派的启示

John A. List

Abstract

Many ideas show remarkable returns in small-scale trials but often disappoint when scaled to broader populations and contexts. Using early childhood investment as a case study, this study develops a dynamic human capital formation model that integrates complementary skill investment with “Option C thinking” on scaling challenges. The model is stylized in the Chicago tradition: micro-founded with optimizing agents, dynamic skill production, and a policymaker evaluating scaling decisions. It formalizes how naive extrapolation from pilot studies systematically overestimates policy efficacy by ignoring “voltage drops,” declining treatment effects due to unrepresentativeness at scale. The model demonstrates that optimal scaling policy requires mechanism-based design that anticipates these failures through backward induction from implementation realities. The scientific insights from a set of recent studies provide valuable perspectives on the model.

中文摘要

许多理念在小规模试验中表现出显著的回报，但在推广到更广泛的人群和环境时却常常令人失望。本研究以早期儿童投资为案例，构建了一个动态人力资本形成模型，该模型将互补性技能投资与关于规模化挑战的“选项C思维”相结合。该模型是芝加哥传统风格的典型代表：以微观基础为起点，包含优化行为的代理人、动态技能生产以及评估规模化决策的政策制定者。它形式化了从试点研究中进行天真外推如何系统地高估政策有效性，原因在于忽略了“电压降”，即由于规模化后样本不具代表性而导致处理效应递减。该模型表明，最优规模化政策需要基于机制的设计，通过从实施现实出发进行反向归纳来预见这些失败。一系列近期研究的科学见解为该模型提供了有价值的视角。

Legalizing Cannabis: Implications for Child Maltreatment

Weiwei Chen, Johanna Catherine Maclean, Michael T. French

Abstract

Cannabis is the most used illicit drug in the United States. Though cannabis possession and consumption are prohibited federally, states are increasingly implementing laws that legalize this substance, initially for medical and, more recently, for recreational use. We study the impact of recreational cannabis laws on child maltreatment reports. How Globalization Unravels: A Ricardian Model of Endogenous Trade Policy

全球化如何瓦解：一个内生贸易政策的李嘉图模型

Jesús Fernández-Villaverde, Tomohide Mineyama, Dongho Song

Abstract

We study how uneven gains from globalization can endogenously generate protectionism as a political equilibrium. Using U.S. data, we document that regions more exposed to import competition display stronger opposition to globalization, especially among households with little financial wealth, and that firms in trade-exposed sectors sharply increase lobbying expenditures. To interpret these patterns, we develop and quantify a general equilibrium Ricardian model with heterogeneous households, input-output linkages, and endogenous trade policy shaped by voting and lobbying. Distributional shocks reallocate political support among voters, while lobbying propagates through production networks, generating strategic complementarities that sustain protectionism. Calibrated to U.S.-China sectoral data from 1991--2019, the model accounts for rising inequality, declining support for globalization, and key aggregate trends in consumption and trade.

No. 116论文详情NBER w34671

With or Without U? Binning Bias and the Causal Effects of Temperature Extremes

有U还是无U？分箱偏差与极端温度的因果效应

Benjamin Jones, Jacob Moscona, Benjamin A. Olken, Cristine von Dessauer

Abstract

Estimates of climate impacts show that extreme temperatures have large and wide-spread effects. To estimate these effects, a common approach counts days in different temperature ranges and considers how exposure to these distinct 'bins' affects outcomes. This often produces non-linear, U-shaped results, in which high and low temperatures have the largest effects. We show that non-linear approaches like these can generate spurious findings. Specifically, global warming induces trends in extreme temperature exposure that correlate mechanically with a location's baseline temperature. Substantial bias emerges if trends in the outcome variable also correlate with baseline temperature for any reason. We demonstrate this problem theoretically, in simulations, and with real outcomes. We then develop solutions. In applications using US data, some results in the literature are unaffected by these corrections, while other results change substantially.

中文摘要

对气候影响的估计表明，极端温度具有巨大且广泛的影响。为了估计这些效应，一种常见的方法是计算不同温度范围内的天数，并考虑暴露于这些不同“分箱”如何影响结果。这通常会产生非线性的U形结果，其中高温和低温的影响最大。我们表明，像这样的非线性方法可能会产生虚假的发现。具体来说，全球变暖会导致极端温度暴露的趋势，该趋势与某个地点的基线温度存在机械相关性。如果结果变量的趋势也因任何原因与基线温度相关，则会出现显著的偏差。我们在理论上、模拟中以及使用真实结果证明了这个问题。然后我们提出了解决方案。在使用美国数据的应用中，文献中的一些结果不受这些修正的影响，而其他结果则发生了显著变化。

No. 117论文详情NBER w34670

Effective Protection with Global Value Chains

全球价值链中的有效保护

Emily J. Blanchard, Mitchell W. Boice, Robert C. Johnson

Abstract

The effective rate of protection (ERP) is a widely-used tool to evaluate the joint impact of input and output tariffs on the net protection offered to individual sectors. Nonetheless, the theoretical foundations underlying the traditional ERP are decades out of date. In this paper, we provide fresh guidance for policy analysts that seek to measure effective protection, with two core elements. First, we develop a new ERP concept, which measures how much tariffs shift the derived demand for real value added at the sector level. The ERP then has an intuitive interpretation: it is the effective subsidy to buyers of sectoral value added that replicates the impact of the tariff structure on demand. Second, we demonstrate how to compute our ERP index accounting for global value chain linkages. The result is an ERP for the GVC age, in which effective protection depends on the structure of value chains across countries and sectors, and the structure of all tariffs applied globally. We demonstrate the usefulness of our approach by analyzing how recent tariff changes have altered effective protection in the United States and the rest of the world.

中文摘要

有效保护率（ERP）是一种广泛使用的工具，用于评估投入品关税和产出品关税对单个部门净保护的综合影响。然而，传统ERP的理论基础已经过时数十年。在本文中，我们为寻求衡量有效保护的政策分析师提供了新的指导，包含两个核心要素。首先，我们提出了一个新的ERP概念，它衡量关税在多大程度上改变了部门层面实际增加值的派生需求。那么，ERP就有了一个直观的解释：它是复制关税结构对需求影响的、对部门增加值购买者的有效补贴。其次，我们展示了如何计算考虑全球价值链联系的ERP指数。其结果是一个适用于全球价值链时代的ERP，其中有效保护取决于跨国家和跨部门的价值链结构，以及全球范围内所有关税的结构。我们通过分析近期关税变化如何改变美国和世界其他地区的有效保护，展示了我们方法的实用性。

No. 118论文详情NBER w34669

Price Discrimination with Costless Resale

无成本转售下的价格歧视

Joshua S. Gans

Abstract

This paper shows that income effects create an endogenous barrier to arbitrage, allowing price discrimination to survive costless resale. A monopolist sells an indivisible good to consumers with heterogeneous incomes who can freely resell. When the good is strictly normal, a consumer's reservation price to resell increases as the purchase price decreases—lower prices leave buyers wealthier and raise their valuation of the good. The monopolist exploits this by subsidising low-income consumers to raise their reservation prices to a target that high-income consumers must also pay. The optimal schedule increases dollar-for-dollar with income in the subsidised segment, weakly dominates uniform pricing, and achieves the first-best allocation when the entire market is served. We show the mechanism extends beyond income effects: low substitutability with market alternatives generates large reservation-price responses even when income sensitivity is modest. Sustaining discrimination requires market power at the individual level—consumer-specific quantity limits—not merely aggregate output restrictions. Extensions examine multiple monopolists and endogenous privacy choices.

中文摘要

本文表明，收入效应创造了一种内生的套利障碍，使得价格歧视能够在无成本转售的情况下存在。一个垄断者向收入异质且可以自由转售的消费者出售一种不可分割的商品。当该商品是严格正常品时，消费者转售的保留价格会随着购买价格的降低而上升——更低的价格使买家更富有，并提高了他们对商品的估值。垄断者利用这一点，通过补贴低收入消费者，将他们的保留价格提高到高收入消费者也必须支付的目标水平。最优定价方案在受补贴的细分市场中与收入呈一对一增长，弱优于统一定价，并且在服务整个市场时实现了最优配置。我们表明，该机制超越了收入效应：即使收入敏感性不高，与市场替代品的低替代性也会产生巨大的保留价格反应。维持歧视需要个体层面的市场力量——消费者特定的数量限制——而不仅仅是总产出限制。扩展部分考察了多个垄断者和内生隐私选择。

No. 119论文详情NBER w34668

Automation Experiments and Inequality

自动化实验与不平等

Seth Gordon Benzell, Kyle R. Myers

Abstract

Many experiments study the productivity effects of automation technologies such as generative algorithms. A key test in these experiments relates to inequality: does the technology increase output more for high- or low-skill workers? However, the theoretical content of this empirical test has been unclear. Here, we formalize a theory that describes the experimental effect of automation technologies on worker-level output and, therefore, inequality. Worker-level output depends on a task-level production function, and workers are heterogeneous in their task-level skills. Workers perform a task themselves or delegate it to the automation technology. The inequality effect of improved automation depends on the interaction of two factors: (i) the correlation in task-level skills across workers, and (ii) workers' skills relative to the technology's effective skill. In many cases we study, the inequality effect is non-monotonic --- as technologies improve, inequality decreases then increases. The model and descriptive statistics of skill correlations generally suggest that the diversity of automation technologies will play an important role in the evolution of inequality.

中文摘要

许多实验研究自动化技术（如生成式算法）的生产率效应。这些实验中的一个关键检验与不平等有关：该技术是增加了高技能工人还是低技能工人的产出？然而，这一实证检验的理论内涵一直不明确。在此，我们形式化了一个理论，描述了自动化技术对工人层面产出（进而对不平等）的实验效应。工人层面的产出取决于任务层面的生产函数，而工人在任务层面的技能是异质的。工人要么自己执行任务，要么将其委托给自动化技术。自动化改进的不平等效应取决于两个因素的相互作用：（i）工人之间任务层面技能的相关性，以及（ii）工人技能相对于技术有效技能的水平。在我们研究的许多情况下，不平等效应是非单调的——随着技术的改进，不平等先下降后上升。该模型和技能相关性的描述性统计普遍表明，自动化技术的多样性将在不平等的演变中发挥重要作用。

No. 120论文详情NBER w34667

Weighing the Impacts of GLP-1s: Quasi-Experimental Evidence From Provider Adoption

权衡GLP-1药物的影响：来自医疗服务提供者采用的准实验证据

Sam Bock, Jasmin Moshfegh, Jonathan Zhang

Abstract

The arrival of GLP-1 medications has been described as one of the most important health care innovations in recent years. We provide large-scale quasi-experimental evidence on their real-world impacts by exploiting variation in the eventual prescribing propensities of patients’ pre-existing primary care providers. Using a panel intent-to-treat design, we compare outcomes for 1.4 million diabetic or obese veterans based on their 2018 provider’s eventual propensity to adopt GLP-1s, leveraging comprehensive electronic health records and biomarker data from the Veterans Health Administration, a setting with minimal insurance attrition and low-cost access to these drugs. Patients whose providers become higher propensity adopters experience substantial improvements in glycemic control and clinically meaningful weight loss; our treatment-on-the-treated estimates closely match estimates from clinical trials. Despite these metabolic benefits, we find no statistically significant average effects on emergency department utilization, mental health and substance use outcomes, or non–GLP-1 medical spending through 2024. However, quantile regression results show heterogeneous effects, with spending declining at lower quantiles and rising at higher quantiles for patients of higher-propensity adopters.

中文摘要

GLP-1药物的问世被描述为近年来最重要的医疗创新之一。我们通过利用患者既往初级医疗服务提供者最终处方倾向的差异，提供了关于其现实世界影响的大规模准实验证据。采用面板意向性治疗设计，我们根据患者2018年时的医疗服务提供者最终采用GLP-1药物的倾向，比较了140万患有糖尿病或肥胖症的退伍军人的结果，利用了退伍军人健康管理局（Veterans Health Administration）的综合电子健康记录和生物标志物数据，该环境具有最低的保险流失率和获取这些药物的低成本途径。其医疗服务提供者成为更高倾向采用者的患者，在血糖控制方面经历了显著改善，并实现了具有临床意义的体重减轻；我们的处理组平均处理效应估计值与临床试验的估计值非常接近。尽管有这些代谢益处，但我们发现，截至2024年，在急诊科使用率、心理健康和物质使用结果或非GLP-1医疗支出方面，没有统计学上显著的平均效应。然而，分位数回归结果显示存在异质性效应，对于更高倾向采用者的患者，支出在较低分位数上下降，在较高分位数上上升。

No. 121论文详情NBER w34666

State and Time-Dependent Pricing

状态依赖与时间依赖定价

Philip Bunn, Nicholas Bloom, Craig Menzies, Paul Mizen, Gregory Thwaites, Ivan Yotzov

Abstract

We present new evidence on how firms set prices using direct questions from a large, economy-wide survey of UK firms. Since 2023, 54% of firms report setting prices in a state-dependent manner, as opposed to changing prices at fixed intervals. In contrast, 44% of firms used state-dependent pricing in 2019. Smaller firms, those with a higher share of non-labour costs, and those reporting higher subjective uncertainty around sales and prices are more likely to be state-dependent. We then analyse the implications of price-setting behaviour for inflation dynamics. State-dependent firms experienced a sharper increase in price growth over 2022-2023, and also a faster subsequent decline. Using evidence from a randomised survey experiment, firm-level forecast errors, and local projections, we show that prices of state-dependent firms respond faster to cost shocks. The difference between state-dependent and time-dependent firms is furthermore larger for bigger shocks, consistent with theoretical predictions.

中文摘要

我们利用对英国企业进行的大规模经济调查中的直接提问，提供了关于企业如何定价的新证据。自2023年以来，54%的企业报告以状态依赖的方式设定价格，而非在固定间隔内改变价格。相比之下，2019年有44%的企业采用状态依赖定价。规模较小的企业、非劳动力成本份额较高的企业，以及报告对销售和价格主观不确定性较高的企业，更倾向于采用状态依赖定价。然后，我们分析了定价行为对通胀动态的影响。状态依赖型企业在2022-2023年期间经历了更剧烈的价格增长，随后也出现了更快的下降。利用来自随机调查实验、企业层面预测误差和局部投影法的证据，我们表明状态依赖型企业的价格对成本冲击的反应更快。此外，对于更大的冲击，状态依赖型企业和时间依赖型企业之间的差异更大，这与理论预测一致。

No. 122论文详情NBER w34665

Brexit and UK Migration: Germany-Benchmarked Evidence on Structural and Reallocation Shifts

英国脱欧与英国移民：关于结构性变化和重新配置变化的德国基准证据

Assaf Razin

Abstract

This paper examines how Brexit reshaped the volume and composition of UK migration flows. To address the inherent endogeneity of migration responses to political change, the study employs a Difference-in-Differences design that benchmarks the United Kingdom against Germany, a stable EU member unaffected by Brexit-related institutional shocks. Treating the 2016 referendum and the 2021 end of free movement as sequential shocks, the results show that migration volume increased after both shocks, but through different channels: the referendum reduced emigration relative to Germany, while the post-2021 points-based system triggered a reallocation of inflows away from EU free-movement migrants toward non-EU migrants from the rest of the world, with a markedly stronger skill-selective profile. The paper analyzes how Brexit reshaped migration flows into and out of the United Kingdom by exploiting the 2016 referendum and the 2021 termination of free movement as sequential institutional shocks. Using a Difference-in-Differences design with Germany as a stable EU benchmark, the results show that Brexit acted as a structural regime shock, not a border-tightening event. Net migration into the UK rose after both shocks—first due to a sharp post-referendum decline in emigration relative to Germany, and later due to a substantial expansion of non-EU immigration under the new points-based system. Immigration patterns exhibit a clear regime shift, with EU inflows contracting sharply after 2016 and globally sourced, skill-selective inflows rising after 2021. In the later period, a modest but notable increase in UK-born emigration relative to Germany also emerges, reflecting frictions in post-Brexit mobility. Overall, Brexit reoriented—rather than reduced—UK migration flows, transforming both their scale and composition.

中文摘要

本文考察了英国脱欧如何重塑英国移民流动的规模和构成。为了解决移民对政治变化反应的内生性问题，本研究采用了双重差分设计，以德国（一个未受英国脱欧相关制度冲击影响的稳定欧盟成员国）作为英国的基准。将2016年公投和2021年人员自由流动的结束视为连续冲击，结果显示，两次冲击后移民数量均有所增加，但通过不同的渠道：公投降低了相对于德国的移民流出，而2021年后的积分制则引发了移民流入从欧盟自由流动移民向世界其他地区非欧盟移民的重新配置，且具有显著更强的技能选择性。本文通过利用2016年公投和2021年人员自由流动的终止作为连续的制度冲击，分析了英国脱欧如何重塑进出英国的移民流动。使用以德国作为稳定欧盟基准的双重差分设计，结果表明英国脱欧是一个结构性制度冲击，而非边境收紧事件。两次冲击后，英国的净移民均有所上升——首先是由于公投后相对于德国的移民流出急剧下降，随后是由于在新的积分制下非欧盟移民的大幅扩张。移民模式呈现出明显的制度转变，欧盟流入在2016年后急剧收缩，而全球来源的、具有技能选择性的流入在2021年后上升。在后期，相对于德国，英国本土出生的移民流出也出现了适度但显著的增长，反映了脱欧后流动性的摩擦。总体而言，英国脱欧重新定位了——而非减少了——英国的移民流动，改变了其规模和构成。

Global Stratification Economics (GSE): A Primer - Definitions and Research Implications

全球分层经济学（GSE）：入门指南——定义与研究意义

Alan A. Aja, Anita Alves Pena, Mary Lopez

Abstract

We coin the term Global Stratification Economics (GSE) to extend Stratification Economics (SE) to international contexts where mechanisms emerge that can be identified as (1) universal but matched to positioning along a country’s development path or (2) context-specific and historically dependent in ways different from the United States and other international environments. Building on SE’s core insight that groups compete over scarce resources and that dominant groups shape rules to preserve advantage, we define GSE as an approach that foregrounds historical genesis (e.g., settler colonialism, slavery, caste, extractive governance, military intervention), local institutions that structure dominance and resistance, and transnational mechanisms (e.g., imported stratification and the lateral mobility hypothesis) that link origin- and destination-country hierarchies. Drawing on evidence from Latin America and the Caribbean, Africa, South and Southeast Asia, and the global macroeconomy, we synthesize research on intergenerational mobility, wealth and asset inequality, labor-market segmentation, colorism, caste and ethnicity, gendered and intersectional constraints, spatial inequality and property regimes, and global value chains. We conclude by outlining how GSE reshapes measurement and international policy evaluation by centering group-differentiated outcomes, institutional transformation, and pillars of recognition, redistribution, and repair and by offering a checklist for researchers to apply GSE.

中文摘要

我们创造了“全球分层经济学”（GSE）这一术语，将分层经济学（SE）扩展到国际背景中，在这些背景下出现的机制可以被识别为（1）普遍存在但与国家发展路径的定位相匹配，或（2）具有情境特异性且历史依赖，其方式与美国及其他国际环境不同。基于SE的核心见解——群体争夺稀缺资源，且主导群体制定规则以维持优势——我们将GSE定义为一种方法，它强调历史起源（例如，定居者殖民主义、奴隶制、种姓制度、掠夺性治理、军事干预）、构建支配与抵抗的地方制度，以及连接原籍国和目的地国等级制度的跨国机制（例如，输入性分层和横向流动性假说）。借鉴来自拉丁美洲和加勒比地区、非洲、南亚和东南亚以及全球宏观经济的证据，我们综合了关于代际流动性、财富和资产不平等、劳动力市场分割、肤色歧视、种姓和民族、性别和交叉性约束、空间不平等与产权制度以及全球价值链的研究。最后，我们概述了GSE如何通过聚焦群体差异化结果、制度转型以及承认、再分配和修复的支柱，并提供一个供研究人员应用GSE的检查清单，来重塑衡量标准和国际政策评估。

The Impacts of Parole Supervision

假释监督的影响

Luke D. Brinkman, Andrew Jordan, Derek Neal

Abstract

We study the impacts of a reform to parole supervision in Illinois. The reform reduced the term of supervision for some parolees from 12 months to 6 months. Using a standard difference-in-differences estimator, we find clear evidence that the reform reduced prison re-entry rates. Sharp drops in technical revocation rates drove these reductions. Rates of prison re-admissions linked to new crimes did not change. Cook County Court records also show no evidence that the reform increased crime rates among parolees. The reform reduced both the cost of incarceration and the cost of parolee supervision without creating harms to public safety.

中文摘要

我们研究了伊利诺伊州一项假释监督改革的影响。该改革将部分假释人员的监督期限从12个月缩短至6个月。使用标准的双重差分估计量，我们发现有明确证据表明该改革降低了重返监狱率。技术性撤销率的急剧下降推动了这些降低。与新犯罪相关的重新入狱率没有变化。库克县法院的记录也显示，没有证据表明该改革提高了假释人员的犯罪率。该改革既降低了监禁成本，也降低了假释监督成本，且未对公共安全造成损害。

No. 125论文详情NBER w34662

Nuclear Operations with a High Penetration of Renewables: The Case of France

可再生能源高渗透率下的核电运营：以法国为例

Nicolas Astier, Frank A. Wolak

Abstract

Nuclear and intermittent renewables (wind and solar) are generally regarded as the only scalable technologies producing low-carbon electricity. However, the extent to which these technologies can co-exist in a reliable power system depends on whether nuclear units can adjust their operations to renewable output fluctuations. Using hourly data from the French power system, we find that nuclear units are operated quite flexibly, and that the foregone energy production due to “load following” actions (relative to the counterfactual of operating at full capacity during load following events) is currently limited. However, we find that an additional load following event is associated with a slightly higher likelihood of a unit failure. We also find that unit-level minimum output constraints are binding more frequently as system-wide renewable generation increases, especially so for units most exposed to solar generation. In 2024, hours during which available nuclear flexibility was exhausted are associated with non-positive hourly day-ahead prices.

中文摘要

核电和间歇性可再生能源（风能和太阳能）通常被认为是仅有的两种可规模化生产低碳电力的技术。然而，这些技术能否在可靠的电力系统中共存，取决于核电机组能否根据可再生能源出力波动调整其运营。利用法国电力系统的每小时数据，我们发现核电机组的运营相当灵活，并且由于“负荷跟踪”行动（相对于在负荷跟踪事件期间满负荷运行的反事实情况）而损失的发电量目前有限。然而，我们发现，额外的负荷跟踪事件与机组故障概率的轻微增加相关。我们还发现，随着整个系统可再生能源发电量的增加，机组层面的最低出力约束更频繁地具有约束力，尤其是对于最受太阳能发电影响的机组。2024年，当可用核电灵活性耗尽时，对应的小时日前电价为非正值。

No. 126论文详情NBER w34661

Macroeconomic Impacts of Microeconomic Damages in General Equilibrium: Productivity and Capital Losses

一般均衡中微观损害对宏观经济的影响：生产率和资本损失

Marc A. C. Hafstead, Roberton C. Williams III

Abstract

The full economic costs and macroeconomic effects of microeconomic damages associated with pollution damages, climate impacts, and similar negative shocks are not well understood. Beyond the direct damages, market distortions, supply chains, changes in capital and labor costs, etc. can potentially magnify (or diminish) the costs of these shocks. In this paper, we use analytical and numerical general equilibrium models to investigate the channels through which microeconomic shocks affect the macroeconomy. We model different types of shocks, evaluate how anticipation affects the macroeconomic implications of shocks, and measure the overall welfare costs relative to the value of direct damages. We find that preexisting taxes magnify the overall welfare costs relative to direct damages, that savings and investment decisions driven by anticipations of certain types of shocks can interact with tax distortions to lower welfare costs, and that the ratio of welfare cost to direct damages varies substantially across sectors of the economy.

中文摘要

与污染损害、气候影响及类似负面冲击相关的微观损害的全部经济成本和宏观经济效应尚不明确。除了直接损害之外，市场扭曲、供应链、资本和劳动力成本变化等因素可能会放大（或缩小）这些冲击的成本。在本文中，我们使用解析和数值一般均衡模型来研究微观经济冲击影响宏观经济的渠道。我们对不同类型的冲击进行建模，评估预期如何影响冲击的宏观经济含义，并衡量相对于直接损害价值的总体福利成本。我们发现，相对于直接损害，预先存在的税收放大了总体福利成本；由对某些类型冲击的预期驱动的储蓄和投资决策可以与税收扭曲相互作用以降低福利成本；并且福利成本与直接损害的比率在经济各部门之间存在显著差异。

Does LLM Assistance Improve Healthcare Delivery? An Evaluation Using On-site Physicians and Laboratory Tests

大语言模型辅助能否改善医疗服务？基于现场医生和实验室检测的评估

Jason Abaluck, Robert Pless, Nirmal Ravi, Anja Sautmann, Aaron Schwartz

Abstract

We deployed large language model (LLM) decision support for health workers at two outpatient clinics in Nigeria. For each patient, health workers drafted care plans that were optionally revised after LLM feedback. We compared unassisted and assisted plans using blinded randomized assessments by on-site physicians who evaluated and treated the same patients, as well as results from laboratory tests for common conditions. Academic physicians performed blinded retrospective reviews of a subset of notes. In response to LLM feedback, health workers changed their prescribing for more than half of the patients and reported high satisfaction with the recommendations, and retrospective academic reviewers rated LLM-assisted plans more favorably. However, on-site physicians observed little to no improvement in diagnostic alignment or treatment decisions. Laboratory testing showed mixed effects of LLM-assistance, which removed negative tests for malaria but added them for urinary tract infection and anemia, with no significant increase in the detection rates for the tested conditions.

中文摘要

我们在尼日利亚的两家门诊诊所部署了大语言模型（LLM）决策支持系统，供卫生工作者使用。对于每位患者，卫生工作者起草护理计划，并可在收到LLM反馈后选择性地进行修改。我们使用现场医生的盲法随机评估来比较未辅助和辅助的计划，这些医生对同一批患者进行评估和治疗，同时我们还使用了针对常见疾病的实验室检测结果。学术医生对部分病历记录进行了盲法回顾性审查。作为对LLM反馈的回应，卫生工作者改变了超过一半患者的处方，并对建议表示高度满意，回顾性审查的学术评审员对LLM辅助计划的评价也更有利。然而，现场医生观察到诊断一致性或治疗决策几乎没有改善。实验室检测显示LLM辅助的效果不一，它减少了疟疾的阴性检测结果，但增加了尿路感染和贫血的阴性检测结果，且对所检测疾病的检出率没有显著提高。

No. 128论文详情NBER w34659

Dementia and Long-run Trajectories in Household Finances

痴呆症与家庭财务的长期轨迹

Jing Li, Kathleen M. McGarry, Lauren Hersch Nicholas, Jonathan S. Skinner

Abstract

Existing evidence suggests that wealth may decline before dementia onset, but the mechanisms underlying these reductions are poorly understood. Using longitudinal data from the Health and Retirement Study, we compare household finance trajectories for individuals who later develop dementia and those who do not. We find that wealth divergence between the two groups is not explained by reduced earnings, higher healthcare spending, intentional “spend-down” to qualify for Medicaid coverage, state-dependent utility, or reverse causation by which wealth declines cause dementia. Instead, our results point to impaired financial decision-making beginning about six years prior to clinically recognizable dementia.

中文摘要

现有证据表明，财富可能在痴呆症发病前下降，但导致这些减少的机制尚不明确。利用健康与退休研究的纵向数据，我们比较了后来发展为痴呆症和未发展为痴呆症的个体的家庭财务轨迹。我们发现，两组之间的财富差异不能用收入减少、医疗支出增加、为获得医疗补助资格而故意“花光资产”、状态依赖效用或财富下降导致痴呆症的反向因果关系来解释。相反，我们的结果指向在临床可识别的痴呆症发病前约六年开始出现的财务决策能力受损。
