World Trading System For Whom? Evidence from Global Tariffs

世界贸易体系为谁而设？来自全球关税的证据

Rodrigo Adão, John Sturm Becko, Arnaud Costinot, Dave Donaldson

Abstract

We use global tariffs to reveal the weights that nations implicitly place on the welfare of their trading partners relative to their own. Our estimated welfare weights suggest that formal and informal rules of the world trading system make countries internalize the impact of their policies onto others to a substantial extent, though not fully. On average, countries place 25% less value on transfers to foreigners than transfers to their own residents. Across nations, we find that countries that put higher welfare weights on the welfare of foreigners also tend to receive higher weights from them, consistent with a general form of reciprocity among nations. Using our estimated welfare weights, we provide a first look at what countries stand to lose, or gain, from the dissolution of the world trading system as we know it.

中文摘要

我们利用全球关税来揭示各国在自身福利与其贸易伙伴福利之间隐含赋予的权重。我们估算的福利权重表明，世界贸易体系的正式和非正式规则使各国在很大程度上（尽管并非完全）将其政策对他国的影响内部化。平均而言，各国对外国人的转移支付估值比对其本国居民的转移支付低25%。跨国来看，我们发现，那些对他国福利赋予更高福利权重的国家，往往也从对方国家获得更高的权重，这与国家间一种普遍的互惠形式相一致。利用我们估算的福利权重，我们首次揭示了各国在我们所熟知的世界贸易体系解体时可能遭受的损失或获得的收益。

No. 130论文详情NBER w34657

Does Advertising Expand the Market for Hospital Services? Evidence from Medicare

广告是否扩大了医院服务的市场？来自医疗保险的证据

Abby E. Alpert, Atul Gupta, Michael R. Richards, Sarah D. Schutz, Christopher M. Whaley

Abstract

Direct-to-consumer advertising is pervasive in US healthcare markets, but little evidence exists on the effects of advertising by hospitals, second only to drug manufacturers in medical marketing. Advertising may help facilities increase market share by stealing existing patients, expand the market for hospital care, or do both. Regardless, it has important public finance implications due to the large sums of taxpayer funds spent by federal and state governments to subsidize hospital operations and finance care through public insurance programs. This paper provides the first causal evidence, to our knowledge, on the market expansion effects of hospital advertising. To obtain causal estimates, we leverage the fact that spikes in political advertising significantly crowd out hospital advertising in the same market, motivating an instrumental variables design. Using claims data on the universe of Traditional Medicare beneficiaries, we find that advertising expands aggregate patient volume and spending on inpatient care – though to a modest degree (implied elasticities of 0.06 and 0.05, respectively). Although the overall effect of advertising on hospital outpatient care is muted, for-profit hospitals obtain higher outpatient Medicare volume and revenue with greater advertising. Across both care settings, therefore, Medicare spending increases with hospital advertising.

中文摘要

直接面向消费者的广告在美国医疗保健市场中普遍存在，但关于医院广告（其支出在医疗营销中仅次于药品制造商）影响的证据却很少。广告可能通过抢夺现有患者来帮助医疗机构增加市场份额，扩大医院护理市场，或两者兼而有之。无论如何，由于联邦和州政府投入大量纳税人资金补贴医院运营并通过公共保险计划资助医疗服务，广告具有重要的公共财政影响。据我们所知，本文首次提供了关于医院广告市场扩张效应的因果证据。为了获得因果估计，我们利用了政治广告激增会显著挤出同一市场中的医院广告这一事实，从而设计了一个工具变量方法。利用覆盖所有传统医疗保险受益人的索赔数据，我们发现广告扩大了住院患者的总体就诊量和支出——尽管程度不大（隐含弹性分别为0.06和0.05）。尽管广告对医院门诊护理的总体影响较弱，但营利性医院通过增加广告获得了更高的门诊医疗保险就诊量和收入。因此，在两种护理环境中，医疗保险支出都随着医院广告的增加而增加。

No. 131论文详情NBER w34656

Aging and Housing Returns

老龄化与住房回报

Natee Amornsiripanitch, Philip E. Strahan, Song Zhang

Abstract

Older home sellers receive lower returns than younger home sellers. Homes sold by older people have fewer major renovations but higher rates of poor upkeep. Older sellers are also more likely to sell off-MLS (“pocket listings”) and to sell to investors, leading to lower prices. These patterns suggest that older sellers may be disproportionately disadvantaged by agents’ incentive to maximize fees through generating high sales volume instead of maximizing sale prices. Age-related cognitive decline makes the elderly more vulnerable. For causal evidence, we show that reforms making pocket listings more transparent reduced both the prevalence of pocket listings and the magnitude of the age gap in returns.

中文摘要

年长房屋卖家获得的回报低于年轻房屋卖家。老年人出售的房屋进行重大翻新的次数较少，但维护不善的比例更高。年长卖家也更有可能通过非MLS渠道（“口袋挂牌”）出售房屋，并出售给投资者，从而导致价格较低。这些模式表明，年长卖家可能因代理人倾向于通过产生高销售量而非最大化销售价格来最大化费用而处于特别不利的地位。与年龄相关的认知衰退使老年人更加脆弱。作为因果证据，我们表明，使口袋挂牌更加透明的改革既降低了口袋挂牌的普遍性，也缩小了回报中的年龄差距。

No. 132论文详情NBER w34655

The Effects of Pension Reforms on Health Inequality in Italy

养老金改革对意大利健康不平等的影响

Agar Brugiavini, Raluca Elena Buia, Giacomo Pasini, Guglielmo Weber

Abstract

Using data from the Survey on Health, Ageing and Retirement in Europe (SHARE), we explore whether the recent pension reforms enacted in Italy had an impact on the inequality in health among individuals. We construct a set of indexes measuring several health outcomes (both physical and mental) and analyze their evolution along time (across SHARE waves) from 2004 to 2022, by relating them to the households’ income. While we can observe some differences in the health-income gradient between genders, we do not find evidence of a positive relationship between the introduction of the pension reforms and an increase in inequality.

中文摘要

利用欧洲健康、老龄化和退休调查（SHARE）的数据，我们探讨了意大利近期实施的养老金改革是否对个体间的健康不平等产生了影响。我们构建了一组衡量多种健康结果（包括身体和心理健康）的指标，并通过将其与家庭收入相关联，分析了这些指标从2004年到2022年随时间（跨SHARE调查波次）的演变。虽然我们观察到性别之间在健康-收入梯度上存在一些差异，但我们没有发现证据表明养老金改革的引入与不平等加剧之间存在正相关关系。

No. 133论文详情NBER w34654

Fiscal Inaction as Monetary Support

作为货币支持的财政不作为

George-Marios Angeletos, Chen Lian, Christian K. Wolf

Abstract

How does the fiscal framework affect the central bank's ability to stabilize output and inflation? The textbook answer, which assumes Ricardian households, recommends that fiscal adjustment should be fast enough to allow for monetary dominance. We instead argue that, with non-Ricardian households, the central bank may indeed welcome slow, or even no, fiscal adjustment. On the demand side, slow fiscal adjustment helps stabilize aggregate spending; on the supply side, it eases tax distortions, improving the output-inflation trade off. And while the first channel favors slow fiscal adjustment only when the business cycle is dominated by demand shocks, the second channel extends this preference to supply shocks. A quantitative exercise affirms our lessons in the U.S. context, with the central bank preferring virtually no fiscal adjustment over the business cycle.

中文摘要

财政框架如何影响中央银行稳定产出和通胀的能力？教科书式的答案假设李嘉图式家庭，建议财政调整应足够迅速，以实现货币主导。我们反而认为，在存在非李嘉图式家庭的情况下，中央银行可能确实欢迎缓慢甚至不进行财政调整。在需求侧，缓慢的财政调整有助于稳定总支出；在供给侧，它缓解了税收扭曲，改善了产出-通胀权衡。虽然第一个渠道仅在商业周期由需求冲击主导时有利于缓慢的财政调整，但第二个渠道将这种偏好扩展到了供给冲击。一项量化练习在美国背景下证实了我们的结论，即中央银行在商业周期中偏好几乎不进行财政调整。

Digital Incentives in Surveys: Response Rates and Sociodemographic Effects in a Large-Scale Parental Nudge Intervention

调查中的数字激励：大规模家长助推干预中的响应率与社会人口学效应

Kalena Cortes, Brian Holzman, Melissa D. Gentry, Miranda I. Lambert

Abstract

This study examines how digital incentives influence survey participation and engagement in a large randomized controlled trial of parents across six school districts. We test how incentive amount and information about vendor options affect response behavior and explore differences by language background. Incentivized parents were more likely to engage in the program, from starting the survey to choosing an essential-goods gift card. However, Spanish-speaking parents exhibited distinct patterns—greater survey participation rates but lower gift redemption rates. Increasing incentive value and providing advance information both improved engagement. Findings inform the design of equitable, effective digital incentive strategies for diverse populations.

中文摘要

本研究考察了数字激励如何影响一项针对六个学区家长的大规模随机对照试验中的调查参与度和参与度。我们测试了激励金额和关于供应商选项的信息如何影响响应行为，并探讨了不同语言背景下的差异。获得激励的家长更有可能参与该计划，从开始调查到选择必需品礼品卡。然而，讲西班牙语的家长表现出不同的模式——更高的调查参与率但更低的礼品兑换率。增加激励价值和提供预先信息都改善了参与度。研究结果为设计针对不同人群的公平、有效的数字激励策略提供了信息。

Self- and Social Signaling: Evidence from Solar Adoption in California

自我信号与社会信号：来自加州太阳能采用的证据

Bryan K. Bollinger, Kenneth Gillingham, A. Justin Kirkpatrick

Abstract

Prosocial behavior plays a role in many economic contexts, and it has been explained by altruism, social pressure, signaling, and expectations of fairness and reciprocity. We examine prosocial behavior in a context that allows us to distinguish the role of self-signaling and social signaling from alternative explanations, including warm glow. Our context is residential solar, and self-signaling is separately identified from social signaling by the exogenous visibility of potential solar arrays. We show that the political affiliation of proximate peers influences the extent of self-signaling and is crowded out by the private benefits of installing solar.

中文摘要

亲社会行为在许多经济背景下发挥作用，并已被利他主义、社会压力、信号传递以及对公平和互惠的期望所解释。我们在一个能够区分自我信号和社会信号与其他解释（包括温暖光辉）作用的背景下考察亲社会行为。我们的背景是住宅太阳能，自我信号通过潜在太阳能阵列的外生可见性与社会信号区分开来。我们表明，邻近同伴的政治派别影响自我信号的程度，并且被安装太阳能的私人收益所挤出。

The first 1000 days and beyond: The process of child development.

生命最初的1000天及之后：儿童发展的过程

Orazio Attanasio

Abstract

This paper reviews recent developments in the economics of human development, focusing on the early years of life as a critical period for shaping long-term outcomes. Early childhood development is inherently multidimensional: cognitive and socioemotional skills evolve dynamically and interact with health, nutrition, and environmental influences. Economists have contributed to this field by providing a conceptual unifying framework that highlights how key drivers of development reflect the choices of individuals operating under incentives and constraints. Within this framework, the paper emphasizes two central challenges: understanding the interactions among multiple dimensions of development and identifying causal links - particularly the effects of different inputs at different ages. Measurement issues are a recurring theme, given the difficulty of assessing young children and the need for comparability across contexts. The paper also stresses these issues’ policy relevance for poverty reduction and social mobility by discussing early childhood interventions in both developed and developing countries.

中文摘要

本文回顾了人类发展经济学的最新进展，重点关注生命早期作为塑造长期结果的关键时期。儿童早期发展本质上是多维的：认知和社会情感技能动态演变，并与健康、营养和环境影响因素相互作用。经济学家通过提供一个概念性的统一框架为该领域做出了贡献，该框架强调了发展的关键驱动因素如何反映在激励和约束下运作的个体选择。在此框架内，本文强调了两个核心挑战：理解发展多个维度之间的相互作用，以及识别因果联系——特别是不同年龄阶段不同投入的影响。鉴于评估幼儿的困难以及跨背景可比性的需要，测量问题是一个反复出现的主题。本文还通过讨论发达国家和发展中国家的儿童早期干预措施，强调了这些问题对减贫和社会流动性的政策相关性。

What Are the Benefits of Metro Rail in Mumbai, India?

印度孟买地铁的效益是什么？

Palak Suri, Maureen L. Cropper

Abstract

We estimate the effects of the first metro rail line in Mumbai using administrative data on assessed property prices from 2011-18 for 723 subzones in the city. Comparing areas within 1 km of the metro with those beyond 1 km but within 3 km, we estimate the effects on property values for commercial, industrial, and residential properties. We find a significant and persistent increase in prices of 6-8% for residential and commercial land use categories in treated areas relative to control areas after Metro Line 1 opens. We show that commute time savings and improvements in employment accessibility are plausible mechanisms underlying these effects.

中文摘要

我们利用2011-2018年孟买市723个分区评估物业价格的行政数据，估算了该市首条地铁线路的影响。通过比较距地铁1公里以内的区域与距地铁1至3公里以内的区域，我们估算了地铁对商业、工业和住宅物业价值的影响。我们发现，在1号地铁线开通后，相对于控制区域，处理区域内的住宅和商业用地类别的价格出现了显著且持续的6-8%上涨。我们表明，通勤时间节省和就业可达性的改善是这些影响背后的合理机制。

No. 138论文详情NBER w34649

Green Waste

绿色浪费

Ingvil Gaarder, Morten Grindaker, Tom G. Meling, Magne Mogstad

Abstract

We develop and apply a framework to test for and measure green waste: the misallocation of public subsidies for green investment projects. Our context is a major Norwegian subsidy program to reduce carbon emissions. We apply the framework to detailed project-level data on carbon emissions and subsidy amounts for both marginal and inframarginal projects. We find that the decision-maker could have achieved the same level of emission reductions at less than half the cost. To isolate the sources of this green waste, we use data on both ex-ante expected and ex-post realized emission reductions for each project. We find that the decision-maker is able ex-ante to identify the projects with the highest ex-post emission reductions but unwilling to select them.

中文摘要

我们开发并应用了一个框架来检验和衡量绿色浪费：即绿色投资项目公共补贴的错配。我们的研究背景是挪威一个旨在减少碳排放的主要补贴项目。我们将该框架应用于边际项目和边际内项目的碳排放量和补贴金额的详细项目层面数据。我们发现，决策者本可以以不到一半的成本实现同等水平的减排。为了隔离这种绿色浪费的来源，我们使用了每个项目的事前预期减排量和事后实际减排量的数据。我们发现，决策者能够在事前识别出事后减排量最高的项目，但不愿意选择它们。

No. 139论文详情NBER w34648

Bayesian Inference in IV Regressions

IV回归中的贝叶斯推断

Domenico Giannone, Michele Lenza, Giorgio Primiceri

Abstract

It is well known that standard frequentist inference breaks down in IV regressions with weak instruments. Bayesian inference with diffuse priors suffers from the same problem. We show that the issue arises because flat priors on the first-stage coefficients overstate instrument strength. In contrast, inference improves drastically when an uninformative prior is specified directly on the concentration parameter—the key nuisance parameter capturing instrument relevance. The resulting Bayesian credible intervals are asymptotically equivalent to the frequentist confidence intervals based on conditioning approaches, and remain robust to weak instruments.

中文摘要

众所周知，在弱工具变量的IV回归中，标准频率学派推断会失效。具有扩散先验的贝叶斯推断也存在同样的问题。我们表明，问题源于第一阶段系数的平坦先验夸大了工具变量的强度。相比之下，当直接在集中参数（衡量工具变量相关性的关键 nuisance 参数）上指定无信息先验时，推断会得到极大改善。由此产生的贝叶斯可信区间在渐近上等价于基于条件化方法的频率学派置信区间，并且对弱工具变量保持稳健。

No. 140论文详情NBER w34647

The Morality of Market Exchanges: Between Societal Values and Tradeoffs

市场交易的道德：社会价值观与权衡之间

Julio J. Elias, Nicola Lacetera, Mario Macis

Abstract

Certain behaviors in markets are unambiguously unethical. In other cases, however, voluntary exchanges that can create gains from trade remain contested on moral grounds, because of what is traded or of the price at which the exchange occurs. This chapter offers a framework to analyze these contested markets and provides examples of two general instances. First, we examine “repugnant” transactions involving the human body—such as compensated organ donation and gestational surrogacy—where concerns about dignity, exploitation, and inequality conflict with welfare gains from expanding supply. Second, we study price gouging in emergencies, where demands for a “just price” clash with the incentive and allocation roles of price adjustments under scarcity. Across both cases, we synthesize evidence on societal attitudes and highlight how support for policy options depends on perceived trade-offs between autonomy, fairness and efficiency, and on institutional features that can separate compensation from allocation.

中文摘要

市场中的某些行为是明确不道德的。然而，在其他情况下，能够创造交易收益的自愿交换在道德上仍存在争议，争议源于交易的对象或交易发生的价格。本章提供了一个分析这些有争议市场的框架，并提供了两种一般情况的例子。首先，我们研究了涉及人体的“令人反感”的交易——例如有偿器官捐赠和代孕——在这些交易中，关于尊严、剥削和不平等的担忧与扩大供应带来的福利收益相冲突。其次，我们研究了紧急情况下的价格欺诈，在这种情况下，对“公平价格”的要求与稀缺条件下价格调整的激励和分配作用相冲突。在这两种情况下，我们综合了关于社会态度的证据，并强调了政策选项的支持如何取决于对自主、公平和效率之间感知到的权衡，以及取决于能够将补偿与分配分开的制度特征。

No. 141论文详情NBER w34646

Entry and Exit in Treasury Auctions

国债拍卖中的进入与退出

Jason Allen, Ali Hortaçsu, Eric Richert, Milena Wittwer

Abstract

Hedge funds have become increasingly active in Treasury markets, yet we have little evidence on how this shift has affected the market. We focus on the primary market, where the government issues its debt through auctions. Using over 20 years of data from Canadian Treasury auctions, we document dealers exiting and hedge funds entering. To evaluate the costs and benefits of this trend for debt issuance, we develop an auction framework with endogenous participation. We find that the expected gains from greater hedge fund participation, driven by increased competition, are smaller than the costs that arise because hedge funds—unlike dealers—do not participate regularly. Currently, dealer participation remains sufficiently strong that policies aimed at stabilizing participation have little effect on funding costs.

中文摘要

对冲基金在国债市场中变得越来越活跃，然而我们对于这种转变如何影响市场的证据却很少。我们聚焦于一级市场，即政府通过拍卖发行债务的市场。利用加拿大国债拍卖超过20年的数据，我们记录了交易商退出和对冲基金进入的现象。为了评估这一趋势对债务发行的成本和收益，我们开发了一个具有内生参与性的拍卖框架。我们发现，由竞争加剧驱动的对冲基金参与度提高所带来的预期收益，小于因对冲基金（与交易商不同）不规律参与而产生的成本。目前，交易商的参与仍然足够强劲，以至于旨在稳定参与的政策对融资成本影响甚微。

No. 142论文详情NBER w34645

Market Power and Capital Constraints

市场势力与资本约束

Milena Wittwer, Jason Allen

Abstract

We explore how traders' equity capitalization influences asset prices in a framework that accounts for market power. In our model, traders with capital constraints engage in transactions in an imperfectly competitive market. We demonstrate that looser capital constraints elevate both asset prices and price impact, the latter diminishing market liquidity. Using Canadian Treasury auction data, we illustrate how to apply our model to quantify these effects. We estimate the shadow costs of capital constraints by leveraging a temporary policy exemption during 2020-2021. We show that while these constraints are only infrequently binding, their relative impact when activated can be sizable.

中文摘要

我们探讨了交易者的股权资本化如何在一个考虑市场势力的框架中影响资产价格。在我们的模型中，面临资本约束的交易者在一个不完全竞争的市场中进行交易。我们证明，放松资本约束会同时提高资产价格和价格冲击，后者会降低市场流动性。利用加拿大国债拍卖数据，我们说明了如何应用我们的模型来量化这些效应。我们利用2020-2021年期间一项临时政策豁免来估计资本约束的影子成本。我们表明，虽然这些约束只是偶尔具有约束力，但它们在激活时的相对影响可能相当大。

No. 143论文详情NBER w34644

Renewable Energy Expansion: Key Challenges and Emerging Opportunities

可再生能源扩张：关键挑战与新兴机遇

Koichiro Ito

Abstract

The global expansion of renewable energy is key to addressing climate change. After a decade of dramatic cost reductions—especially for solar photovoltaics and wind—renewables now approach cost parity with fossil generation. While this cost reduction has led to a steep increase in solar and wind power in several countries, the global share of solar and wind generation remains modest—approximately 15% as of 2023. This article reviews recent economic studies and identifies three central challenges and corresponding opportunities for scaling up renewable energy—underdeveloped regulatory and market design, insufficient intertemporal market integration, and inadequate spatial market integration. The insights from this review highlight effective ways to accelerate the global transition to renewable energy.

中文摘要

全球可再生能源的扩张是应对气候变化的关键。在经历了十年（尤其是太阳能光伏和风能）的成本急剧下降之后，可再生能源现在已接近与化石能源发电的成本平价。虽然这种成本下降导致一些国家的太阳能和风能发电量急剧增加，但全球太阳能和风能发电的份额仍然不大——截至2023年约为15%。本文回顾了近期经济学研究，并指出了扩大可再生能源规模的三个核心挑战及相应的机遇——不完善的监管和市场设计、跨期市场整合不足以及空间市场整合不足。本综述的见解强调了加速全球向可再生能源转型的有效途径。

Ruling for the Rich: the Supreme Court over Time

为富人裁决：最高法院的变迁

Andrea Prat, Fiona Scott Morton, Jacob Spitz

Abstract

To investigate the emergence of a pro-wealthy bias in the US Supreme Court, we develop a protocol to identify and analyze all cases involving economic issues from 1953 to the present. We categorize the parties in these cases as “rich” or “poor” according to their likelihood of being wealthy. A vote is pro-rich if that outcome would directly shift resources to the party that is more likely to be wealthy. Using this dataset, we estimate case-specific intercepts, justice-specific latent ideal points, and party-level time trends using the Bayesian methods pioneered by Martin and Quinn (2002). In the 1950s, justices appointed by the two parties appear similar in their propensity to cast pro-rich votes. Over the sample period, we estimate a steady increase in polarization, culminating in an implied party gap of 47 percentage points by 2022. The magnitude of the gap suggests the usefulness of an economic metric for prediction relative to ideologies such as originalism or textualism.

中文摘要

为了调查美国最高法院中亲富偏见的出现，我们开发了一个协议来识别和分析从1953年至今所有涉及经济问题的案件。我们根据这些案件中的当事人成为富人的可能性，将其分类为“富人”或“穷人”。如果某个投票结果会直接将资源转移给更可能富有的当事人，则该投票被视为亲富。利用这个数据集，我们使用Martin和Quinn（2002）开创的贝叶斯方法，估计了案件特定的截距项、大法官特定的潜在理想点以及当事人层面的时间趋势。在20世纪50年代，两党任命的大法官在做出亲富投票的倾向性上看起来相似。在整个样本期内，我们估计出极化程度稳步上升，最终到2022年隐含的党派差距达到47个百分点。这一差距的幅度表明，相对于原旨主义或文本主义等意识形态，经济指标在预测方面具有实用性。

From Treatment to Safety: The Role of Substance Use Treatment in Preventing Intimate Partner Violence

从治疗到安全：物质使用治疗在预防亲密伴侣暴力中的作用

Mevlude Akbulut-Yuksel, Dhaval M. Dave, Bilge Erten, Pinar Keskin, Catarina R. Meneses

Abstract

Substance use is a well-established driver of intimate partner violence (IPV), with drug-related incidents posing persistent challenges for both public health and criminal justice systems. We examine how expanding access to substance use treatment (SUT) services affects IPV in the United States by leveraging variation in the opening and closing of treatment facilities at the county level. Using administrative data on IPV incidents from the National Incident-Based Reporting System at the agency level from 1998 to 2019 combined with county-level records on treatment facility information, we implement a continuous difference-in-differences research design. Our results show that adding three SUT facilities—the average annual increase per county over the sample period—reduces drug-involved IPV by about 1.5–1.7 percent. We find no evidence of significant effects on alcohol-related or non-substance-related IPV. Staggered event-study analyses confirm parallel outcome trends, across treated and non-treated counties, prior to net facility openings and lend support to a causal interpretation of the estimates. Related evidence from SUT admissions drawn from the Treatment Episode Data Set (TEDS) shows that new centers significantly raise treatment entry, particularly among men, consistent with reduced perpetration driving the observed decline in IPV exposure. Our findings highlight the role of health services infrastructure in shaping violence-related outcomes and underscore the broader public safety benefits of investment in treatment access.

中文摘要

物质使用是亲密伴侣暴力（IPV）的一个公认驱动因素，与毒品相关的事件给公共卫生和刑事司法系统都带来了持续的挑战。我们利用县级治疗设施开放和关闭的变化，研究了扩大物质使用治疗（SUT）服务获取对美国IPV的影响。我们使用1998年至2019年来自国家基于事件的报告系统（NIBRS）的机构层面IPV事件行政数据，结合县级治疗设施信息记录，实施了一个连续的双重差分研究设计。我们的结果显示，增加三个SUT设施——样本期间每个县的平均年增长量——会使涉及毒品的IPV减少约1.5-1.7%。我们没有发现对与酒精相关或与物质无关的IPV有显著影响的证据。交错事件研究分析证实，在净设施开放之前，处理县和未处理县的结果趋势是平行的，这支持了对估计结果的因果解释。来自治疗事件数据集（TEDS）的SUT入院相关证据显示，新中心显著提高了治疗入院率，尤其是在男性中，这与犯罪率降低导致观察到的IPV暴露下降是一致的。我们的发现强调了卫生服务基础设施在塑造暴力相关结果中的作用，并强调了投资于治疗获取所带来的更广泛的公共安全效益。

No. 146论文详情NBER w34641

Valuing Sticky Deposits

评估粘性存款的价值

Matthias Fleckenstein, Shohini Kundu, Francis A. Longstaff

Abstract

We develop a formal fixed-income framework to value sticky deposits. This framework provides closed-form expressions for deposit values and allows us to study the impact of stickiness on deposit interest-rate and runoff risks. The duration of a bank deposit can be either positive or negative, which has important implications for hedging the interest-rate risk of bank balance sheets. Banks that maximize deposit value by following optimal deposit beta strategies may significantly increase their interest-rate and deposit runoff risks. We test the empirical implications of the valuation model using market deposit premia observed in bank merger/acquisition transactions. The results provide strong empirical support for the model’s predictions.

中文摘要

我们开发了一个正式的固定收益框架来评估粘性存款的价值。该框架为存款价值提供了封闭形式的表达式，并使我们能够研究粘性对存款利率和流失风险的影响。银行存款的久期可以是正的也可以是负的，这对对冲银行资产负债表的利率风险具有重要意义。通过遵循最优存款贝塔策略来最大化存款价值的银行，可能会显著增加其利率和存款流失风险。我们使用在银行并购交易中观察到的市场存款溢价来检验该估值模型的实证含义。结果为模型的预测提供了强有力的实证支持。

Tariff War Shock and the Convenience Yield of US Treasuries — A Hedging Perspective

关税战冲击与美国国债的便利收益——一个对冲视角

Viral V. Acharya, Toomas Laarits

Abstract

We explain how the “Tariff War” shock of April 2025 affected the safe-asset status of US Treasuries. Convenience yield erosion for long bonds is consistent with a reduction in the hedging property, reflected in a rising stock-bond covariance. Decomposing the Treasury yield into risk-free rate, credit spread, and convenience yield components reveals that covariance due to the convenience yield component increased for long bonds. The short end of the Treasury curve, however, continued to exhibit the safe-asset hedging property. These effects are consistent with a withdrawal of safe-asset investors from long-term Treasuries and a rotation towards shorter-term Treasuries and gold.

中文摘要

我们解释了2025年4月的“关税战”冲击如何影响美国国债的安全资产地位。长期债券便利收益的侵蚀与对冲属性的降低是一致的，这反映在股票-债券协方差的上升上。将美国国债收益率分解为无风险利率、信用利差和便利收益组成部分，结果显示，长期债券的便利收益组成部分导致的协方差增加了。然而，美国国债收益率曲线的短端继续表现出安全资产的对冲属性。这些效应与安全资产投资者从长期美国国债撤出并转向较短期限美国国债和黄金是一致的。

No. 148论文详情NBER w34639

O-Ring Automation

O型环自动化

Joshua S. Gans, Avi Goldfarb

Abstract

We study automation when tasks are quality complements rather than separable. Production requires numerous tasks whose qualities multiply as in an O-ring technology. A worker allocates a fixed endowment of time across the tasks performed; machines can replace tasks with given quality, and time is allocated across the remaining manual tasks. This “focus” mechanism generates three results. First, task-by-task substitution logic is incomplete because automating one task changes the return to automating others. Second, automation decisions are discrete and can require bundled adoption even when automation quality improves smoothly. Third, labour income can rise under partial automation because automation scales the value of remaining bottleneck tasks. These results imply that widely-used exposure indices, which aggregate task-level automation risk using linear formulas, will overstate displacement when tasks are complements. The relevant object is not average task exposure but the structure of bottlenecks and how automation reshapes worker time around them.

中文摘要

我们研究了当任务在质量上是互补的而非可分离时的自动化问题。生产需要大量任务，这些任务的质量像O型环技术一样相乘。一个工人将其固定的时间禀赋分配给所执行的任务；机器可以以给定的质量替代任务，而时间则分配给剩余的体力任务。这种“聚焦”机制产生了三个结果。首先，逐任务替代逻辑是不完整的，因为自动化一个任务会改变自动化其他任务的回报。其次，即使自动化质量平滑改善，自动化决策也是离散的，并且可能需要捆绑采用。第三，在部分自动化下，劳动收入可以上升，因为自动化放大了剩余瓶颈任务的价值。这些结果表明，当任务是互补的时，广泛使用的、使用线性公式聚合任务层面自动化风险的暴露指数，会高估替代效应。相关的对象不是平均任务暴露，而是瓶颈的结构以及自动化如何围绕瓶颈重塑工人的时间。

No. 149论文详情NBER w34638

Biases in Belief Updating Within and Across Domains

领域内和跨领域的信念更新偏差

Francesca Bastianello, Alex Imas

Abstract

Why do people sometimes overreact to new information and other times underreact? We develop a model in which the strength of a signal—how much one should update their beliefs with new information—depends on multiple features of the information environment. Limited attention to these features leads to misperceptions of signal strength: people approach a problem with an experience-based prior, which they adjust only partially based on how much attention they pay to different features. This mechanism explains a wide range of belief-updating patterns. Insensitivity to a single feature generates underreaction to strong and overreaction to weak signals, and more neglected features amplify this. Insensitivity to multiple features can instead break that pattern: insensitivity to one feature can generate excess sensitivity with respect to another, leading to overreaction to both weak and strong signals. A series of experiments provides support for the model and its underlying mechanism.

中文摘要

为什么人们有时对新信息反应过度，有时又反应不足？我们开发了一个模型，其中信号的强度——即一个人应该根据新信息更新其信念的程度——取决于信息环境的多个特征。对这些特征的有限关注导致了对信号强度的错误感知：人们带着基于经验的先验来处理问题，并根据他们对不同特征的关注程度仅部分调整该先验。这种机制解释了广泛的信念更新模式。对单一特征的不敏感会导致对强信号反应不足和对弱信号反应过度，而更多被忽视的特征会放大这种效应。对多个特征的不敏感反而可能打破这种模式：对一个特征的不敏感可能会产生对另一个特征的过度敏感，导致对弱信号和强信号都反应过度。一系列实验为该模型及其潜在机制提供了支持。

No. 150论文详情NBER w34637

Making Entrepreneurs: Long Term Returns to Training Youth in Business Skills

培养企业家：对青年进行商业技能培训的长期回报

Laura Chioda, Paul Gertler, David Contreras-Loya, Dana R. Carney

Abstract

We study the medium and long term impacts of Skills for Effective Entrepreneurship Development (SEED), a 3-week entrepreneurship training program for secondary school students in Uganda. The mini-MBA, modeled after business school curricula, was implemented as a randomized field experiment with a nationally representative sample of 4,402 youth. After four years, the training improved both hard and soft skills. SEED graduates became more effective negotiators and communicators and exhibited improved self-efficacy, stability, plasticity, and stress management. In the medium run, treated youth were more likely to start enterprises and more successful in ensuring their survival, thereby gaining greater entrepreneurial experience. Their ventures were also of higher quality: more likely to be formal, have employees, be in collaboration with other entrepreneurs, and use effective business management practices. With 52% of the sample still enrolled in post-secondary education, we find suggestive evidence that businesses led by the treatment groups performed better. After nine years, business ownership converged between treatment and control groups as control ownership rates doubled. However, SEED graduates maintained their edge in terms of business quality and operated firms with 20% higher revenues and 16% higher profits, without corresponding increases in capital or labor inputs, consistent with higher total factor productivity. Entrepreneurial success was achieved through the adoption of better business practices and experimentation, with soft skills related to entrepreneurial mindset playing a complementary role. SEED generated high returns on investment: the present discounted values of SEED-induced business and total earnings equal 20 and 27 times program costs, respectively.

中文摘要

我们研究了有效创业发展技能（SEED）项目的中长期影响，这是一个针对乌干达中学生的为期三周的创业培训项目。这个迷你MBA，模仿商学院课程设计，作为一个随机实地实验实施，样本为4402名具有全国代表性的青年。四年后，培训提高了硬技能和软技能。SEED毕业生成为更有效的谈判者和沟通者，并表现出自我效能感、稳定性、可塑性和压力管理的改善。在中期，接受过培训的青年更有可能创办企业，并且在确保企业生存方面更成功，从而获得了更多的创业经验。他们的企业质量也更高：更可能是正规企业、有雇员、与其他企业家合作，并采用有效的企业管理实践。由于52%的样本仍在接受高等教育，我们发现有提示性证据表明，由处理组领导的企业表现更好。九年后，随着控制组创业率翻倍，处理组和控制组的企业所有权趋于一致。然而，SEED毕业生在企业质量方面保持了优势，其运营的企业收入高出20%，利润高出16%，而资本或劳动投入没有相应增加，这与更高的全要素生产率一致。创业成功是通过采用更好的商业实践和实验实现的，与创业心态相关的软技能发挥了补充作用。SEED产生了高投资回报：SEED带来的企业和总收入的现值分别是项目成本的20倍和27倍。

GIFfluence: A Visual Approach to Investor Sentiment and the Stock Market

Ming Gu, David Hirshleifer, Siew Hong Teoh, Shijia Wu

Abstract

We study dynamic visual representations as a proxy for investor sentiment about the stock market. Our sentiment index, GIFsentiment, is constructed from millions of posts in the Graphics Interchange Format (GIF) on a leading investment social media platform. GIFsentiment correlates with seasonal mood variations and the severity of COVID lockdowns. These effects are stronger among portfolios that are more susceptible to mispricing. GIFsentiment positively predicts trading volume, market volatility, and flows toward equity funds and away from debt funds. Our evidence suggests that GIFsentiment is a proxy for misperceptions that are later corrected.

No. 152论文详情NBER w34635

Family Spillovers of Dementia

痴呆症的家庭溢出效应

Onur Altındağ, Jane Greve, Yulya Truskinovsky

Abstract

We use population-wide administrative data from Denmark and an event-study design spanning nearly two decades to examine the impact of having a parent with dementia on adult children’s labor market, physical health, and mental health outcomes. We find no meaningful effects on labor supply, earnings, or physical health care use. In contrast, mental health care use increases substantially, driven by daughters, beginning five years before a parent’s dementia-related death, peaking around the time of death, and converging to the counterfactual trend over seven years. Results suggest that robust long-term care policy can largely insulate adult children economically from parental dementia, but mental health spillovers persist, spurring nearly a decade of elevated use.

中文摘要

我们使用丹麦的全人口行政数据和一个跨越近二十年的事件研究设计，来检验父母患有痴呆症对成年子女的劳动力市场、身体健康和心理健康结果的影响。我们发现对劳动力供给、收入或身体健康护理使用没有显著影响。相比之下，心理健康护理使用大幅增加，主要由女儿驱动，从父母因痴呆症去世前五年开始，在去世前后达到峰值，并在七年内收敛到反事实趋势。结果表明，稳健的长期护理政策可以在经济上很大程度上保护成年子女免受父母痴呆症的影响，但心理健康溢出效应持续存在，引发了近十年的使用率升高。

No. 153论文详情NBER w34634

The Incredible Shrinking Instruments: Using Empirical Bayes to Increase Efficiency in IV Designs with Many Instruments

缩小的工具：利用经验贝叶斯方法提高多工具变量IV设计的效率

Brigham R. Frandsen, Lars J. Lefgren, Emily C. Leslie, Samuel P. McIntyre

Abstract

In instrumental variables (IV) estimation with many instruments, such as judge fixed effects designs, the precision of the jackknife-estimated first stage can vary widely across observations. When such variability exists, we show that the precision of JIVE second-stage estimates is meaningfully improved by shrinking judge propensities towards their conditional means, where the shrinkage factor depends on the precision of the first-stage fitted value. Doing so requires no further assumptions and identifies the same local average treatment effect as the usual (unshrunken) JIVE estimator. We illustrate the precision gains from using a Shrunken JIVE estimator (SJIVE) in an application from the literature studying pre-trial detention of defendants in criminal cases.

中文摘要

在具有多个工具变量的工具变量（IV）估计中，例如法官固定效应设计，刀切法估计的第一阶段的精度在不同观测值之间可能存在很大差异。我们表明，当存在这种变异性时，通过将法官倾向性向其条件均值收缩（收缩因子取决于第一阶段拟合值的精度），可以显著提高JIVE第二阶段估计的精度。这样做不需要额外的假设，并且识别出与通常的（未收缩的）JIVE估计量相同的局部平均处理效应。我们通过一个研究刑事案件中被告审前羁押的文献应用，说明了使用收缩JIVE估计量（SJIVE）带来的精度提升。

No. 154论文详情NBER w34633

Unwilling to Reskill? Experimental Evidence from Real-World Jobseekers

不愿再培训？来自真实世界求职者的实验证据

Alexia Delfino, Andrea Garnero, Sergio Inferrera, Marco Leonardi, Raffaella Sadun

Abstract

We study barriers preventing jobseekers from pursuing reskilling in high-demand occupations. Using a discrete choice experiment, we quantify the demand for reskilling among Italian jobseekers in two white-collar high-demand occupations—information technology assistant and construction technician—and identify its main determinants. Willingness to pay estimates show that participants are willing to pay to reskill into IT, but would require compensation to reskill into construction. Beliefs about monetary returns and social status help explain differences in reskilling demand, but perceived identity fit in the target occupation emerges as the most important individual-level factor shaping reskilling decisions. A light-touch randomized information intervention providing data on occupational returns significantly increases both stated interest in reskilling and actual engagement in real-world training.

中文摘要

我们研究了阻碍求职者追求高需求职业再培训的障碍。通过一个离散选择实验，我们量化了意大利求职者对两种白领高需求职业——信息技术助理和建筑技术员——的再培训需求，并识别了其主要决定因素。支付意愿估计显示，参与者愿意为再培训进入IT领域付费，但需要补偿才愿意再培训进入建筑领域。关于货币回报和社会地位的信念有助于解释再培训需求的差异，但目标职业的感知身份契合度成为影响再培训决策的最重要的个体层面因素。一项提供职业回报数据的轻触式随机信息干预显著增加了对再培训的陈述兴趣以及参与真实世界培训的实际行为。

No. 155论文详情NBER w34632

How Monetary Policy Is Made: Lessons from Historical FOMC Discussions

货币政策是如何制定的：来自历史FOMC讨论的教训

Cooper Howes, Marc Dordal i Carreras, Olivier Coibion, Yuriy Gorodnichenko

Abstract

We construct a new dataset of FOMC meeting transcripts from 1966 to 1990 to analyze the sources of heterogeneity in individual monetary policy preferences and study how this heterogeneity shapes policy decisions. Using these detailed discussions, we manually quantify and characterize each FOMC participants’ preferred policies along with their reasoning and justification. We show that participants' beliefs about the effects of monetary policy—specifically, their perceived slope of the Phillips Curve—play a central role. Participants who believe monetary policy has stronger effects on real activity are more likely to cite output as a justification for easing, while those perceiving stronger price effects emphasize inflation as a reason for tightening. We then show that the Chair plays a unique and powerful role in reconciling these views, not just in setting policy rates, but also in minimizing dissent. The latter occurs because dissenters find their ability to influence policy in subsequent meetings is significantly curtailed.

中文摘要

我们构建了一个1966年至1990年FOMC会议记录的新数据集，以分析个人货币政策偏好的异质性来源，并研究这种异质性如何影响政策决策。利用这些详细的讨论，我们手动量化并描述了每位FOMC参与者的首选政策及其理由和依据。我们表明，参与者对货币政策效果的信念——具体来说，他们感知到的菲利普斯曲线斜率——起着核心作用。认为货币政策对实际活动影响更强的参与者更可能将产出作为宽松政策的理由，而认为价格效应更强的参与者则强调通胀是紧缩政策的理由。然后我们表明，主席在协调这些观点方面发挥着独特而强大的作用，不仅体现在设定政策利率上，还体现在最小化异议上。后者之所以发生，是因为异议者发现他们在后续会议中影响政策的能力显著受限。

No. 156论文详情NBER w34631

Payment-Chain Crises

支付链危机

Saki Bigio, Esteban Méndez, Diana Van Patten

Abstract

This paper introduces an endogenous network of payment chains into a business cycle model. Motivated by evidence of linked payments across firms in Costa Rica, we develop a framework where production orders form bilateral relations: some payments are executed immediately, while others---chained payments---are delayed until upstream payments are received. These chains capture real-world situations in which firms must wait to be paid before paying their own suppliers, leaving resources temporarily idle even when demand and capacity exist. In equilibrium, agents choose the amount of chained payments given interest rates and access to internal funds or credit lines. This choice determines the payment-chain network and aggregate total-factor productivity (TFP). The paper characterizes equilibrium dynamics and pecuniary externalities when agents internalize their own payment delays but not the delays imposed on others.

中文摘要

本文将内生支付链网络引入商业周期模型。受哥斯达黎加企业间关联支付证据的启发，我们构建了一个框架，其中生产订单形成双边关系：一些支付立即执行，而其他支付——链式支付——则延迟到上游支付收到后才进行。这些链条捕捉了现实世界中的情况，即企业必须等待被付款后才能支付自己的供应商，即使存在需求和产能，资源也会暂时闲置。在均衡状态下，代理人根据利率以及内部资金或信贷额度的可获得性选择链式支付的数量。这一选择决定了支付链网络和全要素生产率（TFP）。本文刻画了当代理人内部化自身支付延迟但未考虑强加给其他人的延迟时的均衡动态和货币外部性。

No. 157论文详情NBER w34630

The Labor Market Return to Permanent Residency

永久居留权的劳动力市场回报

Kory Kroft, Isaac Norwich, Matthew J. Notowidigdo, Stephen Tino

Abstract

A central question in immigration policy is how mobility restrictions affect the wages of temporary foreign workers (TFWs). We study the labor market return to TFWs gaining permanent residency (PR), which loosens mobility restrictions. Using administrative data linking matched employer-employee data in Canada to temporary and permanent visa records from 2004–2014 along with an event-study design, we find that gaining PR leads to a sharp, immediate, and persistent increase in the job switching rate of 21.7 percentage points and an increase in earnings of 3.2 percent three years after PR. These gains are driven primarily by reallocation across firms: workers move to higher-paying firms, and our estimates are consistent with no within-firm effects. To guide and interpret our reduced-form results, we develop a search-and-matching model featuring heterogeneous workers and firms. Permanent residents and native-born workers search for jobs in the same labor market and engage in on-the-job search, while TFWs search separately within a segmented labor market and do not receive outside wage offers. We calibrate the model to match our reduced-form results, and we use it to simulate the long-run effects of PR and consider two counterfactual policies: (1) increasing the cost to firms of posting a TFW vacancy and (2) allowing TFWs to switch employers freely under “open” visas. We evaluate how these policies affect output, wages, profits, and overall social welfare.

中文摘要

移民政策的一个核心问题是，流动性限制如何影响临时外国工人（TFW）的工资。我们研究了TFW获得永久居留权（PR）后的劳动力市场回报，这放松了流动性限制。利用2004-2014年加拿大匹配的雇主-雇员数据与临时和永久签证记录的管理数据，并结合事件研究设计，我们发现获得PR导致跳槽率急剧、立即且持续地增加21.7个百分点，并在获得PR三年后收入增加3.2%。这些收益主要由跨企业重新配置驱动：工人流向支付更高工资的企业，我们的估计与无企业内部效应一致。为了指导并解释我们的简化形式结果，我们构建了一个包含异质性工人和企业的搜索匹配模型。永久居民和本土工人在同一劳动力市场中搜索工作并进行在职搜索，而TFW则在分割的劳动力市场中单独搜索，且不接收外部工资报价。我们校准模型以匹配我们的简化形式结果，并用其模拟PR的长期效应，同时考虑两种反事实政策：（1）增加企业发布TFW职位空缺的成本；（2）允许TFW在“开放”签证下自由更换雇主。我们评估这些政策如何影响产出、工资、利润和整体社会福利。

No. 158论文详情NBER w34629

Why Care About Debt-to-GDP?

为何关心债务与GDP之比？

Jonathan B. Berk, Jules H. van Binsbergen

Abstract

We construct an international panel data set comprising three distinct yet plausible measures of government indebtedness: the debt-to-GDP, the interest-to-GDP, and the debt-to-equity ratios. Our analysis reveals that these measures yield differing conclusions about recent trends in government indebtedness. While the debt-to-GDP ratio has reached historically high levels, the other two indicators show either no clear trend or a declining pattern over recent decades. We argue for the development of stronger theoretical foundations for the measures employed in the literature, suggesting that, without such grounding, assertions about debt (un)sustainability may be premature.

中文摘要

我们构建了一个国际面板数据集，包含三种不同但合理的政府负债衡量指标：债务与GDP之比、利息与GDP之比以及债务与权益之比。我们的分析表明，这些指标对近期政府负债趋势得出了不同的结论。虽然债务与GDP之比已达到历史高位，但其他两个指标在过去几十年中要么没有明显趋势，要么呈下降模式。我们主张为文献中使用的衡量指标建立更强的理论基础，并认为，如果没有这样的基础，关于债务（不可）持续性的断言可能为时过早。

No. 159论文详情NBER w34628

A Unified Theory of Delegated Capital Management

委托资本管理的统一理论

Jonathan B. Berk, Peter M. DeMarzo

Abstract

We develop a unified theory of delegated capital management by extending the paradigm of Berk and Green (2004) from mutual funds to alternative assets. With competitive markets and rational investors, we derive the optimal contract and account for observed regularities --- performance fees, persistent alpha, and limits on capital. The key distinction between mutual funds and alternatives is the liquidity of the underlying assets. When assets are illiquid, it is optimal to acquire information about the manager's skill. A positive alpha is therefore necessary to compensate informed investors and a performance based contract is required to induce these investors to allocate their capital optimally. At the same time, a free-rider problem emerges that requires capital constraints on uninformed investors. Thus, liquidity of the underlying assets explains the contrasting contract structures across sectors.

中文摘要

我们通过将Berk和Green（2004）的范式从共同基金扩展到另类资产，发展了一个委托资本管理的统一理论。在竞争性市场和理性投资者的条件下，我们推导出最优契约，并解释了观察到的规律——业绩费、持续的超额收益和资本限制。共同基金与另类资产之间的关键区别在于基础资产的流动性。当资产非流动性时，获取关于管理者技能的信息是最优的。因此，正的阿尔法对于补偿知情投资者是必要的，而基于业绩的契约则是诱导这些投资者最优配置其资本所必需的。同时，出现了一个搭便车问题，需要对不知情投资者施加资本约束。因此，基础资产的流动性解释了不同行业间契约结构的差异。

No. 160论文详情NBER w34627

Global Ripple Effects of Corporate Tax Reforms

公司税改革的全球涟漪效应

Sebastian Dyrda, Guangbin Hong, Muhammad Ali Sajid, Joseph B. Steinberg

Abstract

We study international spillovers of corporate tax reforms in a fragmented global tax regime. Using firm-level evidence on the 2017 U.S. Tax Cuts and Jobs Act (TCJA) and a quantitative general-equilibrium model, we illustrate how multinational enterprises (MNEs) propagate local policy shocks throughout the global economy. Our framework emphasizes two key intrinsic properties of intangible capital: non-rivalry and mobile ownership. We find the TCJA generated positive outward spillovers: First, it boosted U.S. MNEs’ intangible investment, raising their foreign subsidiaries’ output. Second, it increased tangible investment of foreign MNEs’ U.S. subsidiaries, incentivizing them to expand intangible investment at home. Conversely, a Global Minimum Tax (GMT) implemented by the rest of the world generates negative inward spillovers for the United States, even if U.S.-parented MNEs are exempt. These findings illustrate that there is no such thing as a purely domestic corporate tax policy.

中文摘要

我们研究了碎片化全球税收制度下公司税改革的国际溢出效应。利用关于2017年美国《减税与就业法案》（TCJA）的企业层面证据以及一个定量一般均衡模型，我们说明了跨国企业（MNE）如何将地方政策冲击传播到全球经济。我们的框架强调了无形资本的两种关键内在属性：非竞争性和所有权可移动性。我们发现TCJA产生了正向的向外溢出效应：首先，它促进了美国跨国公司的无形资产投资，提高了其外国子公司的产出。其次，它增加了外国跨国公司美国子公司的有形资产投资，激励它们扩大在本国的无形资产投资。相反，世界其他地区实施的全球最低税（GMT）对美国产生了负向的向内溢出效应，即使美国母公司旗下的跨国公司被豁免。这些发现表明，不存在纯粹国内的公司税政策。

No. 161论文详情NBER w34626

The Ins & Outs of Chinese Monetary Policy Transmission

中国货币政策传导的“内”与“外”

Silvia Miranda-Agrippino, Tsvetelina Nenova, Hélène Rey

Abstract

Using a novel indicator for the People's Bank of China monetary policy stance, we estimate a policy rule that accounts for the dual nature of its price stability mandate—encompassing domestic inflation and the exchange rate—and for the evolution of its operational framework. The “Ins”: The domestic transmission follows textbook patterns, with exceptions due to the active management of the renminbi and the financial account. The "Outs": International spillovers are powerful and affect commodity markets, global production and trade. The pass-through to foreign (US) prices is substantial. Financial spillovers are second-order, and mostly derivative from trade spillovers.

中文摘要

利用一个衡量中国人民银行货币政策立场的新指标，我们估计了一条政策规则，该规则考虑了其价格稳定目标的双重性质——涵盖国内通胀和汇率——以及其操作框架的演变。“内部”：国内传导遵循教科书模式，但由于人民币和金融账户的积极管理而存在例外。“外部”：国际溢出效应强劲，并影响大宗商品市场、全球生产和贸易。向外国（美国）价格的传导是实质性的。金融溢出效应是二阶的，且主要源于贸易溢出效应。

No. 162论文详情NBER w34625

Employment Impacts of the CHIPS Act

《芯片法案》的就业影响

Bilge Erten, Joseph E. Stiglitz, Eric Verhoogen

Abstract

The CHIPS and Science Act, enacted in August 2022, is a key element of the revival of U.S. industrial policy. We examine the short-term employment effects of the act. Drawing on quarterly industry-by-county data from the Quarterly Census of Employment and Wages (QCEW), we implement two county-level difference-in-difference designs, the first comparing counties with pre-existing semiconductor facilities to other counties with high-tech industries and the second comparing counties with semiconductor fabrication facilities (which were targeted for the bulk of the CHIPS funding) to counties with non-fabrication semiconductor facilities. Using both approaches, we find robust, positive employment impacts in affected counties. The effects began at the time of the passage in the Senate of a precursor bill, in anticipation of the signing of the CHIPS Act. Our preferred estimates suggest an increase of 110 jobs per affected county in the first design and 180 jobs per affected county in the second design. We also find robust positive impacts on local construction employment. Evidence on total employment and GDP at the county level, as well as on employment in upstream input sectors, is mixed. Simple back-of-the-envelope calculations (which come with caveats) suggest national direct employment effects of approximately 15,000-16,000 jobs in the core semiconductor sector and indirect effects of 15,000-30,000 jobs in related sectors.

中文摘要

2022年8月颁布的《芯片与科学法案》是美国产业政策复兴的关键要素。我们考察了该法案的短期就业效应。利用来自《季度就业与工资普查》（QCEW）的季度行业-县数据，我们实施了两种县级双重差分设计，第一种是比较拥有现有半导体设施的县与其他拥有高科技产业的县，第二种是比较拥有半导体制造设施（这些设施是《芯片法案》大部分资金的目标）的县与拥有非制造类半导体设施的县。使用这两种方法，我们发现在受影响的县中，就业影响稳健且为正。这些效应始于参议院通过一项前身法案之时，早于《芯片法案》的签署。我们的首选估计表明，在第一种设计中，每个受影响的县增加了110个工作岗位，在第二种设计中，每个受影响的县增加了180个工作岗位。我们还发现对当地建筑就业有稳健的正向影响。关于县级总就业和GDP，以及上游投入部门就业的证据则喜忧参半。简单的粗略计算（附带说明）表明，核心半导体部门的全国直接就业效应约为15,000-16,000个工作岗位，相关部门的间接效应为15,000-30,000个工作岗位。

No. 163论文详情NBER w34624

The Effects of Regulating Greenwashing: Evidence from Europe’s Sustainable Finance Disclosure Regulation (SFDR)

监管“漂绿”的效果：来自欧洲《可持续金融披露条例》（SFDR）的证据

Hunt Allcott, Mark L. Egan, Paul Smeets, Hanbin Yang

Abstract

We examine the impact of the European Union’s Sustainable Finance Disclosure Regulation (SFDR) on mutual fund flows and investment sustainability. The SFDR classifies funds into three categories to promote transparency and curb greenwashing: those with a sustainable investment objective (Article 9 or “dark green”), those that promote environmental characteristics (Article 8 or “light green”), and others (Article 6). Using a difference-in-differences design, we find that the SFDR had little effect on fund flows or portfolio sustainability. The disclosures were ineffective in part because they offered little new or clear information beyond what investors could already infer from fund names and mandates. In an experimental setting, we show that the current disclosures have minimal impact on investor decisions, but making the information more intuitive could improve the regulation’s effectiveness.

中文摘要

我们考察了欧盟《可持续金融披露条例》（SFDR）对共同基金资金流和投资可持续性的影响。SFDR将基金分为三类以促进透明度并遏制“漂绿”：具有可持续投资目标的基金（第9条或“深绿色”）、推广环境特征的基金（第8条或“浅绿色”）以及其他基金（第6条）。使用双重差分设计，我们发现SFDR对基金资金流或投资组合可持续性几乎没有影响。这些披露之所以无效，部分原因在于它们提供的新信息或清晰信息很少，投资者早已能从基金名称和授权中推断出来。在一个实验环境中，我们表明当前的披露对投资者决策影响极小，但使信息更直观可以提高监管的有效性。

No. 164论文详情NBER w34623

Principled Identification of Structural Dynamic Models

结构动态模型的原则性识别

Neville Francis, Peter Reinhard Hansen, Chen Tong

Abstract

We take a new perspective on identification in structural dynamic models: rather than imposing restrictions alone, we optimize an objective. While definitive structural identification ultimately requires exogenous economic insight, a weighted correlation-maximizing objective yields an Order- and Scale-Invariant Scheme (OASIS) that selects the orthogonal rotation most aligned with designated target variables. In traditional SVARs, these targets are the reduced-form innovations, making OASIS a natural reference rotation. We show that recursive Cholesky identification is a constrained version of the same objective and that OASIS is systematically closer to perfect correlation, closing roughly twice as much of the gap as recursive orderings, both theoretically and empirically. The same framework also provides a principled estimation strategy for Proxy VARs (IV-SVARs), where the weighted criterion is essential for resolving overdetermination in multi-proxy systems while symmetrically accommodating proxy leakage. Revisiting 22 published SVARs, we find that reduced-form innovations are typically only weakly correlated, helping explain the historical robustness of recursive schemes. Applying OASIS to seminal proxy applications, however, reveals economically important leakage across shocks and shows that accounting for such leakage can materially alter substantive conclusions.

中文摘要

我们对结构动态模型中的识别问题采取了一个新视角：不是仅仅施加约束，而是优化一个目标函数。虽然确定性的结构识别最终需要外生的经济洞察，但一个加权相关性最大化的目标函数产生了一个“顺序与尺度不变方案”（OASIS），该方案选择与指定目标变量最对齐的正交旋转。在传统的SVAR中，这些目标是简化式创新，这使得OASIS成为一个自然的参考旋转。我们表明，递归的Cholesky识别是同一目标函数的一个受约束版本，并且OASIS在理论上和实证上都系统地更接近完美相关性，其缩小差距的程度大约是递归排序的两倍。同一框架也为代理变量VAR（IV-SVAR）提供了一种原则性的估计策略，其中加权准则对于解决多代理系统中的过度确定问题至关重要，同时对称地处理代理泄漏。重新审视22个已发表的SVAR，我们发现简化式创新通常仅弱相关，这有助于解释递归方案的历史稳健性。然而，将OASIS应用于开创性的代理变量应用，揭示了跨冲击的经济上重要的泄漏，并表明考虑这种泄漏可能会实质性地改变实质性结论。

No. 165论文详情NBER w34622

What Drives Corporate Savings

什么驱动了公司储蓄

Nan Chen, Xavier Giroud, Ling Qin, Neng Wang

Abstract

We study the determinants of corporate cash holdings by extending the standard q theory of investment with financing frictions and productivity shocks. While existing models predict a low propensity to hold cash, we show that realistic cash holdings arise only when three ingredients are combined: 1.) costly external financing, 2.) persistent productivity shocks, and 3.) contemporaneous productivity shocks. With costly external financing, persistent productivity shocks generate predictable cash flows and investment opportunities, but yield little need for savings since the internally generated cash flows are aligned with the investment needs. Contemporaneous shocks make internally generated cash flows random, inducing firms to hold cash at levels consistent with those observed empirically.

中文摘要

我们通过将融资摩擦和生产率冲击纳入标准的投资q理论，研究了公司现金持有的决定因素。虽然现有模型预测持有现金的倾向较低，但我们表明，只有当三个要素结合起来时，才会出现现实的现金持有水平：1.) 昂贵的外部融资，2.) 持久的生产率冲击，以及3.) 同期生产率冲击。在存在昂贵外部融资的情况下，持久的生产率冲击会产生可预测的现金流和投资机会，但由于内部产生的现金流与投资需求相一致，因此几乎没有储蓄的必要。同期冲击使内部产生的现金流变得随机，从而诱使公司持有与实证观察到的水平一致的现金。

No. 166论文详情NBER w34621

Household Finance in Retrospect and Prospect

家庭金融：回顾与展望

John Y. Campbell, Tarun Ramadorai

Abstract

Household finance research has come of age during the early 21st Century by exploiting computational advances for solving complex optimization problems, the availability of large administrative datasets, the development of microeconometrics for causal inference, and new paradigms in behavioral economics. We discuss the distinctive concerns of household finance in relation to other fields of financial economics, and we outline directions for the future growth of the field.

中文摘要

家庭金融研究在21世纪初已趋成熟，其发展得益于解决复杂优化问题的计算进步、大型行政数据的可得性、用于因果推断的微观计量经济学发展以及行为经济学的新范式。我们讨论了家庭金融相对于金融经济学其他领域的独特关注点，并概述了该领域未来发展的方向。

No. 167论文详情NBER w34620

The Incidence of Tariffs: Rates and Reality

关税的归宿：税率与现实

Gita Gopinath, Brent Neiman

Abstract

In 2025, statutory tariff rates on U.S. imports rose to levels not seen in over one hundred years. What are the implications for prices? On the one hand, shipping lags, exemptions, and enforcement gaps have kept the actual implemented rates at only half of the statutory rates, moderating the tariffs’ impact. On the other hand, tariff pass-through to U.S. import prices is almost 100 percent, so the United States is bearing a large share of the costs. We study the incidence of the 2018-2019 and 2025 U.S. tariffs and discuss implications for U.S. sourcing, domestic manufacturing costs, and the dollar.

中文摘要

2025年，美国进口商品的法定关税率升至一百多年来未见的水平。这对价格有何影响？一方面，运输延迟、豁免条款和执行漏洞使得实际执行税率仅为法定税率的一半，从而缓和了关税的影响。另一方面，关税向美国进口价格的传导率几乎为100%，因此美国承担了成本的很大一部分。我们研究了2018-2019年和2025年美国关税的归宿，并讨论了对美国采购、国内制造成本和美元的影响。

No. 168论文详情NBER w34619

Theoretical Approaches in Stratification Economics

分层经济学的理论方法

Brendan Brundage, Dan J. McGee, Daniele Tavani

Abstract

We review new developments in formal theory as applied to racial stratification. Across this literature, we discuss how discrimination produces benefits for advantaged groups at a cost to marginalized groups, how groups resolve conflicts between individual and collective interests, how direct discrimination is transformed into persistent inequality, and the implications of these forces for racial disparities, efficiency, and social welfare. For researchers active in Stratification Economics, we highlight parallels between intuitions about dimensions of racial discrimination and inequality developed by SE and insights from formal models by theorists outside SE. For formal theorists interested in working on questions of race and inequality, we provide an overview of how SE conceptualizes racial stratification and identify open questions where formal theory can provide more rigorous micro-foundations to these intuitions.

中文摘要

我们回顾了应用于种族分层的正式理论的新发展。在这类文献中，我们讨论了歧视如何为优势群体带来利益，同时以边缘化群体为代价；群体如何解决个人利益与集体利益之间的冲突；直接歧视如何转化为持续的不平等；以及这些力量对种族差异、效率和社会福利的影响。对于活跃在分层经济学领域的研究者，我们强调了由分层经济学发展出的关于种族歧视和不平等维度的直觉，与分层经济学外理论家从正式模型中得出的见解之间的相似之处。对于有兴趣研究种族和不平等问题的正式理论家，我们概述了分层经济学如何概念化种族分层，并指出了那些正式理论可以为这些直觉提供更严谨微观基础的开放性问题。

No. 169论文详情NBER w34618

Bank Opacity and Deposit Rates

银行不透明性与存款利率

Ana Babus, Maryam Farboodi, Gabriela Stockler

Abstract

Banks face a dual mandate of raising cheap deposits while avoiding liquidity risk. We propose a novel mechanism whereby banks use portfolio opacity to meet this objective. Specifically, banks choose opaque portfolios to secure cheap long-term funding while trading off insolvency and illiquidity. We show that while opacity lowers deposit rates, it also leaves depositors with only noisy information about the bank’s solvency, making them cautious about keeping their funds in the bank—particularly when interest rates are high. We show that opacity raises bank profits, sometimes at the cost of exposure to high probability of illiquidity. In particular, in high-rate environments, banks adopt excessive opacity to further reduce deposit rates—at the cost of more frequent early failures.

中文摘要

银行面临着筹集廉价存款同时避免流动性风险的双重任务。我们提出了一种新的机制，即银行利用投资组合的不透明性来实现这一目标。具体来说，银行选择不透明的投资组合来确保廉价的长期融资，同时权衡破产风险和流动性不足风险。我们表明，虽然不透明性降低了存款利率，但它也让存款人只能获得关于银行偿付能力的噪音信息，使他们对将资金留在银行持谨慎态度——尤其是在利率较高时。我们表明，不透明性提高了银行利润，有时是以面临高概率流动性不足为代价的。特别是在高利率环境下，银行会采用过度的不透明性来进一步降低存款利率——代价是更频繁的早期失败。

No. 170论文详情NBER w34617

The Growth of Private Lending and Retail Access to Alternative Investments

私人借贷的增长与零售投资者对另类投资的可及性

David T. Robinson, Melanie Wallskog

Abstract

Private lending has exploded recently, owing not only to the retreat of banks from corporate lending, but also to the expansion of private equity (PE). Given the growing interest in retail access to alternative assets, we explore fees, performance, and investment behavior for publicly traded Business Development Companies (BDCs). Their compensation structures include fees and provisions common in PE, and they collectively provide debt for PE-sponsored deals and make PE-like investments themselves, especially for higher-spread investments. In-sample risk-adjusted abnormal returns are high, but fees and performance are inversely related. Moreover, BDCs with larger non-institutional investor bases charge higher fees.

中文摘要

私人借贷近年来急剧增长，这不仅是由于银行从企业贷款中撤退，也归因于私募股权（PE）的扩张。鉴于零售投资者对另类资产日益增长的兴趣，我们探讨了公开上市的商业发展公司（BDCs）的费用、业绩和投资行为。它们的薪酬结构包括私募股权中常见的费用和条款，它们共同为私募股权支持的交易提供债务，并自行进行类似私募股权的投资，尤其是针对利差较高的投资。样本内的风险调整后异常回报率很高，但费用与业绩呈负相关。此外，拥有更大非机构投资者基础的商业发展公司收取更高的费用。

No. 171论文详情NBER w34616

Intergenerational Welfare Assessments

代际福利评估

Sergi Barcons, Eduardo Dávila, Andreas Schaab

Abstract

This paper studies welfare assessments in economies with rich demographics. We introduce the notion of demographically disconnected economies, those with no date at which all individuals are concurrently alive. We identify the unique class of units that always enables meaningful welfare comparisons in such economies: those based on perpetual consumption, that is, consumption at all dates. Using these units, we uncover a novel possibility: feasible perturbations of Pareto efficient allocations can yield Kaldor-Hicks efficiency gains. We also introduce a decomposition that attributes intertemporal-sharing efficiency gains to financial frictions or demographic differences. These results allow us to derive new insights in three workhorse intergenerational models: (i) Samuelson (1958) two-date-life model, offering a novel rationale for social security; (ii) Diamond (1965) growth model, providing a new theory for capital taxation and capital over-/under-accumulation; and (iii) Samuelson (1958) three-date-life model, decomposing the efficiency gains from intergenerational transfers into frictional and demographic sources.

中文摘要

本文研究了具有丰富人口结构的经济体中的福利评估。我们引入了人口不连通经济体的概念，即不存在所有个体同时存活的日期的经济体。我们识别出唯一一类始终能在此类经济体中实现有意义的福利比较的单位：基于永久消费的单位，即所有日期的消费。使用这些单位，我们揭示了一种新的可能性：帕累托有效配置的可行扰动可以产生卡尔多-希克斯效率收益。我们还引入了一种分解方法，将跨期共享效率收益归因于金融摩擦或人口差异。这些结果使我们能够在三个经典的代际模型中获得新的见解：(i) 萨缪尔森（1958）两期生命模型，为社会安全提供了新的理论基础；(ii) 戴蒙德（1965）增长模型，为资本税和资本过度/不足积累提供了新理论；(iii) 萨缪尔森（1958）三期生命模型，将代际转移的效率收益分解为摩擦来源和人口来源。

No. 172论文详情NBER w34615

Expanding the Landscape of Cross-Border Flow Restrictions: Modern Tools and Historical Perspectives

拓展跨境流动限制的图景：现代工具与历史视角

Katharina Bergant, Andrés Fernández, Ken Teoh, Martín Uribe

Abstract

Employing large language models to analyze official documents, we construct a comprehensive record of daily changes in de jure restrictions on cross-border flows worldwide since the 1950s. Our analysis uncovers the wide array of instruments used to regulate cross-border financial flows and documents their evolving prevalence over the past seven decades. The fine granularity of the new measures allows us to characterize cross-country and time-series variation across eight categories of restrictions, further distinguishing by flow, direction, instrument type, and overall policy stance. We exploit the high frequency nature of the new data to document novel patterns in the use of these restrictions, as well as their relationship to crises, and political economy determinants. We validate our measures against established indicators of capital account regulation and show that our LLM-based classifications both replicate and substantially extend these benchmarks along multiple dimensions. Finally, we examine policymakers’ stated motivations for adopting these restrictions and account for the intensive margin of these policy actions.

中文摘要

利用大型语言模型分析官方文件，我们构建了自20世纪50年代以来全球跨境流动法律限制每日变化的全面记录。我们的分析揭示了用于监管跨境金融流动的广泛工具，并记录了它们在过去七十年中流行程度的变化。新措施的高精细度使我们能够描述八类限制的跨国和时间序列变化，进一步按流动类型、方向、工具类型和总体政策立场进行区分。我们利用新数据的高频特性，记录了这些限制使用的新模式，以及它们与危机和政治经济决定因素的关系。我们根据既定的资本账户监管指标验证了我们的度量，并表明我们基于LLM的分类既复制了这些基准，又在多个维度上显著扩展了它们。最后，我们考察了政策制定者采用这些限制的公开动机，并解释了这些政策行动的集约边际。

No. 173论文详情NBER w34614

Broadband Internet Access and Adolescent Mental Health in the U.S.

宽带互联网接入与美国青少年心理健康

Brandyn F. Churchill, Kathryn R. Johnson

Abstract

Broadband internet has become a critical component of U.S. infrastructure, but policymakers are increasingly concerned that the widespread adoption of this technology has adversely affected adolescent mental health. To test this hypothesis, we use 2009–2019 National and State Youth Risk Behavior Survey data and leverage the nationwide rollout of broadband internet. First, we show that adolescents in states with greater broadband internet access reported spending more time online. Next, we find that a one-standard-deviation increase in broadband internet access was associated with a 9.3–16.5-percent increase in adolescent suicide ideation. While we document increases in suicide ideation for both girls and boys, the results are most pronounced for adolescent girls. Exploring potential mechanisms, we show that greater broadband internet access was associated with increases in cyberbullying and body dissatisfaction among adolescent girls and a reduction in the likelihood that adolescent boys reported getting an adequate amount of sleep.

中文摘要

宽带互联网已成为美国基础设施的关键组成部分，但政策制定者越来越担心这项技术的广泛采用对青少年心理健康产生了不利影响。为了检验这一假设，我们使用了2009-2019年全国和州青少年风险行为调查数据，并利用了全国范围内宽带互联网的推广。首先，我们表明，宽带互联网接入程度更高的州的青少年报告花更多时间上网。接下来，我们发现，宽带互联网接入每增加一个标准差，青少年自杀意念增加9.3%至16.5%。虽然我们记录了女孩和男孩自杀意念的增加，但结果在青春期女孩中最为显著。在探索潜在机制时，我们表明，更大的宽带互联网接入与青春期女孩中网络欺凌和身体不满意的增加有关，并与青春期男孩报告获得充足睡眠的可能性降低有关。

No. 174论文详情NBER w34610

Quality Upgrading in Global Supply Chains: Evidence from Colombian Coffee

全球供应链中的质量升级：来自哥伦比亚咖啡的证据

Rocco Macchiavello, Josepa Miquel-Florensa, Nicolas de Roux, Eric Verhoogen, Mario Bernasconi, Patrick W. Farrell

Abstract

Do the returns to quality upgrading pass through supply chains to primary producers? We explore this question in the context of Colombia’s coffee sector, in which market outcomes depend on interactions between farmers, exporters (which operate mills), and international buyers, and contracts are for the most part not legally enforceable. We formalize the hypothesis that quality upgrading is subject to a key hold-up problem: producing high-quality beans requires long-term investments by farmers, but there is no guarantee that an exporter will pay a quality premium when the beans arrive at its mills. An international buyer with sufficient demand for high-quality coffee can solve this problem by imposing a vertical restraint on the exporter, requiring the exporter to pay a quality premium to farmers. Combining internal records from two exporters, comprehensive administrative data, and the staggered rollout of a buyer-driven quality-upgrading program, we find empirical support for the key theoretical predictions, both the lack of pass-through of quality premia under normal circumstances and the possibility of a buyer-driven solution through a vertical restraint. Calibration of the model suggests that one-third to two-thirds of the (substantial) gains from the program accrue to farmers, with the vertical restraint playing a critical role. The results are consistent with the hypotheses that quality upgrading can provide a path to higher incomes for farmers, but also that it is unlikely to be viable under standard market conditions in the sector.

中文摘要

质量升级的回报是否会通过供应链传导给初级生产者？我们在哥伦比亚咖啡行业的背景下探讨这个问题，该行业的市场结果取决于农民、出口商（经营加工厂）和国际买家之间的互动，且合同大多不具有法律强制执行力。我们形式化了这样一个假设：质量升级面临一个关键的套牢问题：生产高品质咖啡豆需要农民进行长期投资，但无法保证当咖啡豆到达出口商的加工厂时，出口商会支付质量溢价。一个对高品质咖啡有足够需求的国际买家可以通过对出口商施加纵向约束来解决这个问题，要求出口商向农民支付质量溢价。结合两家出口商的内部记录、全面的行政数据以及一个由买家推动的质量升级项目的分阶段推广，我们找到了支持关键理论预测的经验证据，既包括正常情况下质量溢价缺乏传导，也包括通过纵向约束实现买家驱动解决方案的可能性。模型校准表明，该项目（可观的）收益中有三分之一到三分之二归农民所有，其中纵向约束发挥了关键作用。这些结果与以下假设一致：质量升级可以为农民提供一条通往更高收入的道路，但也表明在该行业的标准市场条件下，质量升级不太可能可行。

No. 175论文详情NBER w34609

Extreme Temperatures Promote High-Fat Diets

极端温度促进高脂肪饮食

Xi Chen, Shuo Li, Ding Ma, Jintao Xu

Abstract

Extreme temperatures threaten agriculture and exacerbate global food insecurity, yet their direct impact on dietary choices remains poorly understood. We provide novel evidence of how short-term exposures to extreme temperatures affect macronutrient intake in China. We show that both hot and cold weather elevate high-fat diet risks. In particular, hot weather reduces carbohydrate and protein consumption but not fat intake, while cold weather increases all nutrient intake, particularly fats. Temperature-induced dietary changes are shaped primarily by physiological responses to thermal stress, whereas physical activities demonstrate little effect. Technologies that improve indoor thermal comfort (via fans, air conditioners, and heating systems) substantially mitigate high-fat diet risks. Socioeconomic disparities are evident, with rural and poor individuals more likely to adopt high-fat diets under hot or cold weather. Projections indicate that more extreme temperatures due to climate change may increase the prevalence of high-fat diets nationally, while substantial regional heterogeneity emerges, with declines in northeast China and increases in southern China. These results highlight a crucial but overlooked pathway linking climate change to dietary health inequality.

中文摘要

极端温度威胁农业并加剧全球粮食不安全，然而它们对饮食选择的直接影响仍知之甚少。我们提供了关于短期暴露于极端温度如何影响中国宏量营养素摄入的新证据。我们表明，炎热和寒冷的天气都会增加高脂肪饮食的风险。特别是，炎热天气减少了碳水化合物和蛋白质的摄入，但不减少脂肪摄入，而寒冷天气增加了所有营养素的摄入，尤其是脂肪。温度引起的饮食变化主要由对热应激的生理反应决定，而身体活动的影响很小。改善室内热舒适度的技术（通过风扇、空调和供暖系统）显著减轻了高脂肪饮食的风险。社会经济差异很明显，农村和贫困人口在炎热或寒冷天气下更可能采用高脂肪饮食。预测表明，气候变化导致的更极端温度可能会在全国范围内增加高脂肪饮食的流行率，同时出现显著的地区异质性，东北地区下降，华南地区上升。这些结果突出了一个关键但被忽视的将气候变化与饮食健康不平等联系起来的途径。

No. 176论文详情NBER w34588

Topography of the FX Derivatives Market: A View from London

外汇衍生品市场的地形：来自伦敦的视角

Sinem Hacioglu Hoke, Daniel A. Ostry, Hélène Rey, Adrien Rousset Planat, Vania Stavrakeva, Jenny Tang

Abstract

Drawing on 100 million transactions, we show how speculators, hedgers, and market makers interact in the world’s largest FX derivatives market, and that derivatives trading can affect exchange rates. Firms in the largest client sectors—pension and investment funds, insurers, and nonfinancials—use FX derivatives primarily to hedge currency risk, with dealer banks providing the liquidity. Hedge funds, with comparatively smaller net exposures, trade speculatively, whereas dealer banks insulate themselves from changes in speculative demand by taking offsetting positions with hedgers, especially nonfinancials. Non-bank market makers, instead, take residual exchange-rate exposures “on the margin”. Hedge funds’ speculative flows help transmit monetary policy shocks to exchange rates, while investment funds' unwinding of hedges contribute to dollar appreciations when credit risk rises. Our results highlight that exchange rates depend on the composition of trading activities in FX derivatives markets.

中文摘要

利用1亿笔交易，我们展示了投机者、对冲者和做市商如何在世界上最大的外汇衍生品市场中互动，以及衍生品交易如何影响汇率。最大的客户部门——养老基金和投资基金、保险公司和非金融企业——主要使用外汇衍生品来对冲货币风险，而交易商银行提供流动性。对冲基金的净敞口相对较小，进行投机性交易，而交易商银行通过与非金融企业等对冲者建立抵消头寸，使自己免受投机需求变化的影响。相反，非银行做市商“在边际上”承担剩余的外汇风险敞口。对冲基金的投机性流动有助于将货币政策冲击传导至汇率，而投资基金解除对冲则会在信用风险上升时导致美元升值。我们的结果强调，汇率取决于外汇衍生品市场交易活动的构成。
